atha nāyakaprakaraṇam । vidyākairavakaumudīṃ śrutiśiraḥ sīmantamuktāmaṇiṃ dārān padmabhuvastrilokajananīṃ vande girāṃ devatām । yatpādābjanamaskriyāḥ sukṛtināṃ sārasvataprakriyābījanyāsabhuvo bhavanti kavitānāṭyaikajīvātavaḥ ।। pūrvebhyo bhāmahādibhyaḥ sādaraṃ vihatāñjaliḥ ।
vakṣye samyagalaṅkāraśāstrasarvasvasaṃgraham ।। cireṇa caritārtho abhūt kāvyālaṅkārasaṃgrahaḥ । pratāparudradevasya kīrtiryena prakāśyate ।। rasapradhānāḥ śabdārthā guṇālaṅkāravṛttayaḥ ।
rītayaśceyatī śāstraprameyaṃ kāvyapaddhatiḥ ।। yadyapyasau prabandheṣu prācāṃ sādhu nirūpitā । tathāpyasyāḥ samaṃ neturnodāharaṇamādṛtam ।। puṇyaślokasya caritamudāharaṇamarhati ।
na kaścit tādṛśaḥ pūrvaiḥ prabandhābharaṇīkṛtaḥ ।। prabandhānāṃ prabandhṝṇāmapi kīrttipratiṣṭhayoḥ । mūlaṃ viṣayabhūtasya neturguṇanirūpaṇam ।। yathā rāmaguṇavarṇanaṃ rāmāyaṇavalmīkajanmanormahāpratiṣṭhākaraṇaṃ, tathā mahāpuruṣavarṇanena hi śreyaskarī prabandhasthitiḥ ।
yathā vedaśāstrapurāṇāderhitaprāptiḥ ahitanivṛttiśca, tathā sadāśrayāt kāvyādapi । iyān viśeṣaḥkāvyāt kartavyatādhīḥ sarasā, anyatra na tathā । yadvedāt prabhusaṃmitādadhigataṃ śabdapradhānācciraṃ yaccārthapravaṇāt purāṇavacanādiṣṭaṃ suhṛtsaṃmitāt । kāntāsaṃmitayā yayā sarasatāmāpādya kāvyaśriyā kartavye kutukī budho viracitastasyai spṛhāṃ kurmahe ।।
tataḥ kāvyaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalajanakatayā bahūpayuktam । "kāvyaṃ yaśase arthakṛte vyavahāravide śivetarakṣataye । sadyaḥ paranirvṛtaye kāntāsaṃmitatayopadeśayuje" ।। iti ।
"parivaḍḍhai viṇṇāṇaṃ saṃbhāvijjai jaso viḍappaṃdi guṇā । sutrai supurusacariaṃ kiṃ tajjeṇa ṇa haraṃti kavvāṭhṭhāvā" ।। (parivardhate vijñānaṃ saṃbhāvyate yaśo arjyante guṇāḥ । śrūyate supuruṣacaritaṃ kiṃ tad yena na haranti kāvyālāpāḥ) ।।
yatra punaruttamapuraṣacaritaṃ na nibadhyate, tat kāvyaṃ parityājyameva । smṛtiḥ"kāvyālāpāṃśca varjayet'; iti । na kevalaṃ kāvyasyāyaṃ panthāḥ । kintu śāstarajātasyāpi sadāśrayatvena mahān lokādaraḥ ।
tathā vaiśeṣikāderīśvarapratiṣṭhāpakatayā jagatpūjyatā । tathā mahābhāratādīnāmapi mahāpuruṣavarṇanaparatayaiva viśvātiśāyitvam । kiṃ bahunā? vedāntā api brahmapratipādakatayā paramutkṛṣyante । aathāto dharmajijñāsā'; ityupakramamāṇena sūtrakṛtā maharṣiṇāpi puruṣāśritasya guṇaśreṣṭhasya dharmasya jijñāsādvāreṇa mahāpuruṣaguṇavarṇanameva śāstrasya prāṇa ityurarīkṛtam ।
tattannyāyanirūpaṇaparasyāpi prabandharāśermahāpuruṣaguṇavarṇanaṃ hemnaḥ paramāmodaḥ । pratāparudradevasya guṇānāśritya nirmitaḥ । alaṅkāraprabandho ayaṃ santaḥ karṇotsavo astu vaḥ ।। kākatīyanarendrasya yaśo bhūṣayituṃ kṛtā ।
vidyānāthakṛtiśceyaṃ svayaṃ tena vibhūṣyate ।। "ādirājayaśobimbamādarśaṃ prāpya vāṅmayam । teṣāmasaṃnidhāne api na svayaṃ paśya naśyati" ।। iti ।
sūktaiva pratipādyamahimnā prabandhamahattā । "upaślokyasya māhātmyādujjvalāḥ kāvyasaṃpadaḥ" । iti । "guṇālaṅkāracārutvayuktamapyadhikojjvalam ।
kāvyamāśrayasaṃpattyā meruṇevāmaradrumaḥ" ।। iti । rudrabhaṭṭenāpi kathitam"udāracaritanibandhanā prabandhapratiṣṭhā'; iti । prapañcitaṃ ca sāhityamīmāṃsāyām"nāyakaguṇagrathitāḥ sūktisrajaḥ sukṛtināmākalpamākalpanti'; iti ।
"kaveralpāpi vāgvṛttirvidvatkarṇāvataṃsati । nāyako yadi varṇyeta lokottaraguṇottaraḥ" ।। iti । ।। mahākulīnatvādināyakaguṇāḥ ।।
atraite nāyakaguṇāḥ । mahākulīnataujjvalyaṃ mahābhāgyamudāratā । tejasvitā vidagdhatvaṃ dhārmikatvādayo guṇāḥ ।। pūrvaśāstrānusāreṇa katicit kathitā ime ।
pratāparudradevasya guṇā vācāmagocarāḥ ।। athaiteṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । mahākulīnatā nāma kule mahati saṃbhavaḥ । tādṛṅmadhyamalokabhāgyavibhavādindrādibṛndārakaiḥ kṣoṇyāṃ krīḍitumicchubhiścirataraṃ saṃprārthitaḥ padmabhūḥ ।
atyarkendukulapraśastimasṛjad yaṃ kākatīyānvayaṃ tasmin saṃprati vīrarudravapuṣā jāgarti lakṣmīpatiḥ ।। rūpasaṃpannadehatvamaujjvalyaṃ parikīrtyate ।। murāreryaḥ pūrvaṃ jalanidhisutāyāmudabhavanmahādevājjātaḥ sa punaravanībhṛdduhitari । vapuṣmān kāmo ayaṃ jayati jagatībhāgyavibhavaiḥ pratāpaśrīrudraḥ svayamiti manīṣā mṛgādṛśām ।।
viśvaṃbharādhipatyaṃ yat tanmahābhāgyamucyate । sevānamranarendramaulivilasadratnaṃśunīrājitaṃ rājyaśrīprathamāvatārapadavīmāruhya siṃhāsanam । kṣoṇīṃ rakṣati vikramairanupamaiḥ pratyarthipṛthvīpatiślāghālaṅghanajāṅghikairguṇanidhiḥ śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। yad viśrāṇanatācchīlyamaudāryaṃ tannigadyate ।।
vadānyo nānyo asti trijagati samo rudranṛpaterguṇaśreṇīślāghāpihitaharidīśānayaśasaḥ । samantādudbhūtairdviradamadagandhaiḥ surabhayaḥ kriyante yadvidvajjanamaṇigṛhaprāṅgaṇabhuvaḥ ।। jagatprakāśakatvaṃ yat tejasvitvaṃ taducyate । sadā tejobhānau sphurati jayinaḥ kākativibhorarikṣmābhṛtkāntācikuratimirāhaṃkṛtimuṣi ।
prakāśavyutpattirbhavati jaraduddāmatamasāmasūryaṃpaśyānāmavadhigiripāścāttyadṛṣadām ।। kṛtyavastuṣu cāturyaṃ vaidagdhyaṃ parikīrtyate ।। cāturyaṃ kimu varṇyate guṇanidheḥ śrīvīrarudraprabhoryatrānyonyaviruddhayorapi mahadvāṇīśriyorārjavam । kiṃ cābhyāṃ sadṛśopacāralalitāṃ tattādṛśairutsavairniḥ sāpatnyamimāṃ bhuvaṃ sa nṛpatirdhatte diśāṃ jitvaraḥ ।।
dharmaikāyattacittatvaṃ dhārmikatvamudīryate । parihāse apyanaucityaṃ svapne apyanyavadhūkathām । śatrāvapyaguṇāropaṃ kākatīndro na mṛṣyati ।। ādigrahaṇānmahāmahimatvapāṇḍityaprabhṛtayaḥ ।
tanmahāmahimatvaṃ syād yā punardevatātmatā ।। kausalyā'sīt prathamajananī, devakī ca dvitīyā viṣṇormātā tadanu mahitā mummaḍāmbā tṛtīyā । yastretāyāṃ raghupatirabhūd dvāpare śaurirāsīt trātuṃ kṣoṇīṃ sa jayati kalau vīrarudrāvatāraḥ ।। atra garuḍadhvajātmakatayā mahāmahimatoktā ।
sarvavidyādhikatvaṃ yat pāṇḍityaṃ tadudāhṛtam । goṣṭhībhiḥ paritoṣayan budhagaṇān ṣaḍdarśanīsīmabhiḥ satsārasvatamārgadarśanacaṇaiḥ sūktaiḥ kavīn prīṇayan । saṃgītopaniṣadrahasyapiśunairātodyayogyakramairdhinvan saṃsadi vaiṇikān viharate śrīkākatīndro nṛpaḥ ।। atha nāyakaguṇanirūpaṇānantaraṃ nāyakasvarūpaṃ nirūpyate ।
yaśaḥ pratāpasubhago dharmakāmārthatatparaḥ । dhuraṃdharo guṇāḍhyaśca nāyakaḥ parikīrttitaḥ ।। dharmālambasamucchritāṃ tribhuvanasyaikātapatraśriyaṃ dhatte kākativīrarudranṛpateḥ sphāraṃ yaśomaṇḍalam । chāyevāsya nabhaḥ sthalī kuvalayaśyāmeyamālokyate tanmanye niyataṃ pratāpatapanastasyopari dyotate ।।
dharmo artha iva pūrṇaśrīrartho dharma iva sthitaḥ । kāmastāviva tau kāma iva rudranareśvare ।। gāyantīranumodate nijavadhūḥ śeṣaḥ śiraḥ kampanairlakṣmīṃ prīṇayate adya kacchapapatirvakṣaḥ sthalīdarśanāt । diṅnāgāśca kareṇukāśucamapākurvantyanuvrajyayā doṣṇā kākativīrarudranṛpatau viśvambharāṃ bibhrati ।।
mukhaiḥ sahastreṇa phaṇī vadeccet karaiḥ sahasreṇa likhedvivasvān । netraiḥ sahasreṇa hariśca paśyet sthāne guṇān kākativīrabhurtuḥ ।। atha nāyakaviśeṣā nirūpyante । udātta uddhataścaiva lalitaḥ śānta ityapi ।
dhīrapūrvā ime pūrvaiścatvāro nāyakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tatra sarvarasasādhāraṇāścatvāro nāyakāḥ dhīrodāttadhīroddhatadhīralalitadhīraśāntāḥ । eteṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । mahāsattvo atigambhīraḥ kṛpāvānavikatthanaḥ ।
pratāparudravada dhīro dhīrodāttaḥ sa saṃmataḥ ।। saṃdigdhe kṛpayā mṛduḥ kṣaṇamarīn hantuṃ dhṛtāsiḥ puraḥ śauryaśrīpraṇayapraśaṃsiṣu namadbhrūrlajjate vandiṣu । ākārān sukharoṣaharṣapiśunān vaktre na dhatte manāk trailokyātiśayālukīrttisubhagaḥ śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। darpamātsaryabhūyiṣṭhaścaṇḍavṛttirvikatthanaḥ ।
māyāvī sulabhakrodhaḥ sa dhīroddhata ucyate ।। re re ghūrjara jarjharo asi samare lampāka kiṃ kampase vaṅga tvaṅgasi kiṃ mudhā balarajaḥ kāṇo asi kiṃ koṅkaṇa । hūṇa prāṇaparāyaṇo bhava mahārāṣṭrāparāṣṭro asyamī yoddhāro vayamityarīnabhibhavantyandhrakṣamābhṛdbhaṭāḥ ।। atra bhaṭānāṃ dhīroddhatatvam ।
asuravaikabhūḥ'; iti pāṭhāntaram । niścinto dhīralalitaḥ kalāsaktaḥ । sukhī mṛduḥ । i ।
śauryoṣmā niravagrahaḥ pratinṛpāḥ sarve api namrīkṛtāḥ pātivratyamupaiti bhūriyamayaṃ nāthaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śivaḥ । dhīro ayaṃ yuvarāja eva vahati śrīvīrarudro dhuraṃ sarvāmityanumodate pratikalaṃ śrīkākatīndro nṛpaḥ ।। dhīraḥ śāntaḥ prasannātmā dhīraśānto dvijādikaḥ ।। vīraṃ rudranṛpālaratnamabhitaḥ prāptodayaṃ modate saṃkhyāvadaraṇa eṣa pūṣaṇamiva pratyagramabjākaraḥ ।
unmīlatkamalāvihāravasatirbhūtvā vikāsairnijairviśvāmodamudañcayannavirataṃ doṣāvasānotsukaḥ ।। atra viprāṇāṃ dhīraśāntatvam । ।। śṛṅgāranāyakā nirūpyante । atha śṛṅgāraviṣayāścatvāro nāyakā ime ।
anukūlo dakṣiṇaśca dhṛṣṭaḥ śaṭha iti smṛtāḥ ।। eṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । ekasyāṃ nāyikāyāṃ viśeṣānurakto anukūlo nāyakaḥ । kiṃ nāmācaritaṃ tapaḥ sakhi ! bhuvā yasyāḥ patirgīyate vīro rudranṛpaḥ kva tat sucaritaṃ tasya priyā syāṃ yataḥ ।
jāne mānini mā viṣīda purataḥ prakhyāpya nāma sthirāṃ tvāṃ ratnākaramekhalāṃ tvayi sadā saktaṃ vidhāsye nṛpam ।। atra pratāparudrasya kṣoṇyāṃ viśeṣānurāgo vyajyate, yena vadhvā sthirā ratnākaramekhaleti tannāmagrahaṇena snehaprakhyāpanaṃ kriyate । tulyo anekatra dakṣiṇaḥ । anekāsu nāyikāsu avaiṣamyeṇa snehānuvartī dakṣiṇo nāyakaḥ ।
narmoktyaiva niyantritā smarakalākelīṣu kācinmayā sākūtena vilokanena hṛdayaṃ kasyaicidāviṣkṛtam । kasyāścit prahitaḥ prasādhananidhirdūtīkareṇa, kva vā gantāsmītyanucintayaiva nṛpaterāsīt prabhātā niśā ।। vāṇīṃ mukhena, netrābhyāṃ śriyaṃ, doṣṇā ca medinīm । mānayaṃstulyatāṃ dhatte tāsu rudranareśvaraḥ ।।
rājyaśrīparibhogaśaṃsi bhavataḥ sarvāṅgamālokyate kastatrāvinayo asti sāhasamidaṃ tannāma mayyarpitam । jāne tvāṃ bahuvallabhaṃ kimaparaṃ vaktavyamalpā vayaṃ tasyāṃ prema tavādhikaṃ vasumatī yā nāma kiṃ jalpitaiḥ ।। gūḍhavipriyakṛcchaṭhaḥ ।। nāyikāmātraviditavipriyakārī śaṭhaḥ ।
dṛṣṭyā paśyasi kevalaṃ na manasā vācā priyaṃ bhāṣase no bhāvena bhujāntaraṃ prakaṭayasyagre na cābhyantaram । jñātaṃ kākatinātha ! bhūstava paraṃ prāṇeśvarī dhyāyato mādṛkṣeṣu viḍambanaiva; tadalaṃ vyarthairbahissaṃbhramaiḥ ।। atra tattannāyakaviṣayatayā kākatīśvarāṇāmudāharaṇena vīrarudrasyaiva varṇanam । eṣāṃ nāyikānukūlane pīṭhamardaviṭaceṭavidūṣakanāmānaḥ sahāyāḥ ।
teṣāṃ svarūpaṃ nirūpyate । kiṃcidūnaḥ pīṭhamarda ekavidyo viṭaḥ smṛtaḥ । saṃdhānakuśalaśceṭo hāsyaprāyo vidūṣakaḥ ।। spaṣṭameṣāmudāharaṇam ।
athāṣṭavidhāḥ śṛṅgāranāyikāḥ । svādhīnapatikā caiva tathā vāsakasajjikā । virahotkaṇṭhitā caiva vipralabdhā ca khaṇḍitā ।। kalahāntaritā caiva tathā proṣitabhartṛkā ।
tathābhisārikā ceti kramāllakṣaṇamucyate ।। priyopalālitā nityaṃ svādhīnapatikā matā । priyāṃ sarvaṃsahāṃ taistairviśeṣairupalālayan । pratāparudranṛpatiḥ pratikṣaṇamavekṣate ।।
priyāgamanavelāyāṃ maṇḍayantī muhurmuhuḥ । kelīgṛhaṃ tathātmānaṃ sā syādvāsakasajjikā ।। svatejasā pariṣkṛtya pradhānāgāramutkayā । śriyābhiṣekavelāyāṃ vīrarudraḥ pratīkṣitaḥ ।।
cirayatyadhikaṃ kānte virahotkaṇṭhitonmanāḥ ।। na śaṅkānyā tādṛgguṇaparimale rudranṛpatau kayā vā goṣṭhyāsau cirayati sakhībhirna sulabhaḥ । samānetuṃ kāntaṃ vraja madana baddho añjalirayaṃ yato viṣvadrīcaḥ kirati kiraṇāṃstvatpriyasakhaḥ ।। kvacit saṃketamāvedya dayitenātha vañcitā ।
smarārtā vipralabdheti kalāvidbhiḥ prakīrtyate ।। gacchāgre sakhi ! kā priyāgamakathā prāpto niśīthaḥ paraṃ saṃketālaya ! mokṣyase mama vṛthā jāto aśrubhiḥ paṅkilaḥ । yadvā rudranareśvare priyatame rājyaśriyo vallabhe bhāratyā dayite bhuvaḥ kṛtapadāḥ prāyo vayaṃ vañcitāḥ ।। nītvānyatra niśāṃ prātarāgate prāṇavallabhe ।
anyāsaṃbhogacihnaistu kupitā khaṇḍitā matā ।। rātriryāmatrayaparimitā vallabhāste sahasraṃ mārgāsaktyā mama gṛhamapi prātarevāgato asi । kiṃ kartavyaṃ vada nṛpatibhirvīkṣaṇīyā hi sarvāḥ ko vā doṣastava punarahaṃ kāmamāyāsayitrī ।। kopāt priyaṃ parāṇudya paścāttāpasamanvitā ।
kalahāntaritā nāma sūribhiḥ parikīrtitā ।। taha taha aṇuṇaanto pio tue hiaa rosakaluseṇa । avahīrido ṇa muṇiaṃ rāeti vioaveaṇaṃ sahasu ।। (tathā tathā anunayan priyastvayā hṛdaya ! roṣa kaluṣeṇa ।
avadhīrito na jñāto rājeti viyogavedanāṃ sahasva) ।। deśāntaragate kānte khinnā proṣitabhartṛkā । trailokyaprathamānakīrttimahasaḥ śrīvīrarudraprabhoḥ sevārthaṃ cirayatsu kākatipure bhūpeṣu tadyoṣitaḥ । dvārāsaktadṛśo nayanti divasān vyuṣṭāśayā ca kṣapāstaddhyānapratibaddhasāndrapulakavyākīrṇakāmeṣavaḥ ।।
kāntābhisaraṇodyuktā smarārtā sābhisārikā ।। saṃbhramairalamalpajñe ! preyānastu mahīpatiḥ । kareṇusthāṃ na paśyāmi na śṛṇomyabhisārikām ।। ।। āsāṃ nāyikānukūlane sahāyāḥ ।।
dūtyo dāsī sakhī kārūrdhātreyī prātiveśinī । liṅginī śilpinī svā ca sahāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। etāsāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca spaṣṭam । kāmaśāstraprasiddhāḥ padmanīcitriṇīprabhṛtayo jātiviśeṣā jñātavyāḥ ।
saṃkṣepeṇa nāyikā trividhāmugdhā madhyā prauḍhā ceti । udayadyauvanā mugdhā lajāvijitamanmathā । lajāmanmathamadhyasthā madhyamoditayauvanā । smaramandīkṛtavrīḍā prauḍhā saṃpūrṇayauvanā ।।
yathākramamudāharaṇāni । mugdhe ! yanmanaso api gopyamakhilaṃ tanmahyamāvedyate kiṃ yā kācidahaṃ tava priyasakhi pracchādya kiṃ tāmyasi । āsaktistava rudradevanṛpatāvāśāsyate kiṃ bhavedityālyāṃ praṇayaikavāci sutanurdattottarā vrīḍayā ।। līlāvibhramapūrvaraṅgamuditaṃ tāruṇyametya trapānepathyāntarabimbitasmarakalālāsyaprapañcaśriyaḥ ।
sakhyaḥ paśyata kākatīyanṛpatau bhāvānubandhojjvalaḥ ko apyasyāstaralabhruvo vijayate śṛṅgāranāṭyakramaḥ ।। sahelaṃ paśyantyāḥ prakṛtisubhagaṃ rudranṛpatiṃ tadātvapratyudyadvividhalalitāṭopamadhuram । rasaprādurbhāvād yugapadudayatsāttvikamaho mṛgākṣyāstāruṇye kusumaśaraśilpaṃ vijayate ।। bhedāntaraṃ yathāsaṃbhavamudāhāryam ।
guṇālaṃkārāṇāṃ rasamahati kāvye vilasitaṃ sphuracchabdārthābhyāṃ tadapi hṛdayānandi bhavati । tayorapyunmeṣaḥ sravadamṛtamādhuryasubhagaḥ paraṃ puṇyaślokaṃ caritamanubadhnan vijayate ।। eṣa saṃgrahaślokaḥ । upaskārahetūnāṃ guṇālaṅkārāṇāṃ sadṛ'śeṅārye sati caritārthatvam ।
yasyālaṅkārāśrayatvaṃ tadeva lokanyāyenālaṅkāryam । tena guṇālaṅkārāṇāṃ kāvyamevāśrayabhūtamiti tadevālaṅkāryam । rasāderalaṅkāryatvoktiḥ prādhānyenātmana iva hāranūpurādyalaṅkāryatvam । jīvitabhūtatvādrasādeḥ kāvyātmatā ।
kvacidrasasya prādhānyam । kvacidalaṅaakārasya prādhānyam । kvacidvastunaḥ prādhānyaṃ ca । ।
īṣadaṅkuritavibhramacārau dehapallavitakāntini tanvyāḥ । yauvane mukulitastanamātre puṣpitaśca phalitaśca manobhūḥ ।। etat kāñcidbālāmālokya saspṛhasya pratāparudrasya vacanam । atra śṛṅgāraraso vyajyate ।।
kīrttau pratāparudrasya viharantyāṃ digantare । lokālokataṭāḥ śaśvaddravaccandropalāṅkitāḥ ।। atra candrakāntakuṭṭimānāṃ lokālokācalataṭānāṃ rudradevakīrttau candrikābuddhyā śaśvat dravo abhūditi bhrāntimadalaṅāro vyajyate । vyaṅgyāvasthāyāmalaṅkārasyāpi prādhānyamastyeva ।।
avatarati vīrarudre kākativaṃśe trilokamahanīye । tyaktvā dugdhapayodhiṃ talpaphaṇīśaḥ svamandiraṃ prāptaḥ ।। atra talpaphaṇīśaḥ dugdhābdhiṃ vihāya svagṛhaṃ prāptaḥ ityanena kṣīrasamudre harirnāstīti vyajyate । anena puruṣottamaḥ pratāparudrarūpeṇa kākatīyakule avatatāreti vastu vyajyate ।
iti trividhaṃ vyaṅgyaprādhānyam ।। kāvyamāśritya guṇālaṅkārāṇāṃ vilāsaḥ । tacca kāvyaṃ śabdasphuraṇenārthasphuraṇena tadubhayasphuraṇena ca sahṛdayahṛdayānandi bhavati ।। śabdasya sphuraṇaṃ nāma prauḍhabandhasya ḍambaraḥ ।
yo bandhāḍambara ārabhaṭyāṃ pratipādayiṣyate tacchabdasphuraṇam । kṣoṇīrakṣaṇadakṣiṇāḥ kṣatajagatkṣobhā durīkṣakramāḥ kṣudrakṣatriyapakṣaśikṣaṇavidhau protkṣiptakaukṣeyakāḥ । uddāmodyamanasya rudranṛpaterderdaṇḍayoścaṇḍayorgarjaddurjanagarvaparvatabhidādambholayaḥ kelayaḥ ।। acumbitārthasaṃpattirarthasphuraṇamiṣyate ।।
khagge jujjñavijimbhie rivumahīṇāhaṃjaliṃ biṃbiaṃ pekkhaṃto jaalacchivāsakamalaṃ maṇṇaṃti viṇṇāṇiṇo । maṇṇe vīrapaāvaruddavihuṇo jaṇṇesu ghettuṃ uṇo siṭhṭhīe ripujīviāi vihiṇo pattassa pīḍhaṃbuam ।। (khaḍge yuddhavijṛmbhite ripumahīnāthāñjaliṃ bimbitaṃ prekṣamāṇāḥ jayalakṣmīvāsakamalaṃ manyante vijñāninaḥ । manye vīrapratāparudravibhorjanyeṣu grahītuṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭyai ripujīvitāni vidheḥ prāptasya pīṭhāmbujam) ।।
udyadbṛṃhitagarjitaiḥ karighaṭākādambinīḍambaraiḥ kṣoṇībhṛtkaṭakoparodhapaṭubhiḥ sadyaḥ sphura ddiktaṭaiḥ । prāvṛṭasaṃbhramaśaṃsino ripuvadhūbāṣpodgamairdurdinaṃ kurvantaścalamartigaṇḍanṛpaterjaitraprayāṇodyamāḥ ।। evaṃvidhaśabdārthasphuraṇābhyāṃ kāvyasya cārutvam । śabdārthayorapi puṇyaślokacaritavarṇanena sahṛdayahṛdayānanditvam ।
ato nāyakasyaiva kāvye prādhānyam । kulācārayaśaḥ śauryaśrutaśīlādivarṇanam । kriyate neturevaṃ yattadeva bahusaṃmatam ।। athavā pratipakṣasya varṇayitvā guṇān bahūn ।
tajjayānnāyakotkarṣavarṇanaṃ ca mataṃ kvacit ।। tattvaṃ yassa paraḥ pumānavataro yasyānvaye kākatikṣmāpānāṃ caritaṃ ca yasya bhuvanakṣemaṃkaraprakramam । ślaghā yasya laghūkṛtāmaratarusvardhenucintāmaṇiḥ so ayaṃ viśvadhuraṃdharo vijayate śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। yattejaḥ pratipakṣabhūpaviharadgarvāndhakārātapo yaddorargalavikramastrijagatīśuddhāntadauvārikaḥ ।
so apyāsīd yudhi sevaṇakṣitipatiḥ sannāhabherīdhvaniṃ śrutvā rudranareśvarasya mahato bhītaḥ palāyyākulaḥ ।। evaṃvidhavarṇanamutpādye nāyake na ghaṭate । tasya lokaprasiddhyarthaṃ kulavyapadeśādayo bahudhā varṇayitumevocitāḥ । svataḥ siddhe tu nāyake dvaividhyamapi saṃbhavati ।
tasya kulavyapadeśādīnāṃ lokaprasiddhatvāt kavibhirbalavatpratipakṣavijayavarṇanaṃ yuktam । evaṃ svataḥ sidhdotpādyatvabhedena nāyakasya dvaividhyam । dhīroddhate yathā raudro varṇyate bāhyasaṃbhramaḥ । yathā ca dhīralalite śṛṅgāro bahubhāvakṛt ।।
na dhīrodāttaviṣaye tathā varṇanamiṣyate । kāryato rasasaṃpūrtistasminnapyucitakramā ।। hāsyādīnāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ rasānāmapi kīrtanam । mandodyamānubhāvaṃ syāddhīrodātte tu netari ।।
sarvanāyakātiśāyitvāddhīrodāttasya tadviṣayatvaṃ prabandhānāmatiślāghākāraṇam ।। nāyakaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।। iti padavākyapramāṇapārāvārapārīṇaśrīmahopādhyāyakolacalamallināthasūrisūnunā viśvajanīnavidyasya vidvanmaṇeḥ peddayāryasyānujena kumārasvāmisomapīthinā viracite pratāparudrīyavyākhyāne ratnāpaṇākhyāne nāyakanirūpaṇaṃ nāma prathamaṃ prakaraṇam ।। ।। atha kāvyasvarūpanirūpaṇam ।।
guṇālaṃkārasahitau śabdārthau doṣavarjitau । gadyapadyobhayamayaṃ kāvyaṃ kāvyavido viduḥ ।। "adoṣau saguṇau sālaṃkārau śabdārthau kāvyam"iti kāvyasāmānyalakṣaṇam । śabdārthau mūrtirākhyātau jīvitaṃ vyaṅgyavaibhavam ।
hārādivadalaṃkārāstatra syurupamādayaḥ ।। śleṣādayo guṇāstatra śauryādaya iva sthitāḥ । ātmotkarṣāvahāstatra svabhāvā iva rītayaḥ ।। śobhāmāhārthikīṃ prāptā vṛttayo vṛttayo yathā ।
padānuguṇyaviśrāntiḥ śayyā śayyeva saṃmatā ।। rasāsvādaprabhedāḥ syuḥ pākāḥ pākā iva sthitāḥ । prakhyātā lokavadiyaṃ sāmagrī kāvyasaṃpadaḥ ।। vācakalakṣakavyañjakatvena trividhaṃ śabdajātam ।
vācyalakṣyavyaṅgyatvenārthajātamapi trividham । tātparyārtho api vyaṅgyārtha eva, na pṛthagbhūtaḥ । abhidhālakṣaṇāvyañjanākhyāstisraḥ śabdavṛttayaḥ । gauṇavṛttirapi lakṣaṇāprabheda eva, saṃbandhānupapattimūlakatvāt ।
yathāgnirmāṇavaka ityatrāgnisādṛśyaviśiṣṭamāṇavakapratipattirvivakṣitā, tathaiva gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityatra gaṅgāsaṃbandhaviśiṣṭatīrapratipattirvivakṣitā । gaṅgāsaṃbandhasyopalakṣaṇatve ghoṣagatapavitratvādyasiddheḥ । ata eva sādṛśyanibandhanā saṃbandhanibandhanā ceti dvividhā lakṣaṇā । saṃbandhanibandhanā jahadvācyā ajahadvācyā ceti dvividhā ।
sādṛśyanibandhanā sāropā sādhyavasāyā ceti vdividhā । evaṃ lakṣaṇā caturvidhā । kaiśikyārabhaṭī sāttvatī bhāratī ceti racanāśritatvena rasāvasthānaṃsūcakāścatasno vṛttayaḥ । "kaiśikyārabhaṭī caiva sāttvatī bhāratī tathā ।
catasro vṛttayo jñeyā rasāvasthānasūcakāḥ ।। a; iti । racanāyā api rasavyañjakatvaṃ prasiddham । rasānanuguṇavarṇaracanāyā doṣatvamuktam ।
vaidarbhīprabhṛtayo rītiviśeṣā na vṛttiṣvantarbhūtāḥ । tatra saṃketitārthagocaraḥ śabdavyāpāro abhidhā । sā dvividhārūḍhipūrvikā yogapūrvikā ceti । tapoviśeṣaiḥ prathitaiḥ prajānāṃ śubhaiścaritrairjagatīmahiṣyāḥ ।
bhāgyaiḥ prabhūtairbhuvanasya cāsya bibharti rājyaṃ varavīrarudraḥ ।। atra sarve śabdā rūḍhāḥ । rājñi rudranarādhīśe rañjayatyakhilāḥ prajāḥ । bhūranvarthā vasumatī ratnagarbhā sthireti ca ।।
atra vasumatīratnagarbhetyevamādayo yaugikāḥ । vācyārthānupapattyā tatsaṃbandhinyāropitaḥ śabdavyāpāro lakṣaṇā । jetuḥ kākatibhūbharturākarṇya paṭahadhvanim । sāmantanagarāṇyuccairākrośanti samantataḥ ।।
atra nagarāṇyuccairākrośantīti vācyasyānanvayaḥ । acetanānāmākrośasyāsaṃbhavāt tatratyā janā lakṣyante । patyuḥ kākatināthasya pādapīṭhīmanāratam । sphuradratnaprabhājālairalaṃkurvanti maulayaḥ ।।
atrālaṃkārasiddhyarthaṃ maulibhistadāśrayabhūtā nṛpatayo lakṣyante । kāraṃ yattuhinadyutau sphurati tat sāraṅgamācakṣate । stanmudrāṅkavarāhamindururasā bibhrat samujjṛmbhate ।। atra candrakalaṅkarūpe kuraṅge varāhatvamāropyate ।
viṣayaviṣayiṇorabhihitayorabhedapratipattirāropaḥ । viṣayanigaraṇenābhedapratipattiradhyavasāyaḥ । kākatīyakulāmbhodheḥ prabhavatyeṣa candramāḥ । kṛtaḥ kuvalayollāso yenodayamupeyuṣā ।।
atra pratāparudraścandratayādhyavasīyate । kākatīyakulāmbhodherityatrāropaḥ ।। anviteṣu padārtheṣu vākyārthopaskārārthamarthāntaraviṣayaḥ śabdavyāpāro vyañjanāvṛttiḥ । sā trividhā śabdārthobhayaśaktimūlatvena ।
vāhinyaḥ kākatīndrasya sarvatomukhasaṃbhramāḥ । kurvantyudyatkabandhāḍhyaṃ pratipakṣabalārṇavam ।। atra vāhinīsarvatomukhakabandhaśabdānāmarthaprakaraṇādinā sainyasarvavyāpitvalūnamastakadehaparāṇāṃ vācakatve niyantrite api śabdaśaktimūlā nadījalapratipattiryato jāyate sā vyañjanāvṛttiḥ । prākaraṇikārthaparyavasitābhidhā na śaknotyaprākaraṇikārthapratipattiṃ kartum ।
aprākaraṇikārthasyāpi vākyārthaśobhārthaṃ vakturvivakṣitatvāt । anyatastadapratītervyañjanākhyaṃ śabdasyaiva vyāpārāntaraṃ kalpyate । nātra lakṣaṇāvṛttiḥ saṃbhavati, vācyānupapattyabhāvāt । nātra vyāpāradvayenārthapratipādane vākyabhedaḥ, prayokturvivakṣāparatantratvāllaukikavākyānām ।।
śrutvā kākatibhūbhartuḥ kṣoṇīpāṇigrahotsavam । aṅguṣṭhenālikhan bhūpāḥ pādapīṭhīṃ natānanāḥ ।। atra bhūpā viṣaṇṇā ityarthaśaktyā vyajyate । na cārthaśaktimūle vyañjane anumānaśaṅkā ।
vyaṅgyavyañjakayoravinābhāvābhāvāt । namrānanatvādikāryasyānekakāraṇakatvāt । niyatakāraṇapratītirvivakṣānugṛhītācchabdādeva । kiṃcaikasmādeva vyañjakāt tattadvyaṅgyārthapratītirvaktavivakṣānusāreṇa bhavati, iyamanekavyaṅgyārthapratītiranumānaparipāṭīviruddhā ।
na cābhidhāvṛttiḥ । saṃketitārtha eva tasyāḥ paricaya itīyatī gamanikā । vijitāripuro mūrtau vilasatsarvamaḍgalaḥ । rājamaulirasau bhāti rudradevo jagatpatiḥ ।।
atra vijitāripura ityarthaśaktimūlatvaṃ, vilasatsarvamaṅgalo rājamauliriti śabdaśaktimūlatvamityubhayaśaktimūlatvam । atra pratāparudraśaṅkarayorupamālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। atha kaiśikyādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ nirūpyate । atyarthasukumārārthasaṃdarbhā kaiśikī matā ।
atyuddhātārthasaṃdarbhā vṛttirārabhaṭī smṛtār ।। īṣanmṛdvarthasaṃdarbhā bhāratī vṛttiriṣyater । īṣatprauḍhārthasaṃdarbhā sāttvatī vṛttiriṣyate ।। atyantasukumārau dvau śṛṅgārakaruṇau matau ।
atyuddhatarasau raudrabībhatsau parikīrttitau ।। hāsyaśāntādbhutāḥ kiṃcitsukumārāḥ prakīrttitārḥ । īṣatprauḍhau samākhyātau rasau vīrabhayānakau ।। yatra śṛṅgārakaruṇāvatikomalena saṃdarbheṇa varṇyete tatra kaiśikī ।
yatra raudrabībhatsāvatiprauḍhena saṃdarbheṇa pratipādyete tatrārabhaṭī । yatra nātisukumārā hāsyaśāntādbhutā nātisukumāreṇa saṃdarbheṇa saṃgrathyante tatra bhāratī । yatra nātiprauḍhau vīrabhayānakau nātiprauḍhena saṃdarbheṇa nirvāhyete tatra sāttvatī । narapatimanimeṣaṃ draṣṭumāśaṃsinīnām ।
diva kuvalayadāmaśyāmalā toraṇaśrīḥ ।। jvālairudbhaṭaśastraghaṭṭanabhavatsphārasphuliṅgotkaraiḥ । ruccaṇḍaścalamartigaṇḍanṛpateḥ krodhāgnirāyodhane ।। kāpyanyā saraṇiḥ pratāpayaśasoranyaiva bāhvoḥ prathā ।
sāmagrī caturānanena kiyatī kīdṛk kva vā kalpitā ।। prasthānārambhabherīninadamarinṛpāḥ pūrṇakarṇajvarārtāḥ । strāyadhvaṃ muñcateti pratinṛpatidhiyā pādapān prārthayante ।। madhyamārabhaṭī tvanyā tathā madhyamakaiśikī ।
vṛttī ime ubhe sarvarasasādhāraṇe mate ।। mṛdvarthe apyanatiprauḍhabandhā madhyamakaiśikī ।। śṛṅgārakaruṇayoratisukumārayoralpaprauḍhatvaṃ na dūṣyate । kiṃ tvatiprauḍhasaṃdarbho neṣyate, pratikūlavarṇarūpadoṣāpatteḥ ।।
madhyamārabhaṭī prauḍhe apyarthe nātimṛdukramā ।। atiprauḍhayorapi raudrabībhatsayorīṣanmṛdubandho na dūṣyate । atimṛdusaṃdarbhastu viruddhaḥ । dhik dhik sāhasamāvayorvighaṭanaṃ ko vā vidhiḥ kāṅkṣati ।
buddhvā mūrcchati kākatīyanṛpate tvadvairinārījanaḥ ।। māṃsakīkasasaṃkīrṇāḥ prasaradrudhirāpagāḥ । vasākardamitā yuddhe bhuvo andhrasubhaṭaiḥ kṛtāḥ ।। evaṃ rasāntareṣvapyudāharaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam ।।
vaidarbhyādirītīnāṃ śabdaguṇāśritānāmarthaviśeṣanirapekṣatayā kevalasaṃdarbhasaukumāryaprauḍhatvamātraviṣayatvāt kaiśikyādibhyo bhedaḥ । saṃdarbhasyātidumṛtvamasaṃyuktakomalavarṇabandhatvam । atiprauḍhatvaṃ paruṣavarṇavikaṭabandhatvam । saṃyuktamṛduvarṇeṣvīṣanmṛdutvam ।
avikaṭabandhaparuṣavarṇeṣvīṣatprauḍhatvam ।। atha rītīnāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । rītirnāma guṇāśliṣṭapadasaṃghaṭanā matā । sā tridhāvaidarbhī, gauḍī, pāñcālī ceti ।
bandhapāruṣyarahitā śabdakāṭhinyavarjitā । nātidīrghasamāsā ca vaidarbhī rītiriṣyate ।। kākatīyanarendrasya kīrtticandanacarcanam । digaṅganā vitanvanti vataṃsīkṛtatadguṇāḥ ।।
vibhavati naranāthe kākatīyānvayendau । kṣitisurajanateyaṃ vītakautūhalā'sīt ।। ojaḥ kāntiguṇopetā gauḍīyā rītiriṣyate । pracaṇḍataradordaṇḍakhaṇḍitārātimaṇḍalaḥ ।
vibhartyarvīdhurāṃ gurvīṃ prabhavannandhrabhūpatiḥ ।। bhrāntibhraśyatpataṅgābhayakaraṇacaṇasphāranāsīrareṇuḥ । prodyanmuktaughatārānikaraparivṛtasvarvadhūvaktracandrā ।। pāñcālarītirvaidarbhīgauḍī ityubhayātmikā ।।
kṣoṇīreṇubhare nabhasyatibhṛśaṃ mūvibhramaṃ bibhrati । gāḍhaṃ gūḍatamā ca gautamanadī pātālagaṅgāyate ।। prāṇairyat paritoṣameti satataṃ, kiṃ tvetadatyadbhutam । yat saṃvardhayati trilokabharitāṃ tvatkīrttilakṣmīsudhām ।।
atha śayyā । yā padānāṃ parānyonyamaitrī śayyeti kathyate । ślāghālaṅighetakalpapādapaguṇaprauḍheragādhaujasaḥ । gaṇḍābhoganirūḍhapāṇḍimadhurāṃ dhatte yaśaḥ prāyaśaḥ ।।
atra padavinimayāsahiṣṇutvādbandhasya padānuguṇyarūpā śayyā ।। atha drākṣādipākāḥ । arthagambhīrimā pākaḥ sa dvidhā hṛdayaṅgamaḥ । drākṣāpāko nārikelapākaśca prasphuṭāntarau ।।
yathākramaṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । drākṣāpākaḥ sa kathito bahirantaḥ sphuradrasaḥ । manāgvrīḍājāḍyān praṇayarasakallolabharitān । kaṭākṣān vāmākṣī kirati parito rudranṛpatim ।।
sā nārikelapākaḥ syādantargūḍharasodayaḥ ।। nepathyāntarabimbitasmarakalālāsyaprapañcaśriyaḥ । ko apyasyāstaralabhruvo vijayate śṛṅgāranāṭyakramaḥ ।। atra na drāgarthapratītiḥ ।
evaṃ vastvalaṃkārapratītāvapi draṣṭavyam । pākāntarāṇi madhukṣīrādīni yathāsaṃbhavamūhyāni ।। atha kāvyaviśeṣāḥ । vyaṅgyasya prādhānyāprādhānyābhyāmasphuṭatvena ca trividhaṃ kāvyam ।
vyaṅgyasya prādhānye uttamaṃ kāvyaṃ dhvaniriti vyapadiśyate । aprādhānye madhyamaṃ guṇībhūtavyaṅgyamiti gīyate । vyaṅgyasyāsphuṭatve adhamaṃ kāvyaṃ citramiti gīyate । gādhānambunidhīn karoṣi, kuruṣe kiṃ dikpatīnalpakān ।
sṛṣṭaḥ padmabhuvā guṇaikavasatiḥ śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrasya kulaśailātiśāyi samunnatatvamatisamudraṃ gāmbhīryaṃ lokapālādhikamaiśvaryaṃ ca dhvanyate । tathā kulaśailapayonidhilokapālanirmāṇasaṃrambhātiśāyi sarvavilakṣaṇaṃ kākatīyanirmāṇavaibhavam iti ca vyajyate ।। viśvatrātari vīrarudranṛpatau siṃhāsanādhyāsini ।
śceṣṭā yābhiramuṣya kākativibhordṛṣṭiḥ kṛpārdrīkṛtā ।। atra prāptābhiṣekamahotsavasya pratāparudradevamahārājasyāgre śaraṇārthināṃ pārthivānāṃ tathāvidhakārpaṇyoktipunaḥ punaḥ praṇāmādikaṃ vyaṅgyaṃ tāstāśceṣṭā darśitā iti vācyādanatiśāyi iti guṇībhūtavyaṅgyatā । citraṃ trividhamśabdacitramarthacitramubhayacitraṃ ceti । kṣudrakṣatriyapakṣaśikṣaṇavidhau protkṣiptakaukṣeyakāḥ ।
garjaddurjanagarvaparvatabhidādambholayaḥ kelayaḥ ।। pekkhanto jaaḷacchivāsakamalaṃ maṇṇaṃti viṇṇāṇiṇo । siṭṭhīe rivujīviāi vihiṇo jattassa pīḍhaṃbuaṃ ।। paśyanto jayalakṣmīvāsakamalaṃ manyante vijñāninaḥ ।
sṛṣṭyai ripujīvitāni vidheryātasya pīṭhāmbujam ।।) vidyāsamudre bhuvanaikabhadre pratāparudre jitavairibhadre । rakṣāvinidre dhṛtaśauryamudre kānteva pṛthvī ramate guṇārdre ।। atrānuprāsopamābhyāṃ citratā ।।
।। atha dhvaniviśeṣāḥ ।। atha dhvaniviśeṣā nirūpyante । atra dhvanerlakṣaṇābhidhāmūlatvenāvivakṣitavācyavivakṣitānyaparavācyākhyau prathamaṃ dvau bhedau । avivakṣitavācyasyārthāntarasaṃkramitātyantatiraskṛtavācyatayā dvividhasya vākyapadagatatvena dvaividhye cāturvidhyam ।
vivakṣitānyaparavācyasya saṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyatayā dvau bhedau । saṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgye śabdaśaktimūle vastvalaṅakārarūpatayā dvaividhye vākyapadagatatvena cāturvidhyam । arthaśaktimūle saṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgye arthasya svataḥ saṃbhavitvena kaviprauḍhoktisiddhatvena kavinibaddhoktisiddhatvena ca traividhyam । trividhasya vastvalaṃkārarūpatayā dvaividhye ṣaḍvidhatvam ।
ṣaḍvidhasyāpi vyaṅgyavyañjakatayā dvaividhye dvādaśavidhatvam । dvādaśavidhasyāpi prabandhagatatvena vākyagatatvena padagatatvena ca traividhye ṣaṭtriṃśatprakāro arthaśaktimūlo anuraṇanadhvaniḥ । ubhayaśaktimūlo vākyagatatvenaikavidha eva । evaṃ saṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyadhvanerekacatvāriṃśadbhedāḥ ।
asaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ prabandhavākyapadapadaikadeśaracanāvarṇagatatvena ṣaḍvidhaḥ । evaṃ vivakṣitānyaparavācyadhvaneḥ saptacatvāriṃśadbhedāḥ । avivakṣitavācyabhedaiścaturbhiḥ saha dhvaneḥ prathamaṃ śuddhā ekapañcāśad bhedāḥ । teṣāṃ pratyekamekaikasyaikaikena saṃbandhe prathamabhedasyaikapañcāśad bhedāḥ ।
dvitīyasya pañcāśad bhedāḥ । tṛtīyasyaikonapañcāśad bhedāḥ । anena krameṇottarottarasyaikakaibhedaparityāge ṣaḍviṃśatyuttaraśatatrayādhikasahasrasaṃkhyākāḥ miśrabhedāḥ । avivakṣitavācyasya vivakṣitānyaparavācyasaṃbandhe yo bhedastasminnevāntarbhūto vivakṣitānyaparavācyasyāvivakṣitavācyasaṃbandhe bhedo na pṛthagbhūtaḥ ।
anenaiva krameṇa vastudhvaneralaṃkāradhvanisaṃbandhabhedo apyalaṃkāradhvanervastudhvanisaṃbandhānna pṛthagbhūta iti pūrvapūrvasyottarottarasaṃbandhe ekaikabhedanyūnatā jñeyā । caturuttaraśatatrayādhikapañcasahasrāṇi bhedāḥ । śuddhāścandraśarā miśrā ṛtunetrānalendavaḥ । saṃsṛṣṭisaṃkarāyātāstvabdhikhāgniśarābhidhāḥ ।।
śuddhānāmekapañcāśadbhedānāṃ nāmadheyani kathyante । padagatārthāntarasaṃkramitāvivakṣitavācyadhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatārthāntarasaṃkramitāvivakṣitavācyadhvaniḥ ।। padagatātyantatiraskṛtāvivakṣitavācyadhvaniḥ ।।
vākyagatātyantatiraskṛtāvivakṣitavācyadhvaniḥ ।। padagataśabdaśaktimūlasaṃlakṣyakramavastudhvaniḥ ।। padagataśabdaśaktimūlasaṃlakṣyakramālaṅkāradhvaniḥ ।। vākyagataśabdaśaktimūlasaṃlakṣyakramavastudhvaniḥ ।।
vākyagataśabdaśaktimūlasaṃlakṣyakramālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। padagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। padagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। padagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
padagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
vākyagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
prabandhagatasvataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। padagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। padagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। padagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
padagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakaviprauḍhotkisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।।
vākyagatakraviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
prabandhagatakaviprauḍhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। padagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। padagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। padagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṃkāreṇālaṅkāradhvaniḥ ।।
padagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇa alaṃkāradhvaniḥ ।।
vākyagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunā vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo vastunālaṅkāradhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇālaṅkāradhvamiḥ ।।
prabandhagatakavinibaddhoktisiddhārthaśaktimūlo alaṅkāreṇa vastudhvaniḥ ।। prabandhagatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।। padagatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।।
padaikadeśagatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।। racanāgatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।। varṇagatāsaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ ।। vākyagatobhayaśaktimūlo rasādidhvaniḥ ।।
tatra diṅmātramudāhriyate । mūrdhāno yūyamāsmākāḥ kimityaunnatyamicchatha । iti pratāparudrasya praṇatāḥ pratipārthivāḥ ।। atra āsmākā iti sarvadainyabhūmayo vayamīdṛśānāmasmākaṃ saṃbandhino yūyamityarthāntarasaṃkramitāvivakṣitavācyatā ।
viśadimaviliptaviyato dhavalimaparipūritākhilāśāntāḥ । viharanti yaśaḥ pūrā gaurāḥ śrīkākatīndrasya ।। atra viśadimaviliptaviyata ityatyantatiraskṛtavācyatvam । anenaiva krameṇa vākyagatatvenāpyudāhāryam ।
abdānṛtūn vinā māsān śuklapakṣān vinā tithīn । rātrīrvināpi kāṅkṣanti kākatīyaripustriyaḥ ।। atra ṛtuprabhṛtīnāṃ kāmoddīpakatvāt tadabhāvo ripustrībhirākāṅkṣyata iti pratīyate । tena tāsāṃ priyaviyogarūpaṃ vastu vyajyate ।
anena pratāparudrasya sarve śatravo nihatā iti vācyādatiśayaḥ । tathā priyavirahavidhurāḥ śatrustriyaḥ katipayavatsarān jīvitāśayā prathamamṛtūnāmabhāvaṃ vāñchanti । anantaraṃ tānapi gamayitumaśaktāḥ katipayamāseṣu prāṇān dhārayitumudyuktā jyotsnāvatāṃ pakṣāṇāṃ vināśaṃ vāñchanti । anantaraṃ māsanapyapanetumapārayantyaḥ katipayatithiṣu jīvitāśayā rātrīṇāmasṛṣṭimabhilaṣantīti bahuvastu vastunā vyajyate ।
dṛṣṭvā kākativīrarudranṛpateḥ kīrttiṃ jagadvyāpinīṃ vastuṃ vāñchati śambhuratra śayituṃ lakṣmīpatiḥ kāṅkṣati । snātuṃ dhāvati divyatāpasagaṇaḥ saṃvardhituṃ vārdhayaśceṣṭante savilāsamabhramurapi spraṣṭuṃ śanairīhate ।। atra harasya kailāsabhrāntiḥ hareḥ kṣīrārṇavabhrāntirityādiḥ bhrāntimadalaṅkāro byajyate ।। pratāparudrasya raṇe kṛpāṇaḥ sadyaḥ samudyadrudhirāruṇaśrīḥ ।
ālambate roṣakaṣāyitasya kālīkaṭākṣasya vijṛmbhitāni ।। atrālambata iti nidarśanālaṅkāreṇa sakalaripukṣayaḥ kṣaṇāt kṛta iti vastu vyajyate ।। kākatīyavibhoḥ kīrttipuṇḍarīke vijṛmbhite । dhatte madhukarakrīḍāṃ tamālaśyāmalaṃ nabhaḥ ।।
atra kīrttipuṇḍarīke nabho bhramarakrīḍāṃ dhatta iti nidarśanālaṃkāreṇāśrayāśrayiṇoranānuguṇyarūpo adhikālaṃkāro vyajyate । āśrayasya kīrttipuṇḍarīkasya vaipulyaṃ amarasādṛśyapratipādanenālpatvaṃ ca nabhasaḥ pratīyate । eṣu svataḥ siddhārthaśaktimūlatvam । chidracchadmaśravaṇapadavīcāriṇīṃ cāraṇaudhaiḥ ।
kauñcakṣmābhṛd bhavati mahato vismayānniścalāṅgaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrasya kīrttiḥ sthāvarāṇāyapi vismayakāriṇīti vastu vyajyate ।। vīrarudrabhaṭān dṛṣṭvā jayalakṣmīvṛtān raṇe । karṣantyarivadhūkeśān kānane kaṇṭakidrumāḥ ।।
atra jayalakṣmīsamāliṅgitān vīrarudrabhaṭān dṛṣṭvā samadanā iva kaṇṭakidrumāḥ śatruvadhūkeśān karṣantīvetyutprekṣā vyajyate । osarai sahīhi samaṃ lajjā vahuāe siḍhilamāṇāe । appaggahaṇabhayeṇa vva savihagae maṇohare daie ।। (apasarati sakhībhiḥ samaṃ lajjā vadhvāḥ śithilamānāyāḥ ।
ātmagrahaṇabhayeneva savidhagate manohare dayite) ।। atrotprekṣayā'liṅganarūpaṃ vastu vyajyate ।। abhayaṃ yācamānānāṃ kākatīyendravidviṣām । rakṣāṃ nāṅgīkarotīva vanaṃ śākhāgrakampanaiḥ ।।
atra nāṅgīkarotīvetyutprekṣayā pratāparudraśatrūṇāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ kartuṃ vanamapi bibhetīvetyutprekṣā vyajyate । ajaha taha va hodu ajjā ṇaraṇāha karehi rakkhaṇaṃ sasiṇo । jaṃ tāe kaḍakhukkā āṇattā taṃ masīkāduṃ ।। (ayathā tathā vā bhavatvāryā naranātha kuru rakṣaṇaṃ śaśinaḥ ।
yattayā kaṭākṣolkā ājñaptā taṃ maṣīkartum) ।। atra virahāturā āryā candrikāmasahamānā roṣojjvalitayā kaṭākṣolkayā candraṃ maṣīkaroti sa rakṣaṇīya ityanena vastunā itaḥ paraṃ sā jīvitaṃ dhārayitumaśaktā, adhunaiva tvayā samāgantavyamiti vastu vyajyate ।। kastvaṃ śubhrākhilāṅgaścarasi, nanu yaśo vīrarudrasya vartte ko ayaṃ te divyadehaḥ sphurati parisare, matsuhṛt tatpratāpaḥ । pracchādyālaṃ sphuradbhiḥ kumudasarasijaiḥ khyāpitaṃ vaḥ svarūpaṃ somākārai svāgataṃ vāmavadhigirirahaṃ kalpito nistamaskaḥ ।।
atra pratāparudrayaśaḥ pratāpayoḥ somārkasādṛśyapratīterupamā vyajyate । uvaha haḷā vahuāe taha ārūḍho vi ṇibhbharo māṇo । ṇivaisamāamalaṃbhamasaṃjāabhao vva osarai ।। (paśyata halā vadhvāstathā rūḍho api nirbharo mānaḥ ।
nṛpatisamāgamasaṃbhramasaṃjātabhaya ivāpasarati) ।। atrotprekṣayā priyaprārthanāṃ vinaiva māninīmanaḥ prasannamiti vibhāvanālaṃkāro vyajyate ।। aprāpya sevāvasaraṃ nātha kāntāvṛtasya te । tvatkīrttiṃ sevamāneva śyāmā sarvāṅgapāṇḍurā ।।
atra sevamānevetyutprekṣayā sarvathā svīkāryatvādirūpaṃ vastu vyajyate ।। evaṃ prabandhādigatatvena yathāsaṃbhavamudāharaṇāni draṣṭavyāni; vistarabhayādiha noktāni ।। atha śabdaśaktimūladhvaniḥ । sa ca vastvalaṃkāragatatvena dvividhaḥ ।
"alaṅkāro atha vastveva śabdādyatrāvabhāsate । pradhānatvena sa jñeyaḥ śabdaśaktyudbhavo dvidhā ।। a; iti । eso saccaṃ rāo sāmā khu tumaṃ samāamo doṇṇaṃ ।
kiṃ uṇa ṇa padosakahā dīsaḥ edaṃ khu accariaṃ ।। (eṣa satyaṃ rājā śyāmā khalu tvaṃ samāgamo dvayoḥ । kiṃ punarna pradoṣakathā dṛśyate etatkhalvāścaryam) ।। atra prakaraṇena kāntānṛpavācakābhyāṃ śyāmārājaśabdābhyāṃ niśācandrapratīterupamā vyajyate ।।
kāntāravāsasaṃtaptāḥ saṃśṛṇudhvaṃ hitāditaḥ । kurudhvamadhunā rājapādasevāṃ nareśvarāḥ ।। atra rājapādasevāmiti śabdaśaktyā prakṛtasya pratāparudrasya pratītiḥ prakaraṇājjāyate । anena pratāparudrasya sevā kartavyā kimaraṇyavāsena saṃtaptā iti vastu vyajyate ।।
jiṣṇureṣa bhujastambhajṛmbhamāṇādbhutāyudhaḥ । muñcantu kṣmābhṛtaḥ sarve nijapakṣavijṛmbhitam ।। atra kṣmābhṛto nijapakṣavijṛmbhitaṃ muñcantu, jiṣṇureṣa ityatra śabdaśaktimūlatā । bhujastambhajambhamāṇādbhutāyudha ityatrārthaśaktimūlatā ।।
asaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyo rasādidhvaniḥ । "rasabhāvatadābhāsabhāvaśāntyādirakramaḥ । bhinno rasādyalaṃkārādalaṃkāryatayā sthitaḥ ।। a; iti ।
rasabhāvodāharaṇaṃ tatsvarūpanirūpaṇaprapañce rasaprakaraṇe bhaviṣyati ।। guṇībhūtavyaṅgyam aṣṭavidhaṃ nirūpyate । guṇībhūtavyaṅgyaṃ madhyamaṃ kāvyamaṣṭavidham । "agūḍhamaparasyāṅgaṃ vācyasiddhyaṅgamasphuṭam ।
saṃdigdhatulyaprādhānye kākvākṣiptamasundaram ।। a; iti । kāminīkucakalaśavad gūḍhasyaiva camatkārakāritvādagūḍhavyaṅgyaṃ madhyamaṃ kāvyam । aunnatyaṃ yadi varṇyate śikhariṇaḥ kradhyanti nīcaiḥ kṛtā gāmbhīryaṃ yadi kīrttyate jaladhayaḥ kṣubhyanti gādhīkṛtāḥ ।
tat tvāṃ varṇayituṃ bibhemi yadi vā jāto asmyagastyaḥ sthitastvatpārśve guṇaratnarohaṇagire śrīvīrarudraprabho ।। atra "yadi vā jāto asmyagastyaḥ sthitaḥ'; ityanena jalanidhiparvatebhyo na bibhemīti vyaṅgyamagūḍham ।। aparasyāṅgaṃ, yatra rasāde rasādiraṅgaṃ tadapi guṇībhūtavyaṅgyameva । vītavrīḍamapāstamānamudayadvaisvaryamāvirbhavatsvedaṃ nirbharagātravepathu milanmūrcchaṃ galadbāṣpakam ।
saṃjātapralayaṃ ca kākatimahīnātha ! smarodvejitā bhūpāḥ śailaguhāsu yānti vijanaṃ bhītyā samāliṅgitāḥ ।। atra śṛṅgārasya bhayarasāṅgatvam । karālaḥ kākatīndrasya karavālanavāmbudaḥ । dhārayā śamayatyugraṃ pratāpajvalanaṃ dviṣām ।।
atra jaladhārā vyaṅgyā । sā ca karavālanavāmbuda ityasya vācyabhūtasya rūpakasya siddhikṛditi guṇībhūtavyaṅgyam ।। vīrarudrakṛpāṇasya mahimā ko apyanaṅkuśaḥ । prasūte kīrttigaṅgāṃ yaḥ pītvā dviṣadasṛṅnadīm ।।
atra kṛpāṇasya jahnorādhikyapratipādanād vyatirekaḥ paramasphuṭaḥ pratīyate ।। kākatikṣmāpaterdṛṣṭiranurāgataraṅgitā । lagnā kalhāramāleva vadhvāstuṅge kucadvaye ।। atrāliṅganecchāyāṃ vākyaviśrāntirathavā stanamaṇḍalāloka eveti saṃdehaḥ ।।
nṛpāḥ pratāparudrasya niṣevadhvaṃ padāmbuje । anyathāsya manastādṛkprasādaṃ kaluṣāyate ।। atra pratāparudrasya pādasevā yadi tyajyate tadānīṃ nagareṣu vāso durlabha iti vyaṅgyārthasya vācyasya ca samaṃ prādhānyam ।। easilāmahilāṇaṃ soūṇa ṇareṃdadassaṇāmoaṃ ।
guruaṇaṇiaṃtiāe vahuāe sāmalaṃ vaaṇaṃ ।। (ekaśilāmahilānāṃ śrutvā narendradarśanāmodam । gurujananiyantritāyā vadhvāḥ śyāmalaṃ vadanam) ।। atra narendradarśananimittaṃ harṣamutpaśyantyā vadhvā mukhaṃ śyāmalamiti vācyasyaiva cārutvam ।
gurujananiyantritāhaṃ narendraṃ draṣṭuṃ na gatavatyasmi iti vyaṅgyārthasyācārutvam ।। yatra kākvār'thāntaramākṣipyate, tadapi guṇībhūtavyaṅgyameva । piasahi kahehi ahiā khoṇī lacchī sarassaī majjhā । jāṃ bahu maṇṇai soaṃ ṇaraṇāho guṇavisesaṇṇo ।।
(priyasakhi kathayādhikā kṣoṇī lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī mattaḥ । yāṃ bahu manyate so ayaṃ naranātho guṇaviśeṣajñaḥ) ।। atra kṣoṇī madadhiketi kākukalpanayādhikā na bhavatīti vastu vyajyate ।। citraṃ tu kāvyaṃ śabdārthālaṅkāracitratayā bahuvidham ।
tatprapañco apyalaṅkāraprakaraṇe vyaktībhaviṣyati ।। ।। mahākāvyopakāvyādiprabandhanirūpaṇam ।। atha mahākāvyādayaḥ prabandhā nirūpyante ।
nagarārṇavaśailartucandrārkodayavarṇanam । udyānasalilakrīḍāmadhupānaratotsavāḥ ।। vipralambho vivāhaśca kumārodayavarṇanam । mantradūtaprayāṇājināyakābhyudayā api ।।
etāni yatra varṇyante tanmahākāvyamucyate । eṣāmaṣṭādaśānāṃ yaiḥ kauścidūnamapīṣyate ।। tattrividham । gadyamayaṃ padyamayamubhayamayaṃ ceti ।।
apādaḥ padasaṃghāto gadyaṃ; padyaṃ catuṣpadam । gadyakāvyaṃ kādambaryādi । padyakāvyaṃ raghuvaṃśādi । asargabandhamapi yadupakāvyamudīryate ।।
asargabandhaṃ sūryaśatakādi । gadyapadyamayaṃ kāvyaṃ campūrityabhidhīyate । vaktraṃ cāparavaktraṃ ca socchvāsatvaṃ ca bhedakam ।। varṇyate yatra kāvyajñairasāvākhyāyikā matā ।
yatra vaktrāparavaktranāmānau vṛttaviśeṣau varṇyete socchravāsaparicchinnā'khyāyikā harṣacaritādi । kṣudraprabandhanirūpaṇam ।। atha kṣudrāḥ prabandhā nirūpyante । yena kenāpi tālena gadyapadyasamanvitam ।।
jayatyupakramaṃ mālinyādiprāsavicitritam । tadudāharaṇaṃ nāma vibhaktyaṣṭakasaṃyutam ।। yatrādau jayatyupakramaṃ mālinyādivṛttaṃ ramyaṃ padyaṃ nibadhyate, anantaram "api ca'; ityupakramāṇyaṣṭavākyāni saprāsāni satālāni prativibhakti nibadhyante, anantaraṃ vibhaktyābhāsāḥ, tat udāharaṇam । saṃbodhanavibhaktyā yat pracuraṃ padyapūrvakam ।
vimuktapunarākṛṣṭaśabdaṃ syāccakravālakam ।। ādyantapadyasaṃyuktā saṃskṛtaprākṛtātmikā । aṣṭabhirvā caturbhirvā vākyaiḥ skandhasamanvitā ।। pratiskandhaṃ bhinnavākyarītirdevanṛpocitā ।
sarvato devaśabdādireṣā bhogāvalī matā ।। varṇyamānāṅkabirudavarṇanapracurojjvalā । vākyāḍambarasaṃyuktā sā matā birudāvalī ।। tārāṇāṃ saṃkhyayā padyairyuktā tārāvalī matā ।
evaṃ kaviprauḍhoktisiddhāḥ kṣudrāḥ prabandhā yathāsaṃbhavamūhyāḥ । athaiteṣāmudāharaṇāni vistarabhayādiha noktāni ।। iti śrīvidyānāthaviracite pratāparudrayaśobhūṣaṇe alaṃkāraśāstre kāvyaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।। ।। atha nāṭakaprakaraṇam ।।
।। atha nāṭyapradhānāḥ prabandhā nirūpyante ।। tatra nāṭyasvarūpaṃ nirūpyate । caturvidhairabhinayaiḥ sāttvikāṅgikapūrvakaiḥ । dhīrodāttādyavasthānukṛtirnāṭyaṃ rasāśrayam ।।
bhāvāśrayaṃ tu nṛttyaṃ syānnṛttaṃ tālalayānvitam । eṣā daśarūpakoktā prakriyā । nṛttyanṛtūyornāṭakādyaṅgatvādiha svarūpanirūpaṇaṃ kṛtam । "madhuroddhatabhedena taddvayaṃ dvividhaṃ punaḥ ।
lāsyatāṇḍavarūpeṇa nāṭakādyupakārakam ।। a; iti । tena nāṭyena daśa rūpakāṇi bhavanti । nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇaṃ bhāṇaḥ prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ ।
vyāyogasamavākārau vīthyaṅkehāmṛgā daśa ।। nāṭyāśrayatvenābheda iti śaṅkā na yujyate । vastunetṛrasāsteṣāṃ rūpakāṇāṃ hi bhedakāḥ ।। vastu trividhamprakhyātam, utpādyam, miśraṃ ceti ।
"prakhyātotpādyamiśratvabhedāt tattrividhaṃ matam a; iti । itihāsanibandhanaṃ prakhyātam, kavikalpitamutpādyam, saṃkarāyattaṃ miśraṃ ceti evamādivastubhedānnāyakabhedāt rūpakāṇāṃ parasparaṃ bhedaḥ । tathā hināṭake prakhyātamitivṛttam, dhīrodātto nāyakaḥ, śṛṅgāravīrarasayoranyatarasya prādhānyam, anyeṣāṃ rasānāmaṅgatvenānupraveśaḥ । prakaraṇe utpādyamitivṛttam, dhīraśānto nāyakaḥ, śṛṅgārarasasyaiva prādhānyam ।
bhāṇe utpādyamitivṛttam, dhūrtaviṭo nāyakaḥ, śṛṅgāravīrayoḥ sūcanāmātrasāratā । prahasane kalpyamitivṛttam, pāṣaṇḍaprabhṛtayo nāyakāḥ, hāsyarasaḥ pradhānam । ḍime prakhyātamitivṛttam, devagandharvapiśācādayo dhīroddhatā nāyakāste ṣoḍaśa, raudrarasaḥ pradhānam, vīraśṛṅgārayoranupraveśaḥ । vyāyoge prakhyātamitivṛttam, dhīroddhato nāyakaḥ, vīrarasaḥ pradhānam ।
samavakāre devāsurādayo dvādaśa nāyakāḥ, vīrarasaḥ pradhānam, kalpitamitivṛttaṃ prasiddhaṃ vā । vīthyāṃ kalpitamitivṛttam, dhīroddhato nāyakaḥ, śṛṅgārarasasya sūcanāmātrasāratā । aṅke prakhyātamitivṛttam, prākṛtajano nāyakaḥ, karuṇarasaḥ pradhānam, īhāmṛge miśramitivṛttam, dhīroddhato nāyakaḥ, śṛṅgārarasasyābhāsatvam । atha teṣāṃ sāmagrī nirūpyate ।
tatra pañca sandhayaḥ । "mukhaṃ pratimukhaṃ garbhaḥ sāvamarśopasaṃhṛtiḥ'; iti । saṃdhirnāmaikena prayojanenānvitānāṃ kathānāmavāntaraprayojanasaṃbandhaḥ । tatrārambhabījasaṃbandho mukhasaṃdhiḥ ।
prayatnabindusaṃbandhaḥ pratimukhasaṃndhiḥ । prāptyāśāpatākayoḥ saṃbandho garbhasaṃdhiḥ । niyatāptiprakaryoḥ saṃbandho vimarśasaṃdhiḥ । phalāgamakāryayoḥ saṃbandho nirvahaṇasaṃdhiḥ ।
"bījabindupatākākhyaprakarīkāryalakṣaṇāḥ । ārambhayatnaprāptyāśāniyatāptiphalāgamāḥ ।। arthaprakṛtayaḥ pañca pañcāvasthāsamanvitāḥ । yathāsaṃkhyena jāyante mukhādyāḥ pañca saṃdhayaḥ ।।
a; iti । autsukyamātramārambhaḥ phalalābhāya bhūyase । prayatnastu phalaprāptau vyāpāro atitvarānvitaḥ ।। upāyāpāyaṅkābhyāṃ prāptyāśā kāryasaṃbhavaḥ ।
apāyābhāvataḥ kāryaniścayo niyatāptikā ।। samagraphalasaṃpattiḥ phalāgama udāhṛtaḥ । stokoddiṣṭaḥ kāryaheturbīṃjaṃ vistāryanekadhā ।। avāntarārthavicchede binduracchedakāraṇam ।
pratipādyakathāṅgaṃ syāt patākā vyāpinī kathā ।। avyāpinī prakarikā kāryaṃ nirvāhakṛt phale ।। mukhaṃ bījasamutpattirnānārtharasasaṃbhavā ।। aṅgāni dvādaśaitasya bījārambhasamanvayāt ।।
bījārambhānuguṇyena mukhasandheraṅgāni prayoktavyāni । upakṣepaḥ parikaraḥ parinyāso vilobhanam ।। yuktiḥ prāptiḥ samādhānaṃ vidhānaṃ paribhāvanā । udbhedabhedakaraṇānyanvarthāni yathākramam ।।
bījanyāsa upakṣepaḥ । bījasya bahūkaraṇaṃ parikaraḥ । bījaniṣpattiḥ parinyāsaḥ । bījaguṇavarṇanaṃ vilobhanam ।
bījānukūlasaṃghaṭanaprayojanavicāro yuktiḥ । bījasukhāgamaḥ prāptiḥ । bījasaṃnidhānaṃ samādhānam । bījasukhaduḥ khaheturvidhānam ।
bījaviṣayāścaryāveśaḥ paribhāvanā । gūḍhabījaprakāśanamudbhedaḥ । bījānuguṇaprotsāhanaṃ bhedaḥ । bījānuguṇaprastutakāryārambhaḥ karaṇam ।
etāni dvādaśa mukhasandheraṅgāni । eteṣāṃ madhye upakṣepaparikaraparinyāsayuktyudbhedasamādhānānāmāvaśyakatvam । lakṣyālakṣyasya bījasya vyaktiḥ pratimukhaṃ matam । binduprayatnānugamādaṅgānyasya trayodaśa ।।
binduprayatnānuguṇyena pratimukhasandheraṅgāni prayoktavyāni । vilāsaḥ parisarpaśca vidhūtaṃ śamanarmaṇī । narmadyutiḥ pragamanaṃ nirodhaḥ paryupāsanam ।। vajraṃ puṣpamupanyāso varṇasaṃhāra ityapi ।।
saṃbhogaviṣayamanoratho vilāsaḥ । dṛṣṭanaṣṭapadārthānusaraṇaṃ parisarpaḥ । aniṣṭavastuvikṣepo vidhūtam । aratyupaśamanaṃ śamaḥ ।
parihāsavacanaṃ narma । anurāgoddhāṭanotthā prītirnarmadyutiḥ । uttarottaravākyairanurāgabījaprakāśanaṃ pragamanam । chadmanā hitāgamananirodhanaṃ nirodhaḥ ।
iṣṭajanānunayaḥ paryupāsanam । pramukhaniṣṭhuravacanaṃ vajram । anurāgaprakāśanaviśiṣṭavacanaṃ puṣpam । anurāgahetuvākyaracanopanyāsaḥ ।
caturvarṇanirvarṇataṃ varṇasaṃhāraḥ । eteṣāṃ madhye parisarpapragamanavajropanyāsapuṣpāṇāṃ prādhānyam । garbhastu dṛṣṭanaṣṭasya bījasyānveṣaṇaṃ muhuḥ ।। asyāptyāśāpatākānuguṇyenāṅgopakalpanam ।।
patākāprāptyāśānuguṇyena garbhasandheraṅgāni prayoktavyāni । abhūtāharaṇaṃ mārgo rūpodāharaṇakramāḥ ।। saṃgrahaścānumānaṃ ca toṭakādhibadhe tathā । udvegasaṃbhramākṣepā dvādaśāṅgānyanukramāt ।।
prastutopayogicchadmācaraṇamabhūtāharaṇam । tattvārthānukīrtanaṃ mārgaḥ । vitarkapratipādanāvākyaṃ rūpam । prastutotkarṣābhidhānamudāhṛtiḥ ।
saṃcintitārthaprāptiḥ kramaḥ ।। prastutopayogisāmadānavacanaṃ saṃgrahaḥ । ।। liṅgādabhyūhanamanumānam ।
roṣasaṃbhramavacanaṃ toṭakam । iṣṭajanātisaṃdhānamadhibalam । apakārijanād bhayamudvegaḥ । śaṅkātrāsau ca saṃbhramaḥ ।
iṣṭārthopāyānusaraṇamākṣepaḥ । eteṣāṃ madhye abhūtāharaṇamārgatoṭakādhibalākṣepāṇāṃ prādhānyam । garbhasaṃdhau prasiddhasya bījārthasyāvamarśanam । hetunā yena kenāpi vimarśaḥ saṃdhiriṣyate ।।
niyatāptiprakaryukteraṅgānyatra trayodaśa ।। niyatāptiprakaryānuguṇyena vimarśasaṃdheraṅgāni prayoktavyāni । tatrāpavādaḥ saṃpheṭo vidravadravaśaktayaḥ ।। dyutiḥ prasaṅgaścalanaṃ vyavasāyo nirodhanam ।
prarocanaṃ vicalanamādānaṃ tu trayodaśa ।। doṣaprakhyāpanamapavādaḥ । roṣasaṃbhāṣaṇaṃ saṃpheṭaḥ । vadhabandhādikaṃ vidravaḥ ।
gurutiraskṛtirdravaḥ । virodhaśamanaṃ śaktiḥ । tarjanodvejane dyutiḥ । gurukīrtanaṃ prasaṅgaḥ ।
upamānaṃ calanam । svaśaktipraśaṃsanaṃ vyavasāyaḥ । krodhasaṃrabdhānāmanyonyavikṣepo nirodhanam । siddhavadbhāviśreyaḥ kathanaṃ prarocanam ।
svaguṇā'viṣkaraṇaṃ vicalanam । kāryasaṃgraha ādānam । eteṣāṃ madhye apavādaśaktivyavasāyaprarocanādānānāṃ prādhānyam ।। bījavanto mukhādyarthā viprakīrṇā yathāyatham ।
aikārthyamupanīyante yatra nirvahaṇaṃ hi tat ।। phalāptikāryānuguṇyādaṅgānyasya caturdaśa ।। phalāptikāryānuguṇyena nirvahaṇasaṃdheraṅgāni caturdaśa pratipādanīyāni । saṃdhirvirodho grathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ paribhāṣaṇam ।।
prasādānandasamayāḥ kṛtyābhāṣopagūhanam । pūrvabhāvopasaṃhārau praśastiśca caturdaśa ।। bījopaśamanaṃ saṃdhiḥ । kāryamārgaṇaṃ virodhaḥ ।
kāryopakṣepaṇaṃ grathanam । bījānuguṇakāryaprakhyāpanaṃ nirṇayaḥ । mitho jalpanaṃ paribhāṣā । paryupāsanaṃ prasādaḥ ।
vāñchitārthaprāptirānandaḥ । duḥ khapraśamanaṃ samayaḥ । kṛtiḥ । prāptakāryānumodanam ābhāṣaṇam ।
adbhutārthaprāptiḥ upagūhanam । iṣṭakāryadarśanaṃ pūrvabhāvaḥ । kāryārthopasaṃhṛtiḥ saṃhāraḥ । śubhaśaṃsanaṃ praśastiḥ ।
evaṃ catuḥ ṣaṣṭyaṅgasamanvitāḥ pañca sandhayaḥ pratipāditāḥ । [andhināṃprayojanāni]eteṣāṃ ṣaṭ prayojanāni saṃbhavantivivakṣitārthapratipādanaṃ, gopyārthagopanaṃ, prakāśyārthaprakāśanaṃ, abhinayarāgasamṛddhiḥ, camatkāritvam, itivṛttavistaraśceti । tatretivṛttaṃ sūcyamasūcyaṃ ceti dvividham । asūcyamapi dvividhaṃdṛśyaṃ śrāvyaṃ ca ।
tatra sūcyasya sūcanākramaḥ pañcavidhaḥ । "viṣkambhacūlikāṅkāsyapraveśāṅkāvatāraṇaiḥ'iti । vṛttavartiṣyamāṇānāṃ kathāṃśānāṃ nidarśakaḥ । saṃkṣepārthastu viṣkambho madhyapātraprayojitaḥ ।।
sa dvividhaḥ-śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇaśceti । kevalasaṃskṛtaprāyaḥ śuddhaḥ । saṃskṛtaprākṛtamiśritaḥ saṃkīrṇaḥ । antaryavanikāsaṃsthaiścūlikār'thasya sūcanā ।।
yatra nepathyagataiḥ pātrairarthaḥ sūcyate sā cūlikā । aṅkāntapātrairaṅkāsyamuttarāṅkārthasūcanā ।। yatra pūrvāṅkāntapātrairuttarāṅkārthaḥ sūcyate tadaṅkāsyam । vṛttavartiṣyamāṇānāṃ kathāṃśānāṃ nidarśakaḥ ।
praveśakastu nādye aṅke nīcapātraprayojitaḥ ।। nīcapātraprayuktaḥ praveśakaḥ ādye aṅke na prayoktavyaḥ । yatra syāduttarāṅkārthaḥ pūrvāṅkārthānusaṃgataḥ ।। asūcitāṅkapātraṃ tadaṅkāvataraṇaṃ matam ।।
ebhiḥ sūcyaṃ sūcayitvā dṛśyamaṅkaiḥ pradarśayet ।। pratyakṣanetṛcarito binduvyaktipuraskṛtaḥ । aṅko nānāprakārārthasaṃvidhānarasāśrayaḥ ।। sūtradhāro naṭīṃ brūte māriṣaṃ vā vidūṣakam ।
svakāryaprastutākṣepi citroktyā yat tadāmukham ।। prastāvanā vā tatra syāt kathodghātaḥ pravartakam । prayogātiśayaśceti trīṇyaṅgānyāmukhasya tu ।। svetivṛttasamaṃ vākyamarthaṃ vā yatra sūtriṇaḥ ।
gṛhītvā praviśet pātraṃ kathoddhāto dvidhaiva saḥ ।। prastūyamānakālasya guṇavarṇanayā svataḥ । praviśet sūcitaṃ pātraṃ yatra tatsyāt pravartakam ।। eṣo ayamityupakṣepāt sūtradhāraprayogataḥ ।
pātrapraveśo yatrāyaṃ prayogātiśayo mataḥ ।। vīthyaṅgānyāmukhāṅgatvāducyante atra svabhāvataḥ । uddhātyakāvalagite prapañcatrigate chalam ।। vākkelyadhibale gaṇḍamavasyanditanālike ।
asatpralāpavyāhāramṛdavāni trayodaśa ।। gūḍhārthapadaparyāyamālārūpeṇa praśnottaramālārūpeṇa coddhātyakaṃ dvividham । avalagitamapi dvividham । yatraikatra samāveśāt kāryamanyatra siddhyati ।
vastuno anyatra vā yatsyāt dvidhāvalagitaṃ matam ।। anyakāryacchadmanā anyakāryakaraṇam, anyakāryaprasaṅgāt prakṛtakāryasiddhiśca । asadbhūtaṃ mithaḥ । stotraṃ prapañcaḥ ।
trigataṃ dvividhaṃpūrvaraṅgāṅgaṃ prastāvanāṅgaṃ ceti । pūrvaraṅge naṭādisaṃlāpaḥ, atra tu sāmyādanekārthayojanaṃ trigatam । priyasadṛśairvākyairapriyairvilobhanaṃ chalam । sākāṅkṣasyāpi vākyasya nivartanamuktipratyuktiḥ vākkelirdvividhā ।
spardhayānyonyavākyādhikyamadhibalam । sahasoditaṃ prastutavirodhi gaṇḍam । rasavaśāduktānyathāvyākhyānamavasyanditam । sopahāsanigūḍhārthaprahelikā nālikā ।
asaṃbandhakathāprāyaḥ pralopo asatpralāpaḥ । anyārthaṃ hāsyalobhakaraṃ vacanaṃ vyāhāraḥ । doṣāṇāṃ guṇatvapratipādanaṃ mṛdavam । eteṣāṃ madhye yathāsaṃbhavaṃ kānicit prastāvanāyāṃ prayoktavyāni ।
tha daśarūpakāṇāṃ svarūpaṃ nirūpyate । sāṅgairmukhapratimukhagarbhamarśopasaṃhṛtaiḥ । pūrṇaṃ prakṛtiranyeṣāmādhikārikavṛttavat ।। vīraśṛṅgārayorekaḥ pradhānaṃ yatra varṇyate ।
prakhyātanāyakopetaṃ nāṭakaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।। arthataḥ śabdato vāpi manāk kāvyārthasūcanam ।। yatrāṣṭabhirdvādaśabhiraṣṭādaśabhireva vā ।। dvāviṃśatyā padairvāpi sā nāndī parikīrtitā ।।
nāṭakādirūpakāṇāmādau vihitaṃ padyaṃ nāndītyucyate । veṇīsaṃhāre aṣṭapadā nāndī । anargharāghave dvādaśapadā । bālarāmāyaṇe dvāviṃśatipadā ।
kaiścit nāndyāṃ padaniyamo nābhyupagataḥ । nāndyanantaraṃ praviṣṭena sūtradhāreṇa raṅgaprasādhanapuraḥ saraṃ bhāratīvṛttyāśrayaṇena ślokaiḥ kāvyārthaḥ sūcanīyaḥ । "raṅgaṃ prasādhya madhuraiḥ ślokaiḥ kāvyārthasūcakaiḥ । ṛtuṃ kaṃcidupādāya bhāratīṃ vṛttimāśrayet ।।
a; iti । eṣā prakriyā nāṭakasyaiva mukhyā । utpādyenetivṛttena dhīraśāntapradhānakam । śeṣaṃ nāṭakatulyāṅgaṃ bhavet prakaraṇaṃ hi tat ।।
bhāratīvṛttibhūyiṣṭhaṃ śauryasaubhāgyasaṃstavaiḥ । sūcyete vīraśṛṅgārau viṭena nipuṇoktinā ।। kalpitenetivṛttena dhūrtacāritravarṇanam । eko aṅko mukhanirvāhau yatra bhāṇaḥ sa saṃmataḥ ।।
yatra sandhyaṅgavṛttyaṅgavarṇanaṃ bhāṇavanmatam । hāsyo rasaḥ pradhānaṃ syādbhavet prahasanaṃ hi tat ।। tacca trividhamśuddhaṃ vaikṛtaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ ceti । pāṣaṇḍavipraprabhṛticeṭīceṭasamākulam ।
veṣabhāṣādisahitaṃ śuddhaṃ hāsyavaco anvitam ।। kāmukādivacoveṣaiḥ ṣaṇḍakañcukitāpasaiḥ । prahāsābhinayaprāyaṃ vaikṛtaṃ tat prakīrtyate ।। yad vīthyaṅgaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ dhūrtasaṃkulam ।।
yatra vastu prasiddhaṃ syād vṛttayaḥ vaiśikīṃ vinā । netāro devagandharvayakṣarakṣomahoragāḥ ।। bhūtapretapiśācādyāḥ ṣoḍaśātyantamuddhatāḥ । hāsyaśṛṅgārarahitā rasā raudrapradhānakāḥ ।।
catvāro aṅkāḥ saṃdhayaśca catvāro marśavarjitāḥ । māyendrajālasaṃgrāmasūryacandragrahādayaḥ ।। śeṣaṃ nāṭakavat sarvaṃ sa ḍimaḥ parikīrtyate ।। yatra khyātetivṛttaṃ syāduddhato nāyako mataḥ ।
garbhāvamarśarāhityaṃ ḍimavad rasapoṣaṇam । ekavāsarakāryaṃ ca sa vyāyogo mahāraṇaḥ ।। yatrāmukhaṃ nāṭakavat saṃdhayo marśavarjitāḥ । netāro dvādaśa pṛthakphalā devāsurādayaḥ ।।
vīrapradhānāśca rasāstrayo aṅkāsteṣu ca kramāt । vastusvabhāvadaivārikṛtāḥ syuḥ kapaṭāstrayaḥ ।। purarodharaṇāgnyādinimittā vidravāstrayaḥ । dharmārthakāmānuguṇāstisraḥ śṛṅgārarītayaḥ ।।
prathame aṅke nibaddhavyā kathā yāmatrayāvadhiḥ । yāmāvadhirdvitīye aṅke tṛtīye aṅke ardhayāmikā ।। asau samavakāraḥ syād vīthyaṅgaiḥ kaiścidanvitaḥ ।। yatra bhāṇavadaṅgānāṃ kḷptirvṛttistu kaiśikī ।।
śṛṅgāraḥ paripūrṇatvāt sūcanīyo atibhūyasā । uddhātyakādīnyaṅgāni sā vīthī vīthivanmatā ।। yatretivṛttaṃ prakhyātaṃ pradhānaṃ karuṇo rasaḥ । strīṇāṃ vilāso vāgyuddhaṃ netāraḥ prākṛtā narāḥ ।।
bhāṇavat saṃdhivṛttyādi sa utsṛṣṭo aṅkasaṃjñakaḥ ।। miśramīhāmṛge vṛttaṃ caturaṅkaṃ trisandhikam । martyadivyau ca niyamānnāyakapratināyakau ।। dhīroddhatau striyaṃ divyāṃ hartukāmau ca kāmukau ।
avadhaṃ yuddhamanyonyamābhāsarasayostayoḥ ।। eṣa prakriyā daśarūpakoktarītyanusāreṇa । nāṭakodāharaṇaprārambhaḥ । tatra sāṅgaṃ nāṭakamudāhriyate ।
śailairmeruhimācalaprabhṛtirbhirdevairharīndrādibhiḥ । sādhvībhiḥ śivayorapāṅgasaraṇirvaivāhikī pātu vaḥ ।। eṣā dvāviṃśatipadā nāndī । asyāṃ vivāhapravṛttayoḥ śivayoḥ varṇanayā sakalanarendraparikarasya pratāparudrasya kākatīyarājyalakṣmīprāptirnāṭakaprayojanarūpā kiṃcidarthaśaktyā sūcyate ।
deyāt siddhiṃ mahālakṣmīrjagadrakṣādhuraṃdharā । viṣṇuvakṣaḥ sphuranmālāvihitālayatoraṇā ।। eṣā ca nāndī pratāparudrarājyalakṣmīmaṅgalavidhilakṣaṇā । āviṣkurvanti murajāḥ sarvataḥ śabdamādhurīm ।
saṅgītopaniṣadvidyāṃ vīṇāḥ prastāvayantyamūḥ ।। etadraṅgaprasādhanam । bhūbhṛtsutāmahādevau pitarau yasya viśrutau । naranāgākṛtiḥ śrīmān sa devaḥ śreyase astu vaḥ ।।
cirādanukūlena kālenāpagatadurdināni diṅmukhāni । viharadrājahaṃsaśrīrvilasanmitramaṇḍalaḥ । prasādhayati sanmārgaṃ prasannaḥ śaradāgamaḥ ।। kāvyārthasūcakābhyāṃ ślokābhyāmṛtusamāśraṇena saṃskṛtaprāyanarāśritavāgvyavahārarūpā bhāratī vṛttiḥ kathitā ।
bho bho madhyamabhuvanabhāgadheyavivartasyaikaśilānagarapuṇyarāśeḥ kākatīyakuladevatāyāḥ svayambhūdevasya satatamahotsavamāsedivāṃso viddhāṃsaḥ ! kalārṇavanāṭyavedācāryasya putramabhinayadarpaṇaṃ māmabhimatarūpakaprayogānujñayā paramanugṛhṇīta । "yasmiñjaganmaṅgalamasti vastu yasmai svayaṃbhūḥ spṛhayatyajasram । tacchrotrayorlocanayoḥ pathāṃ naḥ śṛṅgāṭakaṃ nāṭakamāvirastu ।। a; iti ।
asmanmanorathasaṃvādyeva pariṣadādeśaḥ । yat pratāparudracaritānubandhaḥ prabandhaḥ sāmājikānāṃ manasi vartate । sabhā svayaṃbhūparameśvarasya pratāparudrasya guṇā mahārghāḥ । ahaṃ ca nāṭyaśrutipāradṛśvā sudhāmucastasya kaveśca vācaḥ ।।
eṣā praśaṃsayābhimukhīkaraṇarūpā bhāratīvṛtteraṅgaṃ prarocanā । kiṃ bhāraīe suvvai maṃjīraravo sahāe viharaṃtīe । aha saṃgīasui vvā viṇṇādaṃ ṇaṭṭappamuhatūraṇiṇāo ।। ( ।kiṃ bhāratyāḥ śrūyate mañjīraravaḥ sabhāyāṃ viharantyāḥ ।
atha saṃgītaśrutirvā vijñātaṃ nāṭyapramukhatūryaninādaḥ ।। aajja iamhi । āṇavedu ko ṇioo aṇuṭṭhīadu tti । (aārya iyamasmi ।
ājñāpayatu ko niyogo anuṣṭhīyatāmiti । ) lāsyaṃ cārubhiraṅgahāralalitairāviṣkariṣyāmi yat । prāgityuktavatī tadadya nipuṇe nirvyūḍhamevaṃ tvayā ।। etat priyasadṛśairapriyairvākyairupālambhanācchalam ।
naṭī aaṇaṭṭasāmaggiṃ sajjīkāduṃ vilaṃbiaṃ । sajjīkiā kkhu esā । keṇa uṇa ruvvaeṇa paoo uakkamīadu । (aanāṭyasāmagrīṃ sajjīkartuṃ vilambitam ।
sajjīkṛtā khalveṣā । kena punā rūpakeṇa prayoga upakramyatām । ) sūtradhāraḥnanvidameva rūpayatu । tejaḥ paryāyaharayoḥ kiṃ kiṃ saṃbodhanaṃ matam ।
kimāśīrvādaviṣayo vidyānāthakṛtiśca kā ।। samandasmitaṃ)aṇigūḍhatthaṃ khu edaṃ cheāṇaṃ vaaṇaṃ paḍibhādi । kīrisaṃ uttaraṃ ? ṇirūvedu ajjo । (anigūḍhārthaṃ khalvetacchekānāṃ vacanaṃ pratibhāti ।
kīdṛśamuttaram ? nirūpayatvāryaḥ । ) sūtradhāraḥayi suvyaktametat । eṣā nigūḍhārthā nālikā । naṭī ।
kahaṃ kahāṇāaaṇaāmaheāṇubaṃdhamaṇoharaṃ kkhu nāḍaam । paāvovavadaṃkiaṃ tassa raṇṇo ṇāma kahaṃ jāaṃ ti pucchīadi । ( ।kathaṃ kathānāyakanāmadheyānubandhamanoharaṃ khalu nāṭakam । pratāpopapadāṅkitaṃ tasya rājño nāma kathaṃ jātamiti pṛcchyate । )
sūtradhāraḥpriye śrūyatām । taṃ sujātaṃ samudvīkṣya kṣoṇyāṃ ravimivoditam । pratāparudra ityākhyāmakarot kākatīśvaraḥ ।। viṣṇorviśvaikavīrasya kākatīyakule sthitam ।
avatāramamuṃ jñātvā vīrarudraṃ pracakṣate ।। naṭīaloāṇaṃ kaṇṇajualasya bhāaheeṇa edaṃ ṇāmajualaṃ suṇīadi । cirassa ṇaṭṭavijjaṇuvaṭṭaṇaṃ phaliaṃ, jeṇa loamaṃgalaṃ kākaimariṃdacariaṃ abhiṇijjai । (alokānāṃ karṇayugalasya bhāgadheyena etannāmayugalaṃ śrūyate ।
cirasya nāṭyavidyānuvartanaṃ phalitaṃ, yena lokamaṅgalaṃ kākatinarendracaritamabhinīyate ।। etannāṭyaprasaṅgena prakṛtakāryāvalaganādavalagitaṃ dvitīyam । sūtradhāraḥaho prajñāsaṃvādo ayamāyuṣmatyāḥ, yadiyaṃ kavīnāṃ praśnottaramālikā । kiṃ lokaśravasorbhāgyaṃ maṅgalaśravaṇaṃ muhuḥ ।
kiṃ maṅgalaṃ pratāpāṅkarudrasya caritādbhutam ।। etatpraśno ttaramālārūpamuddhātyakam । naṭī । ayyapariaṇeṇa savvaṃ saṃpaddīadi ।
( । āryaparijanena sarvaṃ saṃpādyate । ) tvayā dārairudāraśrīrnāṭyasaṃpadiyaṃ mama । prabandhalakṣmī rītyeva vidarbhaphaṇitispṛśā ।।
eṣa mithaḥ stotrarūpaḥ prapañcaḥ । naṭī ।। eārisaguṇamahagghapaāvaruddacariaṃ ahikariaṃto tassa kaiṇo saṃpuṇṇo sarassaīpasādo । sūtradhāraḥārye, evameva ।
nanveṣā kavibhāratyorvākkeliḥ । jihvā kākativīrarudranṛpateḥ stotrāya saṃnahyati । tvaṅganmaulitaraṅgiṇīkalakalārambhapriyaṃbhāvukāḥ ।। eṣānyonyasaṃlāparūpā vākkeliḥ ।
naṭī । amhāṇaṃ īrimaṇariṃdacariāṇuūlo ṇaṭṭāḍaṃbaro hoi ṇa ve tti sajjhaseṇa vevai me hiaam । ( । asmākamīdṛśanarendracaritānukūlo nāṭyāḍambaro bhavati na veti sādhvasena vepate me hṛdayam । )
sūtradhāraḥ āḥ kimucyate ! niravadyā nanu mannāṭyavidyāsāmagrī । naṭīasaṃgīdasārassa mahaṇṇavo uvvellijjadi । avahāṇajāṇapattaṃ ārūhadu ajjo । (asaṃgītasārasya mahārṇava udvelyate ।
avadhānayānapātramārohatvāryaḥ । ) etadanyonyavākyādhikyādadhibalam । sūtradhāraḥciramavahita evāsmi । naṭakṛtadhruvāgānapratijñāvacanaṃ saṃbhramoditamiti gaṇḍam ।
naṭī । sūtradhāraḥayi kathamardhokta eva tvarā, "nāṭyavidyā'; iti śeṣaṃ na jighrati । etaduktasyānyathāyojanarūpamavasyanditam । ārye, nūnaṃ dhruvāgānotsukaṃ tava cetaḥ, tadārabhyatāṃ gītiḥ ।
lacchī saraī a imā dhavaliabhuvaṇaṃtarā virāaṃtī । vilasaṃtakuvalaasirī rāassa pasāhaṇaṃ kuṇai ।। (lakṣmīḥ sarasī ceyaṃ dhavalitabhuvanāntarā virājantī । vilasatkuvalayaśrī rājñaḥ prasādhanaṃ kurute ।।
gāḍhāliṅganasaṃmardapratyakṣaragalatsudhām । dhruvāṃ karomi sarvāṅge śrotraikāmṛtavarṣiṇīm ।। eṣa rasavaśādasaṃgatārthavyāhārarūpo asatpralāpaḥ । naṭī asuumārā kkhu esā ayyassa ṇiddaāliṅgaṇavellaṇaṃ ṇa sahai ।
eṣa hāsyalobhakaro vyāhāraḥ । rasāsvādena taralā ye mādyanti vipaścitaḥ । ta eva bhāvuktā loke bhavanti hṛdayālavaḥ ।। etaddoṣasya guṇatvāropānmṛdavam ।
naṭī ।। ayyo aṇaṃtarakaraṇijjaṃ ṇirūvedu । sūtradhāraḥnanvayamidānīṃ sabhāpatirdevaḥ svayaṃbhūrupaślokyate । sarvāṅgavilastasarvamaṅgalālaṃkṛtākṛteḥ ।
rudrasya mahimā bhāti viśvānugrahakāriṇaḥ ।। nepathye । bhoḥ ! satyaṃ satyam । sarvāṅgavilasatsarvamaṅgalālaṃkṛtākṛtirevāyaṃ rudra iti ।
sūtradhāraḥ kathamupakrāntamevāsmadvākyānuguṇyena prastutasyānuguṇaṃ kuśalaiḥ kuśīlavaiḥ, yataḥ kākatīśvaraguṇavarṇanāyodyatayorvaitālikayorvacanamivopakṣipyate । ayaṃ kathoddhātaḥ । idameva guṇavarṇanāt pravartakaṃ ca । kathametau vaitālikāvita evābhivartete ।
eṣo ayamityupakṣepāt prayogātiśayaḥ prastāvanāṅgam । tadehi । āvāmapyanantarakaraṇīyāya sajjībhavāvaḥ । iti samagrāṅgā prastāvanā ।
yasmai śreyāṃsyajasraṃ vitarati bhagavān devadevaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ । so ayaṃ bhūpālamaulirjayati guṇamahān rudradevo narendraḥ ।। svayaṃbhūdevaśreyovitaraṇarūpabījanyāsādupakṣepo aṅgam । so ayaṃ saṃprati kākatīśvarakule sarvāṅganārī sthitaḥ ।
nyāsan vairipurāṇi citramadhunā khaḍge viṣaṃ dhāryate ।। prathamaḥsakhe sādhu samarthitam । anyathā kathamasmai mahārājāya svapne kulagurusadṛśaḥ svayaṃbhūdevastādṛśīṃ śreyaḥ saṃgrahakārikāmupadiṣṭavān । svayaṃbhūdevaprasādarūpasya bījasya bahūkaraṇāt parikaraḥ ।
prathamaḥsakhe, kasya vā na viditamidam । yat sarvasminnapi nijanagare mahotsavamādiśatā rudranareśvareṇa kuladevatāyāḥ svapnopadiṣṭāḥ prasādaviśeṣāḥ prakhyāpyanta eva । kuladevatāprasādarūpasya bījasya prakhyāpanena pariniṣpatteḥ parinyāsaḥ । dvitīyaḥaho nirantaraprasādonmukhatā devasya ।
yathā kākatīyaprasaveṣu śreyāṃsyuttarottaramanubadhyante । etat bījasya śreyo anubandharūpaguṇakhyāpanād vilobhanam । tadasminneva mahīyasi mahe mahīmaṇḍalākhaṇḍalaṃ calamartigaṇḍamupaślokayitumāvayorayamevāvasaraḥ । tadehi rājakulaṃ praviśāvaḥ ।
prathamaḥvayasya, sāṃprataṃ purodhaḥ pramukhānamātyavṛddhānapi puraskṛtya kalyāṇasvapnakramaṃ mīmāṃsamāno nṛpatirabhyantarāsthānīmadhitiṣṭhati । tadāvāmapi tāvadito gatvā yathāvasaraṃ pratīkṣāvahe । aṅkārambhaḥ ।। pātivratyamupaiti sāṃpratamamīṣvasmāsu viśvaṃbharā ।
yatkartavyamupādiśat kulapatirdevaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ svayam ।। purodhasaḥmahārāja, bhavādṛśā eva paramārhanti tādṛśamahimno devasya hitopadeśān । athavā kimatrābhinavam । putrāṇāṃ hitopadeśādhikāraḥ pitureva ।
yaditthaṃ kathayanti tadvidaḥ । saivomā ceti nirdiṣṭā somā ceti prathāmagāt । tava mātā śivā sākṣāddevo gaṇapatiḥ pitā ।। mantriṇaḥevamevaitat ।
anyathā kathamīśvaraprasādādṛte niraṅkuśaṃ strīvyaktiviśeṣasya lokādhipatyam । evaṃ mānuṣaśaṃbhunā gaṇapatimahārājenābhyantarasyānubhavamahimnaḥ sadṛśamatra putra iti vyavahāraḥ kṛtaḥ । tadanuguṇā ca rudra ityākhyā । rājā idaṃ nivedyate ।
puraḥ prādurbhūtaṃ sayuvativapuḥ sākṣaniṭilam । svayaṃbhūdevo asāvayamiti haṭhotthānamabhajam ।। vapuṣā taṃ namaskṛtya stuvan sūnṛtayā girā । svāmine kākatīyānāṃ ratnāsanamupāharam ।।
cāmaragrāhiṇī । aho devassa aṇusaṃdhāṇaṃ jaṃ siviṇe vi kulasāmiṇo samārāhaṇam । purodhasaḥkimucyate । āviṣṭabhaktayaḥ khalu svayaṃbhūdeve kākatīyanaradevāḥ ।
tataḥ । śayyāśiraḥ sthānakṛtasya pūrṇakumbhasya toyaiḥ parikalpya pādyam । atīndusārairmaṇibhiḥ kilāhamapūjayaṃ daivatamasmadīyam ।। vibhuḥ svayaṃbhūravadacchucismitāṃ giraṃ svavāmārdhavadhūpalālitām ।
spṛśan kareṇābhayadānaśālinā kṛtāñjaliṃ māṃ vinayānatānanam ।। unmastakairmadhyamalokabhāgyaistapoviśeṣairanaghaiḥ pṛthivyāḥ । samyakphalaiḥ saccaritaiḥ prajānāṃ pratāparudro ayamihāvatīrṇaḥ ।। svīkṛte putrabhāvena dauhitre prāṅmamājñayā ।
asmin nidhehi dhaureye gurvīmurvīdhurāmiti ।। purodhasaḥ mahārāja, kākatīyakulayogakṣemavidhānadakṣiṇena dākṣāyaṇīpatinā sākṣādevamādiṣṭam । tavāpyayameva manorathaḥ । priyaṃkaraścāyaṃ mahotsavaḥ prajānām ।
tadārohatu prāgatisṛṣṭayauvarājyasya pratāparudrasya bhujaśikharaṃ sāgaramekhalā । tatastataḥ । iyaṃ prayojananirdhāraṇarūpā yuktiḥ । rājātadvacanamākarṇayantī nirbharaharṣavikasvaralocanā medinyapi devasya pārśve dṛṣṭā ।
cāmaragrāhiṇī । mahārāassa hiaaṃ aṇuvaṭṭamāṇāe vasuṃdharāe uido khkhu harisāvibhbhāvo । eṣā svayaṃbhūdevasya vacanākarṇanena medinyāḥ sukhāgamena prāptiḥ । rājākākatīyakulaśreyasāṃ deva eva pramāṇamiti tasyājñā mayā śirasi dhṛtā ।
devo api saprasādātiśayamavalokyāntarhito abhūt । idaṃ medinīprāptihetorbījasya svayaṃbhūdevopadeśasyāṅgīkaraṇāt samādhānam । mantriṇaḥviśvapriyaṃkaraḥ svapnapratyayaḥ । viṣādaharṣayoḥ sīmānaṃ spṛśatyasmākaṃ manaḥ ।
etatsukhaduḥ khahetubhūtaṃ vidhānam । cāmaragrāhiṇī । accariaṃ accariaṃ । kulāmaccamuheṇevva pavvaīvallaheṇa evvamuvadiṭṭham ।
( । āścaryamāścaryam । kulāmātyamukheneva pārvatīvallabhenaivamupadiṣṭam । ) iyaṃ bījaviṣayā'ścaryarūpā paribhāvanā ।
kalpalatāprarohaḥ svayaṃbhūdevānugrahaḥ sarveṣāmapi śravaṇamahotsavaḥ kriyatām । eṣa bījaprakāśanādudbhedaḥ । mantriṇaḥyadājñāpayati kākatīyaparameśvaraḥ । purodhasaḥmahārāja ! kimanyat ? sajjīkriyatāṃ pratāparudradevasya rājyābhiṣekasaṃbhāraḥ ।
eṣa bījānuguṇaprotsāhanarūpo bhedaḥ । mantriṇaḥdigvijayayātrāvaśīkṛtānāṃ sarvapārthivānāṃ vargeṇānītaiḥ sakalatīrthasalilaiḥ prakāśitaṃ svayaṃbhūdevaprasādaṃ mahābhiṣekamanubhavatu rājaputraḥ । purodhasaḥucitamanumantritaṃ mantribhiḥ । rājātarhi jaitrayātrāsādhanāni sajjīkriyantāṃ ṣaḍvidhāni balāni ।
ahamapi sajjo bhavāmi । eṣa ārambhaḥ । idaṃ bījānuguṇārambharūpaṃ karaṇam । evamārambhabījasambandharūpaḥ sāṅgo mukhasandhiḥ ।
vaitālikausukhāya mādhyandinī saṃdhyā bhavatu devasya । tvattejaḥ paṭalaṃ kiyanti bhuvanānyākramya saṃkrīḍate । bhāsvāneṣa samagradīptiradhunā vyomāgramārohati ।। krīḍantyo malayādricandanalatākuñje bhujaṅgāṅganāḥ ।
vātāhāratayā prabhūtamayaśaḥ prakṣālayantyo nijam ।। āghrāya kiraṇān bhānoryajurāmodamedurān । yatante kṛtinaḥ sarve kartuṃ mādhyāhnikīṃ kriyām ।। rājā sādhayata yūyamabhimatācaraṇāya ।
ahamapi tāvadabhyantaraṃ praviśāmi । iti nāṭakaprakaraṇe kalyāṇasvapno nāma prathamoṅkaḥ ।। nepathye) । ido ido ajjo ।
( । ita ita āryaḥ । ) kañcukī cirāya yauvanamatiśayānayā caritārthayā jarayānayā saṃcare । pratāparudramahābhiṣekamanubhavitāsmi ।
eṣa madhyāhnavarṇanayā vicchinnasya prakṛtārthasya punaravamarśādbinduḥ । pade pade skhalantaṃ māṃ vācā gatyātha ceṣṭayā । avalokya hasannāste svāmī rudranareśvaraḥ ।। kākatīyanarendrasya rājyaśrīrmūlaveśmanaḥ ।
yuvarājagṛhānadya gavākṣaiḥ svairamīkṣate ।। eṣa rājyalakṣmyāḥ pratāparudragatābhilāpādvilāsaḥ । kathamayaṃ rājaputraparicārako dārakaḥ sasaṃbhramaṃ māmabhivartate । dārakaḥ ।
ayya paṇamāmi । ( । ārtha praṇamāmi । ) kañcukībhadra kalyāṇāspadaṃ bhūyāḥ ।
kimanumataṃ rājaputrasya digvijayaprasthānaṃ rudranareśvareṇa । dārakaḥakahaṃ kahaṃ vi aṇubhadam । kañcukīsvanāmānuguṇamidaṃ rājaputrasya yat sajjīkṛtasādhanaṃ mahārājaṃ sapādopagrahaṃ nivārya svayameva jaitrayātrāyāmuttiṣṭhate । dārakaḥaaayya aṇaṇuhūdajujhjhaparissamo juvarāo ।
dukkharo khu diaṃtajao kahaṃ bhavissai । (aaārya, ananubhūtayuddhapariśramo yuvarājaḥ । duṣkaraḥ khulu digantajayaḥ kathaṃ bhaviṣyati । ) kañcukībhadra, niraṅkuśāḥ svayaṃbhūdevapravṛttayaḥ ।
viṣṇoravatāraḥ khalvayaṃ vīrarudro api acintyamahimā । eṣa dṛṣṭanaṣṭabījānusaraṇarūpaḥ parisarpaḥ । atra svapnavṛttāntakhyāpanāllakṣyasya digvijayayātrodyamenālakṣyasya bījasyotpādanādudbheda iti pratimukhasaṃdhirayam । dārakaḥ ।
evvaṃ edam । amāṇuso khu so pahāvo । ( । evametat ।
amānuṣaḥ khalu sa prabhāvaḥ । ) dārakaḥakāaīakuladuggādevīsamārāhaṇeṇa viaapatthāṇamaṃgalaṃ kāūṇa tattha haṇumadaalaperaṃtabahirujjāṇe ṇivesiakhaṃdhāvāro amaccaparivudo juvarāo ciṭṭhaī । tā aṇujāṇīhi mama tattha patthāṇaṃ । (akākatīyakuladurgādevīsamārādhanena vijayaprasthānamaṅgalaṃ kṛtvā tatra hanumadacalaparyantabahirudyāne niveśitaskandhāvāraḥ amātyaparivṛto yuvarājastiṣṭhati ।
tadanujānīhi mama tatra prasthānam । ) kañcukībhadra ! sādhaya । ahamapi rājakulaṃ praviśāmi । iyaṃ cūlikā ।
kiṃ cāsmin samudāharanti mahato doṣān bahūn sūrayaḥ । tanneṣṭaṃ kila yauvarājyamapi me bālyotsave krīḍataḥ ।। tadvayaṃ mahārājabhujaparighamasṛṇiteṣu diganteṣu vijayayātrāvinodena viharāmahe । etadrājye anicchābhidhānādvidhūtam ।
mantriṇaḥrājaputra ! sarvapathīnayā kākatīyānvayabhāgyasaṃpadā tvāṃ dhuraṃdhuraṃ labdhvā narendraściramāsaktāṃ dhuraṃ śithilayitumadhyavasyati । ācāraścāyaṃ kākatīśvarāṇāṃ yaddhaureye putre śamonmukhatvam । kulasvāminā svayaṃbhuvāpyevamevānuśiṣṭam । anatikramaṇīyā rājaputreṇa gurvorgarīyasī khalvājñā ।
kalikāladoṣaśithiladharmapratiṣṭhāṃ nirvoḍhuṃ voḍhuṃ ca mahatīṃ mahīdhuramavatīrṇasya kākatīyaviṣṇostava na sāṃprataṃ pratyākhyātum । svayaṃbhūstāta ityetāvīśvarau divyamānuṣau । tayoranyataro rājā yuvarājo asmi sarvathā ।। mantriṇaḥrājaputra ! sādhāraṇo ayaṃ vinayaḥ kākatīśvarāṇāṃ svayaṃbhuvi mahārāje ca ।
eṣa prakṛtaviṣayāratyupaśamācchamaḥ । parijanaḥ । kāaīakulaṭṭhaviro tattabhavaṃto saaṃbhūdevo dhuraṃ dhāredu । rāautto uṇa rajjasiriaṃ aṃke ārovedu ।
(kākatīyakulasthavirastatrabhavān svayaṃbhūdevo dhuraṃ dhārayatu । rājaputraḥ punā rājyaśriyamaṅke āropayatu । ) etat parihāsavacorūpaṃ narma । parijanaḥacireṇa cariatthā meiṇī saṃvuttā ।
(acireṇa caritārthā medinī saṃvṛttā । gotragiriśikharaniṣṭhuravikaṭaśilāvasatibarbarāṅgyāḥ । kṣoṇyā bhavatu vāso bāhau pratāparudrasya ।। gottagirisiharāṇiṭhṭhuraviaḍasilāvasaibabbaraṃgīe ।
khoṇīe hodu vāso bāhummi paāvaruddassa ।। ajaha haricaṃdassa bhue jaha rahuṇāhassa bāhuphalaammi । kāailacchīpaiṇo bāhummi tahā mahī ramadu ।। (ayathā hariścandrasya bhuje yathā raghunāthasya bāhuphalake ।
kākatilakṣmīpaterbāhau tathā mahī ramatām ।। eṣā parijanavacanotthā prītirnarmadyutiḥ । mantriṇaḥrājaputra ! kākatīyapuruṣottamasya tava pāṇigrahaṇāya spṛhayantī rājyalakṣmīrvilambaṃ na sahate । parijanaḥ ।
vijjāvahūṇaṃ ahiaṃ daṭhṭhūṇa paimmi paṇaavissaṃbhaṃ । khoṇī lacchī a kahaṃ vilaṃbiaṃ sahau juvarāe ।। (vidyāvadhūnāmadhikaṃ dṛṣṭravā patyau praṇayavisrambham । kṣoṇī lakṣmīśca kathaṃ vilambitaṃ sahatāṃ yuvarāje) ।।
mantriṇaḥitthameva । svatejasā pariṣkṛtya pradhānāgāramutsukā । pratīkṣate adya rājyaśrīryuvarājasamāgamam ।। eṣa mantriṇāṃ parijanasya ca vākyairbījānurāgaprakāśanāt pragamaḥ ।
paridṛ ।। kahaṃ aṃdario khu eso mahūsao disāvijaajattāe । ( ।। kathamantaritaḥ khalveṣa mahotsavo digvijayayātrayā । )
etaddigantayātrayā prakṛtakāryavilambanānnirodhaḥ । mantriṇaḥ kathaṃ cirayantyandhracamūpatayaḥ । athavā kiṃ taiḥ; vayamapi na kevalaṃ mantraśastrāḥ, kiṃtu bahuśaḥ samarāpadānārādhitasvāmina eva । etanniṣṭhuravacanarūpaṃ vajram ।
dauvārikaḥ । jedu jedu juaroo । ede khu camūpaiṇo paḍihārabhūmibhāammi sajjīkiacauraṃgabalā vaṭṭanti । ( ।
jayatu jayatu yuvarājaḥ । ete khalu camūpatayaḥ pratīhārabhūmibhāge sajjīkṛtacaturaṅgabalā vartante । ) mantriṇaḥaciraṃ bhoḥ praveśaya । dauvārikaḥtathā ।
senāpatayaḥ svāmin kākatīyakulatilaka ! sarvatomukhāṭopā vāhinyaḥ śauryodanvantaṃ bhavantamanuprāptā eva । tadanugṛhayālunā kaṭākṣeṇa nirīkṣyantām । etadanunayavacanarūpaṃ paryupāsanam । mantriṇaḥrājaputra ! tarhi samāruhyatāṃ pratipakṣanivāraṇo vāraṇaḥ ।
ālokyantāṃ nirantaraparipanthipramāthinyo varūthinyaḥ । prastūyatāṃ senāpuraḥ-sarākrāntasakalasāmantavijayasthānaṃ prasthānam । pratāparudraḥyathābhirucitamamātyebhyaḥ । karodagreṇa mahasā viṣvagākramituṃ diśaḥ ।
ārohati gajaṃ vīrarudro bhāsvānivodayam ।। etat prakṛtānuguṇyena viśeṣabandhavacanaṃ puṣpam । senāpatayaḥ svāminnito dīyatāṃ dṛṣṭiḥ । dhūlījālāmbudāntarvilasadasilatāvidyududdāmadīptāḥ ।
prāvṛṭlakṣmīṃ dhvajinyaḥ karikaraṭataṭasyandidānāmbudhārāḥ ।। purandaraharijjayavyavasitāḥ sahāyoddhatāḥ । bharāvanamadunnamadbhujagarājaphakkatphaṇāḥ ।। parijanaḥ ।
mahaṃto khu eso tiliṅgasubhaḍāṇaṃ ussāho । ( । mahān khalveṣa triliṅgasubhaṭānāmutsāhaḥ । ) svairodgīrṇabhusuṇḍhayaḥ paṭutarākṛṣṭadhvanatkārmukāḥ ।
khelantyandhracamūbhaṭāḥ savapuṣo raudraprakārā iva ।। mantriṇaḥaho turaṅgataraṅgāstriliṅgādhipateḥ । pāścāttyābhyāṃ padābhyāmapi dharaṇimavaṣṭabhya saṃrabdhanunnām । krāmantyaśvāḥ sahelakramaṇapariṇamatpañcadhārāprapañcāḥ ।।
aho vidalitaparabalamanorathānāṃ rathānāṃ sabhraṃmaḥ । kṣamātalasamuccaladbahuladhūlijālāmbudaiḥ । vidhāya mukharībhavantyanibhṛtākṣadhūrnisvanāḥ ।। pratāparudraḥ kathaṃ samagrasādhanāni sainyāni ।
bṛṃhamāṇagajākīrṇā hreṣamāṇahayākulāḥ । saṃkrīḍatsyandanāḥ kṣveḍasubhaṭāḥ sainyasaṃpadaḥ ।। mantriṇaḥyuvarājālokanādudvelaḥ sainyasāgaro vartate । abhyāpatantīrabhito mahībhṛdvāhinīrbahūḥ ।
kākatīyabalāmbhodhireṣa svairaṃ grasiṣyate ।। senāpatayaḥyadādiśantyamātyāḥ । vijayayātrākutūhalinyo dhvajinyaḥ sāṃprataṃ yuvarājasyājñāṃ pratipālayanti । mantriṇaḥ pratiṣṭhantāṃ prācīṃ prati sainyāni ।
senāpatayaḥyathā'diśantyamātyāḥ । pavanenānukūlena prasāritapaṭāñcalāḥ । udyuñjanta ivākraṣṭuṃ dhvajāḥ sautrāmaṇīṃ diśam ।। eṣa prasthānānuguṇaśakunaguṇakathanādupanyāsaḥ ।
pratāparudraḥ kathaṃ karābhyāmutkṣiptasākṣatakanakapātraḥ samāgata eva vipravaraḥ । vipraḥ vijayatāṃ vijayatāṃ vīrarudraḥ । rājaputra ! svayaṃbhūdevamahotsavādyanantaraṃ mahīsuravarāśīrvādavāsitāḥ kākatīyamahārājena preṣitāḥ khalvime maṅgalākṣatāḥ । ājñā kṣatriyamaulimaṇḍanamaṇestātasya sānugrahā ।
paurāṇāṃ ca jayottarāṇi tadamūrīṣajjayāḥ syurdiśaḥ ।। eṣa brāhmaṇakṣatriyādivarṇakīrtanādvarṇasaṃhāraḥ । mantriṇaḥrājaputra ! svabhāvanirargalasya tava bhujārgalayorojāyitasya kiyatī bhūtalavijayaviḍambanā । parijanaḥ ।
viaalacchīpāṇiggahaṇasamaadiṇṇā via maṅgalakhkhadā juvarāassa sīse dīsaṃdi । vipraḥrājaputra ! tattaddigvijayayātrāvārtāhāriṇaḥ puruṣā nāticirādeva preṣaṇīyā iti mahārājasyājñā । pratāparudraḥśirasi kṛtastātasya niyogaḥ । katicana yūyaṃ kākatīśvarasevārthaṃ nivartadhvam ।
katipaye vijayayātrāparāḥ pravartadhvam । amātyāḥ yadājñāpayati yuvarājaḥ । vipraḥsvasti vijayāya śivāḥ panthānaḥ santu rājaputrāya । pratāparudraḥ bhagavannanujānīhi ।
vayamitaḥ pratiṣṭhāmahe । ।। iti vijayayātrāvilāso nāma dvitīyo aṅkaḥ ।। etatpūrvāṅkāntapātreṇa vipreṇa nirdiṣṭayoḥ pātrayoruttarāṅke praveśādaṅkāsyam । prathamaḥ aho pratāparudrasya mahimānubhāvaḥ, yasya vijayayātrāsaṃbhrameṇaiva vyākulīkṛtāni dvayeṣāmapi bhūbhṛtāṃ kaṭakāni ।
kākatīyapradīpo ayamaṃśaścāturbhujaḥ svayam । yadvajrakavacāyante prasādāśca svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। eṣa svayaṃbhūdevaprasādarūpasya bījasyānveṣaṇād garbhasandhiḥ । prathamaḥ prāpteyamandhranagarī ।
aho ! niratiśayamaudāryaṃ rudranareśvarasya । yadete vaitālikāḥ sarvāto bhogāvalīpramukhāṃścāṭuprabandhānuccaiḥ paṭhantaḥ svabhāvaramaṇīyāḥ pratiraveṇa pāṭhayanti ca kakubhaḥ । dvitīyaḥ sakhe ! paśya paśya । sūcyante prabhutārahasyapiśunairāviṣkṛtailakṣaṇaiḥ ।
ākāraraimanuṣyamātrasulabhairvṛttairanīcairapi ।। prathamaḥnūnamete pratāparudrasamaraparāṅmukhā vakṣaḥ sthalaviracitavarāhalakṣmāṇaḥ prāṇatrāṇārthamanayā rītyā kākatīyamahārājaṃ prasādayitumadhyavasyantīti tarkayāmi । etat prastutopayogipratirājacchadmācaraṇādabhūtāharaṇam । jāṅghikena punastaistairlakṣaṇairnareśvarābhyūhanādanumānaṃ ca ।
dvitīyaḥaho ! vijayayātrāśravaṇakutūhalitā paurāṇām, yadāvāmanusaranti punaḥ punaḥ praśramālayā । tat sakhe ! prakāśyatāṃ pratāparudrasya bhujayorvijayodāharaṇam । prathamaḥ bho bhoḥ ! śrūyatāṃ kākatīyakulaślāghākāmadhenuḥ priyodantaḥ । kṣmāpālāḥ karadīkṛtāḥ kṛtamidaṃ nirvīramurvītalam ।
mañjīradhvanipūrṇakandaramukhairvyākurvate parvatāḥ ।। eṣa tattvānukīrtanarūpo mārgaḥ । dvitīyaḥsakhe ! nūnameṣu divaseṣu kākatīyamahārājo nirantaraṃ puraskṛtapurodhaḥ pravarāmātyavṛddho yuvarājavijayamāśaṃsamāno gamayati vāsarāṇi । prathamaḥucitamanucintitaṃ vayasyena ।
dvitīyaḥ kathamasmadīyaṃ vacanamākarṇya nūnaṃ mahārājāya nivedayitumamātyaputraḥ saharṣasaṃbhramaṃ rājakulābhyantaraṃ praviśati । tadāvāmapi pratīhārabhūmimadhyāsya kākatīśvarāvasaraṃ pratipālayiṣyāvaḥ । parikrāmataḥ । ) etad vitarkapratipādanādrūpam ।
amātyaputraḥ aho mama dhanyatā, yadīdṛśānāṃ mahotsavānāṃ nivedayitāsmi saṃvṛttaḥ । yanmayā vijñāpitaiḥ śravaṇapriyaṃkaraṇairvārtāmṛtaiḥ svapnasākṣātkṛtādapi svayaṃbhūdevaprasādāt pramodayiṣyate kākatīyavṛṣā । eṣotkarṣavacanarūpodāhṛtiḥ । kathamayaṃ mahārājaḥ purohitairamātyairanyena parijanena ca parivṛto mahāsthānamaṇṭapamadhitiṣṭhati ।
tadahamupasarpāmi । rājā aho śaiśave apyucitakāritvaṃ vatsasya vīrarudrasya । yadasmadanurodhārthamimānamātyān nivartya svayameva jigīṣuḥ prasthitaḥ । mantriṇaḥ mahārāja ! bhavatā khalu pitṛmān kumāraḥ ।
purodhasaḥvijayaprasthānātprabhṛti naktaṃdivamunmiṣanti kalyāṇāni । tadvijitā eva diśo rājaputreṇa । rājābhavatāmāśiṣa eva kākatīyakulaśreyāṃsi svayaṃ praduhate । parijanaḥ ।
kāaīakulassa kiṃ ṇu ṇa saṃpuṇṇaṃ puṇṇeṇa, jassiṃ avaiṇṇo bhuvaṇekkabhaddo paāvaruddo । amātyaputraḥ(savinayasaṃbhramamupasṛtya sapraṇāmaṃ deva madhyamalokapāla ! yuvarājapraṣretau vijayavārtāhāriṇau praghāṇaprāṅgaṇamadhivasataḥ । eṣa saṃcintyamānārthaprāptirūpaḥ kramaḥ । mantriṇaḥbhadra ! śīghraṃ praveśaya ।
amātyaputraḥyadādiśanti mahāmantriṇaḥ । puruṣau deva ! viśvaikavijayinā putreṇa vardhase । bāḍhamaprameyamahimā pratāparudrabhujasthemā, yacchaiśave apyatiśayitataruṇakākatīyaparākramastasya vikramaḥ । rājā manorathābhyāmiva cintitopagatābhyāṃ mahārghaṃ pāritoṣikaṃ pratipādyatām ।
dviguṇīkṛtaharṣayoranayormukhādvatsasya vijayalakṣmīparigrahavṛttāntaśravaṇamahotsavena caritārthayāmaḥ śrotravṛttim । mantriṇaḥyadājñāpayati devaḥ । eṣa sāmadānācaraṇarūpaḥ saṃgrahaḥ । mantriṇaḥbhadrāvita etya yuvarājavijayavihṛtayaḥ parākramapallavitā mahārājasadasaḥ karṇapūrīkriyantām ।
puruṣausāvadhānamavadhārayatu mahārājaḥ । kṣuṇṇakṣoṇitalotthite atibahule pāṃsau viyadvyāpini । trāsāt kvāpi palāyitā iva dṛśāṃ naivābhavan gocarāḥ ।। nedaṃ dundubhigarjitaṃ tripurajitkalpāntaḍhakkāravaḥ ।
ccheṣāśeṣaphaṇāsu vismitamatha trastaṃ digīśairapi ।। purodhasaḥaho niraṅkuśamojāyitamandhracamūpatīnām । dvitīyaḥatha yuvarājājñayā prathamaṃ māghavanīṃ diśaṃ pracalitāni sainyāni । rathenābhimukhyātaṃ vīrarudro vilokya mām ।
mṛṣyate nāyamityarkaḥ sainyareṇau tirohitaḥ ।। mantriṇaḥtatastataḥ । yuddhāya samanahyanta kaliṅgāḥ sphuṭapauruṣāḥ । mādyaddvipaghaṭoddāmasaṃbhramāḍambaroddhatāḥ ।।
matto mastiṣkalagnairdalitanṛpavapuḥ kīkasaiḥ sṛṣṭadaṃṣṭraḥ । saṃgrāmorvyāḥ kaliṅgairbalividhimakarodvīrarudrasya khaṅgaḥ ।। purodhasaḥmānuṣaveṣatirohitenāpi kākatīyaviṣṇunā kiṃcidāviṣkṛto nijaprabhāvaḥ । mantriṇaḥ aho parākramātibhūmiḥ pratāparudrasya ।
parijanaḥ । sarisaṃ khu edaṃ, jaṃ mahārāaruddaṇaresaraṇaṃdaṇeṇa kādavvaṃ, jaṃ kāaikulappasavāṇaṃ khamaṃ, jaṃ kuladevadāe saaṃbhūdevassa ppasattivisesāṇaṃ juttaṃ, taṃ khu kiaṃ juvarāeṇa । ( । sadṛśaṃ khalvetatyanmahārājarudranareśvaranandanena kartavyaṃ, yat kākatikulaprasavānāṃ kṣamaṃ, yat kuladevatāyāḥ svayaṃbhūdevasya prasattiviśeṣāṇāṃ yuktaṃ, tat khalu kṛtaṃ yuvarājena । )
rājā tatastataḥ । bhrāntibhraśyatpataṅgābhayakarapṛtanāreṇubaddhāndhakārā । prodyanmuktaughatārānikaraparivṛtasvarvadhūvaktracandrā ।। pārepūrvapayodhi kalpitajayastambhāḥ sphurattejasaḥ ।
śṛṇvanto muhurandhrasainyapatayaḥ prāptā diśaṃ dakṣiṇām ।। bhavantyetā nadyaḥ kaluṣapayasaḥ sainyarajasā । patākāḥ sotprāsāḥ pratipadamanṛtyannatitarām ।। anantaraṃ pāṇḍyapramukhān dākṣiṇātyān kṣitīśvarān śaraṇamupagatān kākatīyavīrarudraḥ svacamūpatinirviśeṣaṃ saṃbhāvya taiḥ saha pratīcīṃ diśaṃ pracalitaḥ ।
mantriṇaḥsādhu sādhu samācaritamātmanīnaṃ pāṇḍyairyat pūrvameva devasya caraṇamūlaṃ prāptāḥ । tatastataḥ । vrātairyaccaṇḍatuṇḍāhativihatapaṭeṣvāhatakṣiptapakṣaiḥ । praṣṭhānāṃ janyamanyannijanibiḍabhujādaṇḍakaṇḍūviḍambaḥ ।।
jitvā pratīcīmatha vīrarudraḥ pratyarthinārīnayanāmbupūrṇām । revāṃ samuttīrya gajānubaddhasetuṃ vijetuṃ gatavānudīcīm ।। tatrāṅgavaṅgakaliṅgamālavaprabhṛtayaḥ sarve bhūpālā militvā yuddhāya baddhādarāḥ purataḥ prādurabhavan । mantriṇaḥaho paramanātmaveditodīcyānāṃ yatpratāparudrasyāpi paripanthino bhavanti ।
rājātatastataḥ । vaṅga ! tvaṅgasi kiṃ mudhā balarajaḥ kāṇo asi kiṃ koṅkaṇa ! । yoddhāro vayamityarīnabhibhavantyandhrakṣamābhṛdbhaṭāḥ ।। ।।
etadroṣasaṃrabdhavacanarūpaṃ toṭakam । parijanaḥ ।। sāhu sāhu camūvariṇaṃ vaaṇaṃ । evvaṃ phaṇiā uṇa kīrisaṃ uvakkaṃdaṃ tehiṃ ।
(।।sādhu sādhu camūpatīnāṃ vacanam । etat bhaṇittvā punaḥ kīdṛśamupakrāntaṃ taiḥ ।) kiṃ kathyate ? sainikānāṃ nirupamaḥ parākramaḥ । yātyākṣīt surabhūyakāraṇanijāhaṃkāramucchṛṅkhalam ।
dhārātīrthamupetya divyanagarīmārohato bhūpatīn ।। anantaraṃ tatra tatra pralīnātmanaḥ pratipakṣamūlānanveṣṭukāmāstriliṅgasainikāstattaddeśaveṣabhāṣādikamāviṣkurvāṇāḥ sarvataḥ paryaṭanti sma । jīvagrāhaṃ gṛhītvā samānayanti sma yuvarājāntikam । mantriṇaḥsādhīyān khalu sainikānāmudyamaḥ ।
etat prakṛtopayogitvena vañcanādadhibalam । rājātatastataḥ । dvitīyaḥanantaraṃ narapatayo nijaparijaneṣvapyakṛtaviśvāsāḥ pratāparudrasya pādamūlameva śaraṇamupagatāḥ । parijanaḥ ।
aho ṇaravariṇaṃ jujjhakāarattaṇaṃ । eṣa bhayapratipādanādudvegaḥ । prathamaḥkimucyate kātaryamiti । kāśmīrāḥ smaraṇīyavikramakathā hūṇā nirīṇaśriyaḥ ।
nepālāḥ paripālanavyasaninaḥ suhmāśca nīraṃhasaḥ ।। gauḍāḥ pīḍitavigrahāḥ śritakulagrāvāṅkaṇāḥ koṅkaṇāḥ । karṇāṭāḥ paripūrṇavepathubhṛtastandrālavo mālavāḥ ।। pāṇḍyāḥ khaṇḍitavikramāḥ prakaṭitahrījarjarā ghūrjarāḥ ।
kāmpilyāḥ śritapallayaḥ kṛtayaśobhaṅgāḥ kaliṅgā api ।। parijanaḥ । aho vīraruddassa aisaidatihuvaṇāi jujjhāvadāṇāi । rājā mahatīṃ pratiṣṭhāmāropitaṃ khalu kākatīyakulaṃ viśvaikavijayinā vatsena ।
