purodhasaḥāmūlacūḍaṃ phalitāḥ prasattayaḥ kākatīyānvayadevatānām । rājātatastataḥ । prathamaḥanantaraṃ sakaladigvijayasamuttejitejovilāsaḥ sarvanareśvarāṇāṃ tāni tānyupāyanāni svīkṛtya samagrasainyaiḥ sapakṣairmahībhṛdgaṇairāśritena mahatā balārṇavena nyavartata viśvaikavīro vīrarudraḥ । mantriṇaḥ kutredānīṃ rājaputraḥ ? dvitīyaḥsāmprataṃ kiṃkurvāṇarājalokaḥ sarvānapi senāpatīn nagaraṃ prasthāpya katipayamaulaparivṛtaḥ kākatīyavīraḥ svairaṃ godāvarīparisarāraṇyeṣu mṛgayākutūhalī viharate ।
mantriṇaḥ mahārāja ! nūnaṃ tvayyeva śāsati vasumatīṃ yauvarājyameva bahumanyate rājaputraḥ । eṣā prāptyāśā । digvijayākṛṣṭanareśvaravṛttāntasya vyāpitvāt patākā nirūpitā । rājātadacirameva yuṣmābhirānetavyo vatsaḥ, anunetavyaścarājyābhiṣekāya ।
mantriṇaḥyadājñāpayati devaḥ । nepathye bho bho nāgarikāḥ ! satvaramapasarata dūram । vegotpātitadhūrgataḥ kaṭataṭīniryanmadāmbusrutiḥ । viṣvagvyākulayatyamandarabhasaḥ svairaṃ karigrāmaṇīḥ ।।
eṣa śaṅkātrāsarūpaḥ saṃbhramaḥ । rājā kathaṃ vyākulayati kaṭakaṃ karīndraḥ । puruṣaḥmahārāja ! nūnamidānīṃ nagaraṃ praviśatāṃ nareśvaropāyanānāṃ dvipānāṃ gandhānilāya saṃkru dhyan nirargalo jātaḥ pradhānahastī । pitrā svayaṃbhūpatinopadiṣṭaṃ pratāparudrasya mahābhiṣekam ।
nirvighnamāpādayituṃ gajāsyaḥ kareṇurājākṛtirabhyupaiti ।। eṣa garbhabījodbhedanādākṣepaḥ । rājā tarhi vayamapi pramadavanadvāraprāsādamāruhya gajendramavalokayiṣyāmaḥ । ।।
iti vīrarudravijayo nāma tṛtīyo aṅkaḥ ।। ।। atha caturtho aṅkaḥ ।। dhātrī । haṃje eārisasahassakajjapajjāule rāaulamahūsave vi saalā vi raaṇī keṇa sama tue ṇīdār ।
irisamahagghāi bhūsaṇāi kudo coriāi । kahaṃ ṇa viṇṇādaṃ tue dāsīeuttīesaalā diso jeūṇa cauraṃtasāmaṃtaparivāro paāvaruddo ṇaaraṃ paviṭhṭho । kuṃladevadāe pasattīe mahārāassa aṇṇāe purohidāṇaṃ aṇuroheṇa amaccāṇaṃ aṇuvaṭṭaṇeṇa paāṇaṃ bhāaheee khoṇīe tavoviseseṇa aṃhārisassa pariaṇassa sukaaparipāeṇa abbhupagaamahārajjāhiseo juvarāo saṃjāo । evvaṃ vi eāiṇiṃ maṃ mahūsavāuliaṃ mottūṇa kahiṃ ṭhidā ।
( ।hañje etādṛśasahasrakāryaparyākule rājakulamahotsave api sakalāpi rajanī kena samaṃ tvayā nītār ? idṛśamahārghāṇi bhūṣaṇāni kutaścoritāni ? kathaṃ na vijñātaṃ tvayā dāsyāḥ putryāsakalā diśo jitvā caturantasāmantaparivāraḥ pratāparudro nagaraṃ praviṣṭaḥ । kuladevatāyāḥ prasattyā mahārājasyājñayā purohitānāmanurodhenāmātyānāmanuvartanena prajānāṃ bhāgadheyena kṣoṇyāstapoviśeṣeṇāsmādṛśasya parijanasya sukṛtaparipākeṇābhyupagatamahārājyābhiṣeko yuvarājaḥ saṃjātaḥ । evamapyekākinīṃ māṃ mahotsavākulitāṃ muktvā kutra sthitā ?) anena roṣavaśānniyatāptipradarśanamukhena bījasyāvamarśādvimarśasandhiḥ । ceṭīgatadoṣaprakhyāpanādapavādo aṅgam ।
ceṭī ।। sāmiṇi ! avarāhaṃ sahassa । dhātrī a dāsīeutti, paṭaṃcaleṇa sappadaṃsaṇaṃ paḍimajjesi jaṃ paṇāmeṇar irisāparāhaṃ siḍhilesi । (a dāsyāḥ putri ! paṭāñcalena sarpadaṃśanaṃ parimarjayasi-yatpraṇāmenedṛśāparādhaṃ śithilayasi ।
eṣa roṣasaṃbhāṣaṇarūpaḥ saṃpheṭaḥ । ceṭīr । irisasahāvā evva tumaṃ । tā ṇikkāraṇakoviṇiṃ hodiṃ amuvaṭṭiuṃ ahaṃ ṇa pajjattār ।
( । idṛśasvabhāvaiva tvam । tat niṣkāraṇakopinīṃ bhavatīmanuvartitumahaṃ na paryāptā ।) dhātrī ।। vakkasīladullalie ! lūṇakaṇṇāsiaṃ tumaṃ bandhiūṇa kārāgharabhāaṇaṃ karemi ।
।। eṣa bandhanarūpo vidravaḥ । ceṭī a sāmiṇi ! rakkhohi rakkhehi asaraṇaṃ ṇiravarāha imaṃ jaṇaṃ । tuha attiāe hiḍiṃbassamaṃ gacchatīe ahaṃ balakkāreṇa ṇīdā ।
taddha paḍiūlaṃ devvaṃ pasādaaṃtīe vilaṃbidaṃ । kiṃ karemi । (a svāmini ! rakṣa rakṣa aśaraṇaṃ niraparādhamimaṃ janam । tavāttikayā hiḍimbāśramaṃ gacchantyāhaṃ balātkāreṇa nītā ।
tatra pratikūlaṃ daivaṃ prasādayantyā vilambitam । eṣa gurutiraskṛtirūpo dravaḥ । ceṭīdṛ sāmiṇi ! sahehi vilaṃbiaṃ । tue kādavvaṃ maṃgalovaāraṃ sigghaṃ ṇivvaṭṭemi ।
(dṛ svāmini ! sahasva vilambitam । tvayā kartavyaṃ maṅgalopacāraṃ śīghraṃ nirvartayāmi । haṃje ! uṭhṭhehi uṭṭhehi । eṣā virodhaśamanarūpā śaktiḥ ।
ceṭī a ido ido tattahodī । dhātrī aa kahaṃ eso paḍihārappavaro sasaṃbhamaṃ ṇiggao । tā paccāsaṇṇo via mahāhiseasamao । teṇa rāauttassa maṃgalaṇīrāaṇadīvariṃchcholiṃ ṇivvaṭṭeduṃ abbhaṃtaraṃ pavisahma ।
(aa kathameṣa pratīhārapravaraḥ sasaṃbhramaṃ nirgataḥ । tat pratyāsanna iva mahābhiṣekasamayaḥ । tena rājaputrasya maṅgalanīrājanadīpariñcholiṃ nirvartayitumabhyantaraṃ praviśāvaḥ । yasyodyadghanabṛṃhitairna ghaṭikāghaṇṭādhvaniḥ śrūyate ।
niṣkrāmat praviśacca nāgarakulaṃ na svairamāceṣṭate ।। eṣā tarjanodvejanarūpā dyutiḥ । bho bho kulāmātyavṛddhāḥ pradhānādhikāriṇaḥ parijanāḥ paurāśca saṃśṛṇudhvam । eṣā rudradevasyājñā ।
yasyā mānuṣaśambhunā gaṇapatikṣoṇībhujābhūt prathā । seyaṃ saṃprati vīrarudrabhujayoryātu pratiṣṭhāṃ sthirām ।। eṣā svavaṃśajānāṃ kīrtanād gurukīrtanarūpaḥ prasaṅgaḥ । adhikṛtāḥ kimidānīmārabhadhve ।
kimupakrāntaḥ svayaṃbhūdevasamārādhanavidhiḥ । kacciddattāḥ puradevatābhyo balayaḥ ? kimabhyarcitāḥ sarve varṇavṛddhāḥ ? kaccit prasādhitā mahābhiṣekavediḥ ? kiṃ sajjīkṛtāni kanakakalaśeṣu puṇyatīrthasalilāni ? kaccidabhyarṇamupanītānyuttamopakaraṇāni ? kiṃ maṅgalamuhūrte kṛtāvadhānanā jyotirvidaḥ ? kaccidalaṃkṛtāstriliṅganagarīmṛgīdṛśaśca ? yadidānīṃ vasumatīpāṇigrahaṇocitamaṅgalācāraveṣaḥ pratāparudraḥ kākatīyamārājyalakṣmīmahāntaḥ pure vartate । tat tvaradhvam । kathaṃ rājāno na viramanti ।
bho bho bhūpālāḥ ! yathāvakāśamādhvam । sajjīkurudhvamupāyanajātam । na vṛyā saṃmardaṃ sahate mama vetrayaṣṭiḥ । etadavamānarūpaṃ chalanam ।
aho ! tṛṇīkṛtajagatāṃ kṣitibhṛtāmudvelaṃ saṃmardaṃ nivārayato mama prabhāvaḥ । athavā kākatīyadauvārikāṇāṃ likhitapaṭhitameva rājanivāraṇam । eṣa svaśaktyāviṣkaraṇarūpo vyavasāyaḥ । dauvārikaḥ re kena khalvasamayavidā bhūpatayo nivāritāḥ ? mahotsavadidṛkṣavaḥ sarve praviśantu ।
prathamaḥ re kākatīyakulavṛdhdapratīhāraṃ māmasamayavedinamudāharasi । dvitīyaḥbhavatu yo vā ko vā bhavān । praveṣṭavyā narapataya iti mahārājasyājñā । etat pratīhārayoranyonyaroṣasaṃrabdhavacanarūpaṃ virodhanam ।
prathamaḥkimanena samaṃ śuṣkakalahena । yāvat pradhānāgāradvāravedikāmadhyamadhyāsīnaṃ purohitapuraskṛtaṃ yuvarājamevopasarpāmi । dvitīyaḥahamapi yathānirdiṣṭamanutiṣṭhāmi । purodhasaḥkākatīyakulatilaka ! yuvarājena bhavatā līlayaiva diśo daśa vijitā ityamī samyagadya satyāśiṣo vayam ।
adyānvayaḥ kākatibhūpatīnāṃ prāptastrilokīprathitāṃ pratiṣṭhām । rājanvatī bhūriyamadya jātā vītopasargāḥ sakalāḥ prajāśca ।। eṣā siddhavadbhāviśreyaḥ kathanāt prarocanā । sūryasomānvayāmātyamahattādyādharīkṛtā ।
asmābhiradhikurvāṇaiḥ kākatīyakulasthitim ।। etat prakṛtānuguṇapraśaṃsanād vicalanam । purodhasaḥrājaputra ! sajjīkṛteyaṃ mahābhiṣekasāmagrī । kākatīyanareśvarakramādhiṣṭhiṃta bhadrāsanaṃ bhavadadhirohaṇaṃ pratīkṣate ।
tat paripālaya svayaṃbhūdevānugṛhītāṃ mahārājasyājñām । etat kāryasaṃgraharūpamādānam । pratāparudraḥtarhi kuladevatāṃ svayaṃbhūdevaṃ namaskṛtya, gurvājñāṃ voḍhumicchāmi । purodhasaḥsadṛśo ayamācāraḥ kākatīyakulapradīpasya bhavataḥ ।
kiṃ tu pratyāsīdati mahābhiṣekasamayaḥ । tadacireṇaiva vihitakartavyena rājaputreṇāgantavyam । vayamitaḥ karaṇīyaśeṣaṃ prati pālayāmaḥ । pratāparudraḥyadādiśanti kākatīyānvayapratyāyayitāraḥ ।
।। iti tvaritamahotsavo nāma caturtho aṅkaḥ ।।)।। ।। atha pañcamo aṅkaḥ ।। jyotirvidaḥ bho bhoḥ ! tvaradhvam । kutra purodhasaḥ ।
kutra vā mantriyāḥ ? samānīyatāṃ svayaṃbhūdevasamārādhanāsaktacitatayā vilambamāno rājaputraḥ । yena pratyāsannataro vartate mahābhiṣekamuhūrtaḥ । etaduttarāṅkasya pūrvāṅkārthānusaṃgatvādaṅkāvataraṇam । aho viśvātiśāyinī kākatīyakulapratiṣṭhā ।
śivo yaṃ sajja kurute parākramajitaḥ kṣoṇīpatīnāṃ gaṇaḥ । viṣṇorvīkṣya mahābhiṣevanavidhiṃ nandanti sarve janāḥ ।। eṣa svayaṃbhūdevopadeśanareśvaravijayapramukhamukhasaṃdhyādibījanānārthānāṃ mahāprayojanībhūtamahābhiṣekārthatayā yojanānnirvahaṇasaṃdhiḥ । svapne apyāsūtritāmājñāṃ pālayantaṃ kulodvaham ।
na māntyantarmudaḥ śaṃbhorvibhorapyabhinandataḥ ।। eṣa mukhasaṃdhau prasiddhasya svapnopadeśarūpasya bījasyopagamāt saṃdhiḥ । śreyaḥ prasravanirbharā dvijanuṣāmāśīrgiro jāgrati । nakṣatrāṇi śivaṃkarāṇi śubhadāścānye nimittodayāḥ ।।
tadvayameva rājaputrānayanāya prayatiṣyāmahe । eṣa prakṛtakāryamārgaṇādvirodhaḥ । bhūpālaiḥ karasaṃbhṛtopakaraṇairāptairamātyātmajaiḥ । strīvargaiśca yathocitaṃ parivṛto nīrājanodyogibhiḥ ।।
tadvayaṃ cāsthānīmeva gatvā samucitamācariṣyāmaḥ । mantriṇaḥ kākatīyakulatilaka ! ita itaḥ । idaṃ rājyalakṣmīśuddhāntapradhānāgāraṃ praviśatu svāmī । na vilambārhāḥ kuladevatāyā manorathāḥ ।
etat paṭṭabandharūpakāryasyopakṣepaṇād grathanam । saṃprāptaḥ sumuhūrta eṣa vijayī kalyāṇasaṃpatkhaniḥ । kṣmāpālāṃ ciramanvaśādgaṇapatirbhūbhṛtkulagrāmaṇīḥ ।। eṣa jyotirvidbhiranubhūtārthakhyāpanānnirṇayaḥ ।
parijanaḥ । paccāsaṇṇe vi muhūte kiṃ vilaṃbiadi mahāmaccehiṃ । mantriṇaḥ nātha ! kiṃ vismṛtā gurvājñā । nāyamavasaro nareśvaravijñāpanākarṇanasya ।
mahāsthānyāmevānugṛhyantāmamī । pratāparudraḥśirasi dhṛtaiva khalu tātasyājñā । kiṃ tu nopadiśyate punaranantarakaraṇīyam । etat prakṛtānuguṇyenānyonyaparibhāṣaṇāt paribhāṣaṇam ।
purodhasaḥ svīkṛtamahābhiṣekocitaveṣaḥ kanakavedikāmārohatu pratāparudraḥ । nṛpāḥdeva ! mahārājaparyāyeṇa bhavadbhujaśikharamārohatu medinī । pratāparudraḥtathā bhavatu । nṛpāḥ vijayatāṃ vijayatāṃ kākatīyakulasvāmī ।
eṣa nareśvaraparyupāsanāt prasādaḥ । parijayaḥ a puvvapavvaakaṇaasāṇuṃ sahassarassī via sumerukaṇaataḍaṃ mahendro via pakhkhivakkavaṭṭiṇaṃ cakkadharo via kaṇaavediṃ ārūḍho paāvaruddo । mantriṇaḥkākatīśvara ! samāruhyatāmidaṃ bhadrāsanam । amī purodhaso mahābhiṣekāya tīrthasalilapūrṇān kanakakalaśān dhārayanti ।
pratāparudraḥtathā bhavatu । pratāparudranṛpate ! kākatīyakulocitaiḥ । prajānurañjanaiḥ kṣoṇīṃ pālayācandratārakam ।। eṣa vāñchitārthaprāptirānandaḥ ।
jātaḥ kākativīrarudranṛpate rājyābhiṣekotsavaḥ । devāḥ pūrṇahavirbhujastadadhunā yūyaṃ kṛtārthīkṛtāḥ ।। tasyājñā kṣitipālamaulivalabhīḥ svacchandamārohati । ārohanti ca vindhyabhūdharataṭān pratyarthinaḥ pārthivāḥ ।।
lakṣmīṃ prīṇayate adya kacchapapatirvakṣassthalīdarśanāt । doṣṇā kākativīrarudranṛpatau viśvaṃbharāṃ bibhrati ।। kumbhebhyo api phaṇābhṛtāmadhipatermūrdhnāṃ sahasrādapi । bāhau saṃprati vīrarudranṛpateḥ prāptapratiṣṭhā mahī ।।
eṣa sarvaduḥ khaśamanāt samayaḥ । mantriṇaḥaho ! prabhāvaḥ kākatīyānvayasya । pratāparudrasya mahābhiṣekapayaḥ kaṇā ye nipatanti rājñām । praṇāmanamreṣu śirassu teṣāṃ taiḥ kalpitaḥ svasvapadābhiṣekaḥ ।।
purodhasaḥkākatīyakulottaṃsa ! rājyalakṣmīsaṃvaraṇasragiyamuttaṃsīkriyatām । sarve priyaṃ naḥ priyaṃ naḥ । eṣā prakṛtakāryasthirīkaraṇāt kṛtiḥ । mantriṇaḥ kasko atra bhoḥ ! ānīyatāṃ chatraṃ cāmarayugalaṃ ca ।
pratīhāraḥyadājñāpayanti mahāmātyāḥ । īdṛgviśvajanīnaśauryagarimā jāgarti kaḥ kṣmātale । kiṃkurvāṇasamastabhūpatigaṇaḥ śrīvīrarudro yathā ।। etadakhilātiśāyitvakathanamukhena prakṛtakāryānumodanādābhāṣaṇam ।
yat kākatīyanṛparājyavilāsacihnaṃ yacchāyayā vasumatī vijahāti tāpam । chatreṇa tena kṛtalakṣmaṇi vīrarudre muktātapatravibhavāḥ suhṛdo dviṣaśca ।। eṣa rājyaprāptihetubhūtacchatrāropaṇarūpakāryadarśanāt pūrvabhāvaḥ । mantriṇaḥ nātha ! kākatīyalakṣmīpate ! sanāthāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtayaḥ surājānaṃ tvāṃ didṛkṣante ।
tat sāṃprataṃ mahāsthānīṃ prasādhayatu devaḥ । purodhasaḥācāro ayaṃ kākatīśvarāṇāṃ yanmahābhiṣekānantaraṃ prajānāṃ yogakṣemaparīkṣaṇam । rājāyadājñāpayanti dharmavidaḥ । prakrāntamurvīścaramauliratnaiḥ kurvanti nīrājanamambujākṣyaḥ ।
pratāparudrasya lasatpratāpapradīpanīrājitadiṅmukhasya ।। nṛpatayaḥ aho ! caritārthā sāṃpratamāsmākī cakṣuṣmattā, yayā khalvīdṛganubhūyate । nīrājayantyandhrapurīramaṇyaḥ pradīpajālairvaravīrarudram । candrānanā gotrapatiṃ rajanyastārāgaṇairmerumiva sphuradbhiḥ ।।
mantriṇaḥmahārāja ! kākatīśvara ! sajjīkṛtaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ sarvataḥ pariṣkṛtamidaṃ mahāsthānamaṇṭapaṃ sanāthīkriyatām । pratīhāraḥ deva ! ita itaḥ । prāntaṃ saṃśraya, mālavendra, śanakaiḥ svopāyanaṃ prāpaya । svāmī kākativīrarudranṛpatiḥ sarvān kramādīkṣate ।।
purodhasaḥsvasti kākatīyakulāvatīrṇāya kuparṇaketanāya mahāmahimne adya suprajasā kākatīyānvayena sanāthāni trīṇyapi jaganti । śāsitaryavinītānāṃ narendra ! tvayi śāsati । madhyasthatāsya lokasya cireṇānvarthatāṃ gatā ।। rājā svayambhūcha devavarānukūlānāṃ bhavadāśīrvādānāṃ phalamidaṃ yatkākatīyakṣātraṃ vardhate ।
sarveṣāṃ kākatīyānāṃ bhāgadheyavibhūtayaḥ । evaṃrūpā vivartante yatkulaprabhavo bhavān ।। purodhasaḥna kevalaṃ kākatīyānāmeṣa puṇyaparipākaḥ, api tu sarvāsāmapi prajānām । pratihāraḥdeva ! sarvāḥ prakṛtayo varṇavṛddhān puraskṛtya pratīhāramadhyāsate ।
mantriṇaḥśīghraṃ praveśyantām । pratīhāraḥyadājñāpayantyamātyāḥ । varaḥ pratāparudro ayaṃ vadhūreṣā vasuṃdharā । tayorghaṭayitā devaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ sadṛśaḥ kramaḥ ।।
etat svayaṃbhūdevasya svayaṃ saṃdhātṛtvādadbhutaprāpterupagūhanam । yadvā viśvavibhau svayaṃbhuvi śive nastanvatāmāśiṣaḥ । vācandrārkamimāṃ kṣamāṃ kṛtayaśorakṣau yuvāṃ rakṣatam ।। mantriṇaḥsvāminnete svāyaṃbhuvāḥ sudhiyaḥ ।
yastvadgotramahattarasya jagatāṃ trātuḥ svayaṃbhūvibhos tattādṛkcaritādbhutairmahimabhiḥ svīyairdvitīyo abhavat । nuptuste kulamaṇḍanasya mahatīṃ puṣṇātu rājyaśriyam ।। purodhasaḥrājannete gāṇapetaśvarāḥ sūrayaḥ । yeṣāṃ kākatirājakīrttivibhavaiḥ kailāsaśailāḥ kṛtāḥ ।
drākṣārāmanivāsinaḥ pratidinaṃ tvacchreyase jāgratu ।। purodhasaḥ rājannekaśilānagaravāsino mahādvijāstvete । mantriṇaḥsādhīyān āśīrvādakramaḥ । te jāte laghunī guṇairvijayini śrīkākatīyānvaye ।
prāpyānugrahamūrjiteṣu punarapyete labhete sthitim ।। (rājā sarvān paśyati । purodhaso yathārhaṃ sarvānupaveśayanti । ) prakṛtayaḥvijayatāṃ vijayatāṃ pratāparudramahārājaḥ । rāmo ayaṃ na jagāma locanapathaṃ tenaiva khinnā vayam ।
vīkṣyaivaṃ caritārthatāṃ sumahatīmahnāya gāhāmahe ।। mantriṇaḥsvāmin sāṃprataṃ yathārhamarhaṇayā mānanīyāḥ paurāṇāṃ śreṇayaḥ । jāgartu rājaśabdo ayaṃ mamaivājñāphalaikabhūḥ । rājyopabhogavibhavaḥ sarvasādhāraṇo hi naḥ ।।
sarve sadṛśo ayaṃ prasādaḥ kākatīyakulatilakasya bhavataḥ । rājāprasīdatu bhagavān svayaṃbhūdevaḥ । (iti purohitāvarjitakanakakalaśasasiladhārāpuraḥ saraṃ sakalabhogasamagrān sapraśrayādaraṃ viprasāt karoti । anyeṣāmapi nagaravāsināṃ yathāpradhānaṃ saṃbhāvanāmācarati । ) nṛpatayaḥ svāmin kākatīyamahārāja !
tvadbhṛtyā iti siddhasādanamidaṃ viśvaikanāthe tvayi । kukṣisthākhilaviṣṭapasya sadṛśaṃ kiṃ vātra vijñāpyate ।। mantriṇaḥsvāminnete somārkavaṃśyā narapatayo mahatīmarhaṇāmarhanti । tena sveṣu sveṣu padeṣu pratiṣṭhāpanīyāḥ prasthāpanīyāśca ।
rājātathā । prakṛtayaḥciramanuvartitavyā kākatīyanareśvaraparipālanaparipāṭī mahārojena । pāṇī sūcayataḥ sacāpakuliśāvudvāhalīlāṃ bhuvaḥ । ākhyātastaditīha siddhavacanaṃ pratyakṣamīkṣāmahe ।।
rājā kimasādhyaṃ svayaṃbhūdevamūrtyantarāṇāṃ bhūdevatānāṃ bhavatāmanugrahasya । purodhasaḥ mahārāja ! kākatīśvarakulavāsanāvāsitayā bhavadupāsanayā paraṃ prasedivān paraḥ sahasraprasādonmukhaḥ svayaṃbhūnāthaḥ kiṃ te bhūyaḥ priyamupakarotu । eṣā vākyārthasamāptirūpā saṃhṛtiḥ । rājā kākatīyarājyadhurāyāmavahitameva svayaṃbhūdevena; tathāpīdamastu ।
bhūrastu saṃpannasamastasasyā bhūdevatāḥ pūrṇamanorathāśca । bhūpāśca dharmapravaṇaikacittāḥ sarve janāḥ santu nirāmayāśca ।। eṣāṃ śubhāśaṃsanarūpā praśastiḥ । iti pratāparudrarājyābhiṣeko nāma pañcamo aṅkaḥ ।।
evaṃ sāṅgaṃ nāṭakamudāhṛtam । ।। atha rasaprakaraṇam ।। tha sarveṣāṃ prabandhānāṃ jīvitabhūtasya rasasya svarūpaṃ nirūpyate । vibhāvānubhāvasāttvikavyabhicārisāmagrīsamullāsitaḥ sthāyī bhāvo rasaḥ ।
"vibhāvairanubhāvaiśca sāttvikairvyabhicāribhiḥ । ānīyamānaḥ svādutvaṃ sthāyī bhāvo rasaḥ smṛtaḥ" ।। iti । bhāvasya sthāyitvaṃ nāma sajātīyavijātīyānabhibhūtatayā yāvadanubhavamavasthānam ।
"sajātīyairvijātīyairatiraskṛtamūrtimān । yāvadrasaṃ vartamānaḥ sthāyī bhāva udāhṛtaḥ" ।। śṛṅgārahāsyakaruṇā raudravīrabhayānakāḥ । bībhatsādbhutaśāntāśca rasāḥ pūrvairudāhṛtāḥ ।।
ratirhāsaśca śokaśca krodhotsāhau bhayaṃ tathā । jugupsāvismayaśamāḥ sthāyibhāvā nava kramāt ।। vibhāvaḥ kathyate tatra rasotpādanakāraṇam । ālambanoddīpanātmā sa dvidhā parikīrtyate ।।
rasasamavāyikāraṇamālambanavibhāvaḥ । itarat kāraṇajātamuddīpanavibhāvaḥ । sa caturvidhaḥ । tathā coktaṃ śṛṅgāratilake "ālambanaguṇaścaiva tacceṣṭā tadalaṃkṛtiḥ । taṭasthaśceti vijñeyaścaturdhoddīpanakramaḥ ।।
ālambanaguṇo rūpayauvanādirudāhṛtaḥ । tacceṣṭā yauvanodbhūtahāvabhāvādikā matāḥ ।। nūpurāṅgadahārādi tadalaṅkaraṇaṃ matam । malayānilacandrādyāstaṭasthāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
kāryabhūto anubhāvaḥ syāt kaṭākṣādiḥ śarīrajaḥ ।। paragatasukhādibhāvanābhāvitāntaḥ karaṇatvaṃ sattvam । tato bhavāḥ sāttvikāḥ । stambhaḥ pralayaromāñcau svedo vaivarṇyavepathū । aśru vaisvaryamityaṣṭau sāttvikāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
nirvedaglāniśaṅkākhyāstathāsūyāmadaśramāḥ । ālasyaṃ caiva dainyaṃ ca cintā mohaḥ smṛtirdhṛtiḥ ।। vrīḍā capalatā harṣa āvego jaḍatā tathā । garvo viṣāda autsukyaṃ nidrāpasmāra eva ca ।।
suptirvibodho amarṣaścāpyavahitthamathogratā । matirvyādhistathonmādastathā maraṇameva ca ।। trāsaścaiva vitarkaśca vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । trayastriṃśadamī bhāvā rasasya sahakāriṇaḥ ।।
"kāraṇānyatha kāryāṇi sahakārīṇi yāni ca । ratyādeḥ sthāyino loke tāni cennāṭyakāvyayoḥ । vibhāvāścānubhāvāśca kathyante vyabhicāriṇaḥ" ।। iti।
loke kāryakāraṇasahakāriśabdavācyā nāyikānāyakakaṭākṣabhrūvikṣepanirvedādayaḥ, kāvyanāṭyayostu vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicāriśabdavyapadeśyā bhavanti । śṛṅgāravīraraudrādbhutānāṃ lokottaranāyakāśrayatvena paripoṣātiśayaḥ । ata eva śṛṅgārasya mlecchādiviṣayatve tvābhāsatvam । tathā coktam "ekatraivānurāgaścet tiryaṅmlecchagato api vā । yoṣito bahusaktiścedrasābhāsastridhā mataḥ" ।। iti।
vyabhicāribhāvānāmudayena, praśāmyadavasthayā, parasparaviruddharasāśritayorbhāvayoḥ spardhayā saṃbandhena anyonyopamardakatayā bahūnāṃ samāveśena ca cāturvidhyam । tathā coktaṃ daśarūpake "bhāvasya śāntirudayaḥ saṃdhiḥ śabalatā tathā'; । iti । ।। ratyādisthāyibhāvalakṣaṇodāharaṇāni ।।
atha yathākramaṃ sthāyibhāvānāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । tatra saṃbhogaviṣaya icchāviśeṣo ratiḥ । rindustiṣṭhatu vibhramaikavasatirjāgartu puṣpākaraḥ । jātaḥ kākativallabho mama patiḥ kāmasya kāmotsavaḥ ।।
vikṛtidarśanādijanyo manovikāro hāsaḥ । strīveṣān niśi kākatīndranagare pracchannarūpān nṛpān । hī hī kaṣṭamiti tyajanti vipaṇiśreṇīṣu dhūrtā viṭāḥ ।। iṣṭajanaviyogādinā'tmani duḥ khātibhūmiḥ śokaḥ ।
tattādṛgvibhavā gṛhāḥ kva nu gatāḥ sthānaṃ maruḥ kalpitam । yoṣāṇāṃ tadanūpamaśrubhiraho jātaṃ sthalaṃ māravam ।। śatrukṛtāpacāreṇa manaḥ prajvalanaṃ krodhaḥ । uttīrṇā kila yena gautamanadī prāpto asi mṛtyormukham ।
prakṣubhyatpratipakṣapārthivamahābhūtagrahoccāṭanī ।। lokottareṣu kāryeṣu stheyān prayatna utsāhaḥ । saṃnaddheṣvapi parvateṣu parito gaṇḍopalān varṣitum । ślāghā naḥ kiyatīti kākativibhorgarjanti sainye bhaṭāḥ ।।
raudrasaṃdarśanādibhiranarthāśaṅkanaṃ bhayam । prasthānāranamerīninadamarinṛpāḥ pūrṇakarṇajvarārtāḥ । trāyadhvaṃ muñcateti pratinṛpatidhiyā pādapān prārthayante ।। arthānāṃ doṣasaṃdarśanādibhirgarhaṇā jugupsā ।
śreṇīlabdhapracārāḥ pravahaduruvasāmajjaraktapravāhāḥ । kurvantyāyodhanorvyo bhayamavanibhṛtāṃ vīrarudreṇa sṛṣṭāḥ ।। apūrvārthasaṃdarśanāccittavistāro vismayaḥ । kāpyanyā saraṇiḥ pratāpayaśasoranyaiva bāhvoḥ prathā ।
sāmagrī caturānanena kiyatī kīdṛkkramā kalpitā ।। śamo vairāgyādinā nirvikāracittatvam । labdhvā saṃpadamapyananyasugamāmindreṇa kiṃ vā kṛtam । apyadyopaplavamandhranāthatilake viśvaṃbharāṃ bibhrati ।।
śṛṅgārapratibhūrvilāsavipaṇiḥ kandarpaghaṇṭāpathaḥ । asyā manmathamanmathaḥ priyatamaḥ śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। mṛgākṣyāstaruṇyaṃ tribhuvanamidaṃ vyākulayati । bhavitrī kiṃ vānyadvijitamakhilaṃ puṣpadhanuṣā ।।
manāgvrīḍājāḍyān praṇayarasakallolabharitān । kaṭākṣān vāmākṣī kirati parito rudranṛpatim ।। ।। sāttvikānāṃ svarūpodāharaṇāni ।। []atha sāttvikānāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca ।
stambhaḥ syānniṣkriyāṅgatvaṃ rāgabhītyādisaṃbhavam । kāaipuretthiāo pekhkhaṃtīo ṇareṃdakaṃdappaṃ । maaṇasarukkiṇaṇāo via ṭṭhiā ṇiccaḷaṃgīo ।। (kākatipurastriyaḥ paśyantyo narendrakandarpam ।
madanaśarotkīrṇā iva sthitā niścalāṅgyaḥ ।।) pralayaḥ sukhaduḥkhādyairgāḍhamindriyamūrcchanam ।। jiamaaṇarūvasāro sahi eso vīraruddaṇivacaṃdo । jaṃ daṭhṭhūṇa ṇimajjai mucchāe iṃdiaggāmo ।।
(jitamadanarūpasāraḥ sakhi eṣa vīrarudranṛpacandraḥ । yaṃ dṛṣṭvā nimajjati mūrcchāyāmindriyagrāmaḥ ।।) sukhādyatiśayāñjātā romāñco romavikriyā । rāgaroṣabhayādibhyo vepathurgātrakampanam ।।
adaiāliṅgaṇaṇibhbhakaṃpā a vahū vioajiṇṇaṃgī । uggirai aṃtaraṭṭhidamaaṇasare pulaacammeṇa ।। (adayitāliṅgananirbharakampā ca vadhūrviyogajīrṇāṅgī । udgiratyantarasthitamadanaśarān pulakacchadmanā ।।)
vapurjalodgamaḥ svedo ratidharmaśramādibhiḥ । śṛṇvatī priyasaṃdeśaṃ preyasaḥ kākatīśituḥ । smararājyābhiṣikteva svinnāṅgī vāmalocanā ।। viṣādamadaroṣādervarṇānyatvaṃ vivarṇatā ।।
ṇaraṇāha caṃdadhavale tujjha guṇe sāhu sahmaraṃtīe । aṃgāi pāṃḍurāiṃ ehṇiṃ jāāi sāmāe ।। (naranātha candradhavalān tava guṇān sādhu saṃsmarantyāḥ । aṅgāni pāṇḍurāṇi idānīṃ jātāni śyāmāyāḥ ।।)
aśru netrodbhavaṃ vāri duḥ kharoṣapraharṣajam । vīrarudranṛpādbhītaṃ pāṇḍyaṃ magnaṃ payonidhau । anveṣṭumiva tadyoṣidaśrudhārā'pagāyate ।। mataṃ gadgadabhāṣitvaṃ vaisvaryaṃ pramadādijam ।।
aviaṇammi pieṇa samaṃ khāmakkhāmakkharaṃ bhaṇaṃtīe । ekko muṇai aṇaṃgo atthaṃ bahuāe bhaṇiāṇaṃ ।। (avijane priyeṇa samaṃ kṣāmakṣāmākṣaraṃ bhaṇantyāḥ । eko jānātyanaṅgo arthaṃ vadhvā bhaṇitānām ।।)
।। vyabhicāribhāvānāṃ svarūpodāharaṇe ।। atha vyabhicāriṇāṃ nirvedādīnāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । duḥ kherṣyātattvabodhādernirvedo niṣphalatvadhīḥ । tatra cintāśruniḥ śvāsadīnatāḥ saṃbhavanti ca ।।
sahi kappūreṇa kiaṃ kiṃ katthūrīe malaajo ṭhāu । guṇasisiraṃ jasasurahiṃ āṇehiapaāvaruddaṃ a ।। (sakhi karpūreṇa kṛtaṃ kiṃ kastūryā malayajastiṣṭhatu । guṇaśiśiraṃ yaśaḥ surabhimānaya pratāparudraṃ ca ।।)
glānirbalasyāpacayo vaivarṇyāratikāraṇam । aateḷḷokkaṃ vahai mahī taṃ dharai bhuo paāvaruddassa । taṃ hiaeṇa dharaṃtī sāhasiī dubbalaṃgi mhi ।। (aatrailokyaṃ vahati mahī tāṃ dharati bhujaḥ pratāparudrasya ।
taṃ hṛdayena dharantī sāhasikī durbalāṅgyasmi ।।) atha śaṅkā । aniṣṭābhyāgamotprekṣā śaṅkā roṣādikāraṇam ।। ṇa muṇadu aṇṇo tti mae hiae paricao piassa kido ।
kiṃ paaḍha mhi jaṇāṇaṃ savvaṃgīṇehiṃ pulaehiṃ ।। (na jānātvanya iti mayā hṛdaye paricayaḥ priyasya kṛtaḥ । kiṃ prakaṭāsmi janānāṃ sarvāṅgīṇaiḥ pulakaiḥ ।।) athāsūyā ।
parotkarṣāsahiṣṇutvamasūyā parikīrtitā । aahiāīe guṇehiṃ rūveṇa a majjha kiṃ mahī ahiā । jaṃ taṃ paāvaruddo bahumaṇṇai bhāaheaṃ taṃ ।। (aabhijātya guṇai rūpeṇa ca mattaḥ kiṃ mahī adhikā ?।
yattāṃ pratāparudro bahumanyate bhāgadheyaṃ tat ।।) atha madaḥ । madirādikṛto mohaharṣavyatikaro madaḥ ।। aabhaṇai a asaṃgaatthaṃ hasai amaṃdaṃ a rāabhariacchī ।
piaciṃtāmairāe paravasā uvai sāmaṃgī ।। (aabhaṇati cāsaṃgatārthaṃ hasatyamandaṃ ca rāgabharitākṣī । priyacintāmadirayā paravaśā paśyata śyāmāṅgī ।।) atha śramaḥ ।
śramaḥ khedo adhvaratyāderjātaḥ svedātibhūmikṛt । āacchai evva pie kīsa kareṃtī gaāgaāāsaṃ । tammasi sedajalehiṃ suṃdari luliaṃgarāāsi ।। (āgacchatyeva priye kasmātkurvatī gatāgatāyāsam ।
tāmyasi svedajalaiḥ sundari lulitāṅgarāgāsi ।।) athālasyam । mandodyamatvamālasyaṃ kartavyeṣu prakīrtyate ।। āstāṃ mṛgākṣyā gṛhakṛtyavārtā svāṅgopacāreṣvapi yatnamāndyam ।
kartavyamagre dayitasya yat syānnūnaṃ balātkārayati smarastat ।। atha dainyam । sattvatyāgādanauddhatyaṃ dainyaṃ kārpaṇyasaṃbhavam । āṇeduṃ ṇaraṇāhaṃ gado kkhu sahījaṇo vilaṃbei ।
mammaha ṇamāmi caṃdaṃ sikkhaa cireha īsi tti ।। (ānetuṃ naranāthaṃ gataḥ khalu sakhījano vilambate । manmatha namāmi candraṃ śikṣaya ciraya īṣaditi ।।) atha cintā ।
iṣṭānabhigamāt dhyānaṃ cintā śūnyatvatāpakṛt ।। asaṇṇihiaṃ vi guruaṇaṃ ṇa a pekhkhai pucchiā vi ṇaāḷavai । esā vi maggai gaiṃ hiaassa piāṇubaṃdhassa ।। (asaṃnihitamapi gurujanaṃ na ca prekṣate pṛṣṭāpi nālapati ।
eṣāpi mārgate gatiṃ hṛdayasya priyānubandhasya ।।) atha mohaḥ । mohastu mūrcchanaṃ bhītiduḥ khāveśānucintanaiḥ । viracitanavaveṣā preṣayitvātha dūtīḥ ।
abhihatasakalāṅgī mūrcchitā komalāṅgī ।। atha smṛtiḥ । pūrvānubhūtaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ smṛtirudāhṛtā ।। pratāparudrasya bhuje vasantyā kṣoṇyātapaḥ kīdṛśamārjitaṃ syāt ।
spṛṣṭaṃ sakṛd yena madīyamaṅgaṃ prāpnoti viṣvak sukhavajralepam ।। atha dhṛtiḥ । dhṛtiścittasya naisspṛhyaṃ jñānābhīṣṭāgamādibhiḥ । vīrarudranṛpatau hṛdaya ! tvadvallabhe tribhuvanaikadhurīṇe ।
sādhu sādhu kṛtakṛtyamasi tvaṃ manyase jagadaśeṣamasāram ।। atha vrīḍā । cetaḥ saṃkocanaṃ vrīḍānaṅgarāgastavādibhiḥ ।। tathā samālokanakautukānāṃ manorathairandhrapurāṅganānām ।
vilokite rudranṛpe bhavanti paryastapakṣmāṇi vilocanāni ।। atha capalatā । cāpalaṃ tvanavasthānaṃ rāgadveṣādisaṃbhavam । dṛṣṭvā rudranarendraṃ taralatarākṣī vilāsamṛduhāsā ।
kalayati mauktimahāraṃ spṛśati ca karṇotpalaṃ bālā ।। atha harṣaḥ । prasattirutsavādibhyo harṣaḥ svedāśrukampakṛt ।। vakṣojau yuvayostadadya phalitaṃ jātau kṛtārthau yuvām ।
kastūrīdviguṇabhavatparimalā kalhāramālā yataḥ ।। athāvegaḥ । iṣṭāniṣṭāgamāñjāta āvegaścittasaṃbhramaḥ । draṣṭuṃ kākativīrarudranṛpatiṃ pratyagrakautūhalāḥ ।
ārohanti suvarṇasaudhavalabhīśṛṅgāṇi paurastriyaḥ ।। atha jaḍatā । jāḍyamapratipattiḥ syādiṣṭāniṣṭāgamodbhavā ।। vapuḥ saundaryaśrīvijitamadanodārayaśasi ।
purastādālīnāṃ na calati tathā no viramati ।। atha garvaḥ । anyadhikkaraṇādātmotkarṣo garvo balādijaḥ । kīdṛgvairaṃ pratidharaṇibhṛtkheṭakīṭeṣvamīṣu ।
saṃkrīḍante raṇabhuvi bhaṭāḥ kākatīndrasya jetuḥ ।। atha viṣādaḥ । viṣādaścetaso bhaṅga upāyāpāyacintanaiḥ ।। pesemi maṇa tti muhā taṃ maṃ mokkhūṇa vallahe laggaṃ ।
maṃ ujjhia ṇo gacchai maaṇo sahi kiṃ ṇu kādavvaṃ ।। (preṣayāmi mana iti mudhā tanmāṃ muktvā vallabhe lagnam । māmujjhitvā no gacchati madanaḥ sakhi kiṃ nu kartavyam ।।) athautsukyam ।
kālākṣamatvamautsukyaṃ manastāpatvarādikṛt । aaṃdhavurabhāmiṇijaṇo aṃgāi pasāhiūṇa tuvaraṃto । ruddaṇareṃdāgamaṇe vilaṃbiaṃ sahai kiccheṇa ।। (aandhrapurabhāminījano aṅgāni prasādhya tvaramāṇaḥ ।
rudranarendrāgamane vilambitaṃ sahate kṛcchreṇa ।।) atha nidrā । nidrā cittanimīlanam । siviṇe diṭṭhaṃ daiaṃ vahuā āliṅgiduṃ kidojjoā ।
uvaha daramīliacchī gaaṇammi kare pasārei ।। (।svapne dṛṣṭaṃ dayitaṃ vadhūrāliṅgituṃ kṛtodyogā । paśyata daramīlitākṣī gagane karau prasārayati ।।) athāpasmāraḥ ।
āveśo mohaduḥ khādyairapasmāro aṅgatāpakṛt ।। hā hā rakṣetyasakalagiraḥ saṃbhramotthānabhājaḥ । ārādbhūtānapi ripugaṇā vyastanāmagraheṇa ।। atha suptiḥ ।
suptirnidrāsamudrekaḥ । viśvaikarakṣājuṣi kākatīndre niścintatāṃ prāptavato murāreḥ । tatkīrtticandrātapavardhito api dugdhāmbudhirnaiva bhinatti nidrām ।। atha vibodhaḥ ।
vibodhaścetanāvāptirjṛmbhākṣiparimārgakṛt । pratāparudre nṛpamauliratne viśvaṃbharāṃ rakṣati śikṣitārau । vijṛmbhamāṇāḥ paritaḥ prajānāṃ bhāgyaśriyastatkṣaṇamunmiṣanti ।। athāmarṣaḥ ।
amarṣaḥ sāparādheṣu cetaḥ prajvalanaṃ matam ।। pravṛttāḥ svastrīṇāmahamahamikā vīravaraṇe । raṇāgre garjanti prakaṭitaruṣo rudranṛpateḥ ।। athāvahitthā ।
harṣādyākārasaṃguptiravahittheti kathyate । goṭṭhīe mahilāṇaṃ soūṇa paāvaruddacariāi । ālihai oṇaamuhī muddhā calaṇeṇa mahipaṭṭhaṃ ।। (goṣṭhyāṃ mahilānāṃ śrutvā pratāparudracaritāni ।
ālikhatyavanatamukhī mugdhā caraṇena mahīpṛṣṭam ।।) athogratā । dṛṣṭe aparādhe caṇḍatvamugratā tarjanādikṛt ।। priyamānīya māninyā virahārtirnivāryatām ।
yadetasyāḥ kaṭākṣolkāpātairindurmaṣīkṛtaḥ ।। atha matiḥ । tattvamārgānusaṃdhānādarthanirdhāraṇaṃ matiḥ । ko saṃsao mahialaṃ caṃdo evva vīraruddaṇaraṇāho ।
jassa karappassādo aṃgāi miaṃkaraaṇaṃti ।। (kaḥ saṃśayo mahītale candra eva vīrarudranaranāthaḥ । yasya karasparśādaṅgāni mṛgāṅkaratnanti ।।) atha vyādhiḥ ।
manastāpādyabhibhavājjvarādirvyādhiriṣyate ।। pratāparudrasya diśāṃ jigīṣoḥ pratyarthinārījanadehajanmā । smarajvaroṣmā himavatpradeśān smartavyanīhārakathān karoti ।। athonmādaḥ ।
unmādastulyavartitvaṃ cetanācetaneṣvapi । pratāparudrasya jayaprayāṇabherīdhvanau mūrcchati diṅmukheṣu । trāsākulā bhrāntimupetya vṛkṣān pṛcchanti mārgaṃ ripubhūmipālāḥ ।। atha maraṇam ।
maraṇaṃ maraṇārthastu prayatnaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। piavirahaṃ asahaṃtī vahuā ṇiajīviaṃ uvekkhaṃtī । sevvai johṇaṃ dakhkhiṇapavaṇassa taṇuṃ samappei ।। (।priyavirahamasahamānā vadhūrnijajīvitamupekṣamāṇā ।
sevate jyotsnāṃ dakṣiṇapavanasya tanuṃ samarpayati ।।) sākṣānmaraṇasyāmaṅgalatvānnodāharaṇatvamucitam । atha trāsaḥ । ākasmikabhayāccittakṣobhastrāsaḥ prakīrtyate ।
apaṇaakuviā cireṇa vi vahuā soūṇa ghaṇaghaṇatthaṇiaṃ । daiaṃ sarahasavaliā āliṅgai vevamāṇaṃgī ।। (apraṇayakupitā cireṇāpi vadhūḥ śrutvā ghanaghanastanitam । dayitaṃ sarabhasavalitā āliṅgati vepamānāṅgī ।।)
atha vitarkaḥ । saṃdehāt kalpanā'nantyaṃ vitarkaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। sakhībhirnāloci kṣitipatirasau durlabha iti । kiyān ko ayaṃ kīdṛk kiyadavadhirantarvyatikaraḥ ।।
tatra sāttvikānāṃ vyabhicāriṇāṃ cānekarasasādhāraṇatvānna viśeṣamapekṣyodāharaṇaṃ kṛtam । tathā hi śṛhgāre sarveṣāmanupraveśaḥ saṃbhavati । hāsye glāniśramacapalatvaharṣāvahitthānāṃ saṃbhavaḥ । karuṇe madadhṛtivrīḍāharṣagarvautsukyogratābhirvinānye saṃbhavanti । raudre glāniśaṅkā'lasyadainyacintāvrīḍāvegajaḍatāviṣādasuptinidrāpasmārāvahitthāvyādhyunmādaśamatrāsāḥ na saṃbhavanti । vīre raudrānnirvedo adhikaḥ । bhayānake asūyāmadadhṛtivrīḍāharṣagarvanidrāsuptyamarṣāvahitthogratāmatibhirvinānye saṃbhavanti । bībhatse adbhute ca cintātrāsādayo yathāsaṃbhavamūhyāḥ । śānte nirvedadhṛtī saṃbhavataḥ । tha śṛṅgāraceṣṭā nirūpyante । bhāvo hāvaśca helā ca mādhuryaṃ dhairyamityapi । līlā vilāso vicchittirvibhramaḥ kilakiñcitam ।।
moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭamitaṃ bibboko lalitaṃ tathā । kutūhalaṃ ca cakitaṃ vihṛtaṃ hāsa ityapi ।। evaṃ śṛṅgāraceṣṭāḥ syuraṣṭādaśavidhā matāḥ । tatrāsāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca ।
bhāvaḥ । rasābhijñānayogyatvaṃ bhāva ityabhidhīyate ।। ruddaṇareṃdasya guṇe gāai bālattaṇammi vissaddhaṃ । lajjai darapulaio juvaijaṇo jovvaṇe gāuṃ ।।
(।rudranarendrasya guṇān gāyati bālatve visrabdham । lajjate darapulakito yuvatijano yauvane gātum ।।) atha hāvaḥ । īṣaddṛṣṭavikāraḥ syādbhāvo hāvaḥ prakīrtyate ।
atraiveṣatpulakita iti । atha helā । suvyaktavikriyo bhāvo heleti pratipādyate ।। mā hodu kassa vi phphuḍaṃ ia muddhe kuṇasi vallahaṃ hiae ।
ghosijjai tuha bhāo savvaṃgīṇehi pulaehiṃ ।। (mā bhavatu kasyāpi sphuṭamiti mugdhe karoṣi vallabhaṃ hṛdaye । ghoṣyate tava bhāvaḥ sarvāṅgīṇaiḥ pulakaiḥ ।।) atha mādhuryam ।
abhūṣaṇe api ramyatvaṃ mādhuryamiti kathyate । jitatrailokyalāvaṇyā prakṛtyā hariṇekṣaṇā । kiṃ tu bhūṣayituṃ dhatte bhūṣaṇānīti me matiḥ ।। atha dhairyam ।
śīlādyalaṅghanaṃ nāma dhairyamityabhidhīyate ।। akulavahuāṇaṃ ṇa jujjai majjāālaṃghaṇaṃ khu visame vi । ruddaṇariṃdaguṇā uṇa hiaaharā kiṃ ṇu kādavvaṃ ।। (akulavadhūnāṃ na yujyate maryādālaṅghanaṃ khalu viṣame api ।
rudranarendraguṇāḥ punarhṛdayaharāḥ kiṃ nu kartavyam ।।) atha līlā । priyānukaraṇaṃ līlā vāgbhirgatyātha ceṣṭitaiḥ । aapechchaha sahio esā lacchī raṇṇo paāvaruddassa ।
cariāi aṇukuṇaṃtī raṇṇīsu paivvaā jāā ।। (aaprekṣadhvaṃ sakhya eṣā lakṣmī rājñaḥ pratāparudrasya । caritānyanukurvatī rājñīṣu pativratā jātā ।।) atha vilāsaḥ ।
tātkāliko vikāraḥ syādvilāso dayitekṣaṇe ।। tadātvapratyudyadvividhalalitāṭopamadhuram । mṛgākṣyāstāruṇye kusumaśaraśilpaṃ vijayate ।। atha vicchittiḥ ।
vicchittiratiramyatvaṃ svalpairapi vibhūṣaṇaiḥ । kassa kie keṇa kiaṃ kāaipuraitthiāṇa suṃderaṃ । sāhāraṇabhūsāe jaṃ sahi teḷḷokkaramaṇijjaṃ ।। (kasya kṛte kena kṛtaṃ kākatipurastrīṇāṃ saundaryam ।
sādhāraṇabhūṣayā yatsakhi trailokyaramaṇīyam ।।) atha vibhramaḥ । vibhramastvarayā kāle bhūṣāsthānaviparyayaḥ ।। asoūṇa sahimuhādo diaho virato tti saṃbhameṇa vahū ।
hatthesu ṇourāiṃ caraṇesu a kuṇai valaāiṃ ।। (aśrutvā sakhīmukhāddivaso virata iti saṃbhrameṇa vadhūḥ । hastayornūpure caraṇayośca karoti valayāni ।।) atha kilakiñcitam ।
roṣāśruharṣabhītyādeḥ saṃkaraḥ kilakiñcitam । gehṇai kāaiṇāhe viaṇaṃmi paḍaṃcalaṃ miachchīe । vevai taṇū vi ṇaccai bhiuḍī avi gaggaā vāā ।। (gṛhṇati kākatināthe vijane paṭāñcalaṃ mṛgākṣyāḥ ।
vepate tanurapi nṛtyati bhrukuṭyapi gadgadā vācaḥ ।।) atha moṭṭāyitam । moṭṭāyitaṃ syādiṣṭasya kathādau bhāvasūcanam ।। amahurāi ruddaṇaravaicariāi vahūe ṇaṃ suṇaṃtīe ।
taṇugovaṇaeṇa paaḍo jaha bhāo ṇa taha pulaehiṃ ।। (amadhurāṇi rudranarapaticaritāni vadhvā nanu śṛṇvatyāḥ । tanugopanena prakaṭo yathā bhāvo na tathā pulakaiḥ ।।) atha kuṭṭamitam ।
saṃmarde api sukhādhikyaṃ ratau kuṭṭamitaṃ matam । raṅgervismitamānasāṃ priyasakhīmālokya jātatrapā । sadyo namramukhendurinduvadanā kṣoṇīṃ likhantī sthitā ।। atha bibbokaḥ ।
manāk priyakathālāpe bibboko anādarakriyā ।। krīḍāṃ naiva jahātu, kiṃ ca satataṃ vāṇī mukhe tiṣṭhatu । vyāhāraiḥ kṛtameva dūti ! madanaścāpāya saṃnahyatu ।। atha lalitam ।
sukumāro aṅgavinyāso lalitaṃ parikīrtyate । sahelaṃ vyāvalgatkaravalayanikvāṇasubhagam । purandhrīṇāmāsīdanurahasasevāvilasitam ।। atha kutūhalam ।
kutūhalaṃ ramyadṛṣṭau cāpalaṃ parikīrtyate ।। vīrarudramadhirūḍhasindhuraṃ draṣṭumandhranagarīpurandhrayaḥ । kurvate racitasaṃkramatvarāstuṅgasadmaśikharādhirohaṇam ।। atha cakitam ।
cakitaṃ bhayasaṃbhramaḥ । haṭhādutpaśyantyāścakitacakitodañcitadṛśaḥ । tathaiva pratyetuṃ punaravanipālaḥ spṛhayati ।। atha vihṛtam ।
vihṛtaṃ prāptakālasya vākyasyākathanaṃ hriyā । pratāparudrasya bhujāntarasthāṃ kalhāramālāmamunā spṛśeti । stanadvaye patralipiṃ likhantīṃ sakhīṃ vadhūḥ paśyati sābhimānam ।। atha hasitam ।
ākasmikaṃ tu hasitaṃ yauvanādivikārajam ।। jaha jaha hasai miacchī jovvaṇalacchīe sikhkhiā mahuraṃ । taha taha kusumesusarā viasaṃti piassa āsā a ।। (yathā yathā hasati mṛgākṣī yauvanalakṣmyā śikṣitā madhuram ।
tathā tathā kusumeṣuśarā vikasanti priyasya āśā ca ।।) ।। atha manmathāvasthā dvādaśa nirūpyante ।। atha śṛṅgārasyāṅkuritatvapallavitatvakusumitatvaphalītatvahetavo dvādaśāvasthā nirūpyan te । cakṣuḥ prītirmanaḥ saṅgaḥ saṃkalpo atha pralāpitā ।
jāgaraḥ kārśyamaratirlajjātyāgo atha saṃjvaraḥ ।। unmādo mūrcchanaṃ caiva maraṇaṃ caramaṃ viduḥ । avasthā dvādaśa matāḥ kāmaśāstrānusārataḥ ।। kecittu daśāvasthā iti kathayanti ।
āsāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । ādarāddarśanaṃ cakṣuḥ prītirityabhidhīyate । sahi eso ruddaṇio ṇaaṇāṇa atakkiossao jāo । maaṇo va muttimaṃto caṃdo via mukkalañchaṇo puṇṇo ।।
(sakhi ! eṣa rudranṛpo nayanayoratarkitotsavo jātaḥ । madana iva mūrtimān candra iva muktalāñchanaḥ pūrṇaḥ ।।) atha manaḥ saṅgaḥ । manaḥ saṅgaḥ priyatame nityaṃ cittasya viśramaḥ ।।
saha maha maṇo vilaggai ruddaṇarendammi kīsa kuviāo । teṇāhaṃ vi vimukkā sahio tuhmesu kā vattā ।। (sadā mama mano vilagati rudranarendre kasmāt kupitāḥ । tenāhamapi vimuktā sakhyo yuṣmāsu kā vārtā ।।)
atha saṃkalpaḥ । saṃkalpo nāthaviṣayo manoratha udāhṛtaḥ । adarahasiagabbhiṇāiṃ siṇehasiṇiddhāi rāabhariāi । ruddaṇivaviloiāiṃ kāhe ṇu mammi ṇivadaṃti ।।
(adarahasitagarbhitāni snehasnigdhāni rāgabharitāni । rudranṛpavilokitāni kadā nu mayi nipatanti ।।) atha pralāpaḥ । prālapaḥ priyasaṃśliṣṭaguṇālāpa udāhṛtaḥ ।।
taha ṇiuṇo taha mahuro taha suhao taha a sommasabbhāo । ekko ruddaṇivo via idi goṭṭhī poḍhamahilāṇaṃ ।। (tathā nipuṇastathā madhurastathā subhagastathā ca saumyasvabhāvaḥ । eko rudranṛpa eveti goṣṭhī prauḍhamahilānām ।।)
atha jāgaraḥ । jāgarastu vinidratvam । agamiaṃ kaha kaha vi diṇaṃ caṃdādavadūsahā ṇisā dīhā । maaṇo vi puṃkhiasaro ṇiddā vi ṇivo vi ṇovei ।।
(agamitaṃ kathaṃ kathamapi dinaṃ candrātapaduḥ sahā niśā dīrghā । madano api puṅkhitaśaro nidrāpi nṛpo api nopaiti ।।) atha kārśyam । kārśyamaṅgasya tānavam ।
premṇāṃ preyasi vaibhavaiḥ sa khalu ko bhūmeḥ sapatnī yataḥ । śyāmāṅgīṃ sa khalu sthirāṃ ramayate tvāṃ tāṃ ca śailastanīm ।। athāratiḥ । anyatrāprītiraratiḥ ।
dūsei caṃdasiṭṭiṃ ṇiṃdai malaāṇilassa māhappaṃ । ūsavaparaṃmuhī sā suhaa ! tumaṃ kiṃ ṇu maṃtesi ।। (dūṣayati candrasṛṣṭiṃ nindati malayānilasya māhātmyam । utsavaparāṅmukhī sā subhaga ! tvaṃ kiṃ nu mantrayase ।)
atha lajjātyāgaḥ । alaṃghiamahilāsamaaṃ taha bhaṇiaṃ maaṇaduvviṇīdāe । jaha soūṇa guruaṇo osarai vilajjio dūraṃ ।। (alaṅghitamahilāsamayaṃ tathā bhaṇitaṃ madanadurvinītayā ।
yathā śrutvā gurujano apasarati vilajjito dūram ।।) atha jvaraḥ । tāpādhikyaṃ jvaro mataḥ ।। amohasisirovaārā vahuā virahajjareṇa gurueṇa ।
dāṇiṃ ruddaṇaresara ! kāṃkhai tuha daṃsaṇāmiaaṃ ।। (amoghaśiśiropacārā vadhūrvirahajvareṇa guruṇā । idānīṃ rudranareśvara ! kāṅbhati tava darśanāmṛtam ।।) unmādamaraṇayoḥ prāgevodāharaṇaṃ darśitam ।
atha mūrcchā । mūrcchā tvabhyantare avṛttirbāhyendriyanimīlanāt । aaciṃtaṃtīe ṇarendaṃ daṭṭhuṃ hiaaṭhṭhidaṃ miacchīe । karaṇāi bāhirāiṃ visaṃti abbhaṃtaraṃ vi suṇṇāe ।।
(aacintayantyā narendraṃ draṣṭuṃ hṛdayasthitaṃ mṛgākṣyāḥ । karaṇāni bāhyāni viśanti abhyantaramapi śūnyāyāḥ ।।) atha śṛṅgāraḥ । saṃbhogo vipralambhaśceti । "saṃyuktayostu saṃbhogo vipralambho viyuktayoḥ a; iti aśṛṅgāratilake'; । saṃbhogasya parasparāvalokanasaṃbhāṣaṇā'liṅganacumbanādyanekavyāpāramayatvenānantyādekavidhatvena gaṇanā kṛtā । nivṛttā mānājñā viralamapi lajjāvilasitam ।
smarāveśaḥ ko api priyasakhi ! nṛpeṇaikayati mām ।। vipralambhaḥ punarabhilāṣerṣyāvirahapravāsahetukatvena caturvidhaḥ । abhilāṣo nāma saṃbhogāt prāganurāgaḥ । śayyā ca sārdhamapadāni manorathānām ।
labhyate rudranṛpateravalokitaṃ vā ।। īrṣyā nāma nāyakasyānyāsaktabhāvāt cittavikriyā । vaktrasthā ca sassvatī na sahate sākaṃ tvayā bhāṣaṇam । kṣoṇīndre na hi kaitavāni subhage mānena kiṃ tāmyasi ।।
viraho nāma labdhasaṃyogayornāyakayoḥ kenacit kāraṇena punaḥ samāgamakālātikṣepaḥ । aṅgeṣu jīrṇeṣu vibhūṣaṇānāṃ vyatyāsamārgo api muhūrtaśobhī । sakhyastadāstāṃ parikarmarītirānīyatāṃ rudranṛpaḥ kimanyat ।। yūnordeśāntaravṛttitvaṃ pravāsaḥ ।
rabhyutsaveṣu sulabhā na hi vallabhā naḥ । daṅgāni yānti tanutāṃ divasā yuganti ।। pārāvatīṃ ramaṇacumbitacañcukoṭim । mālokya kākativibhuḥ smitamātanoti ।।
sakhyetasya kimatra kāryamaparaṃ kiṃ janmasadmādarāt । preyān rudranṛpastaveti kathitā namrānanābhūd vadhūḥ ।। atra lajjāyā udayaḥ । sṛṣṭyāmambujaviṣṭarasya sadṛśoryogaści rāt saṃbhṛtaḥ ।
gityāliṃ praṇatāṃ vilokya vikasadvaktrāmbujā māninī ।। atra kopasya praśamaḥ । pratāparudrasya digantajaitrayātrāprabhūtaiḥ paṭahapraṇādaiḥ । priyānulāpaiśca tathā bhaṭānāṃ raumāñcavarmāvṛtamaṅgamāsīt ।।
atra vīraśṛṅgārakṛtayorharṣayoḥ sandhiḥ । bhāgyenānumataṃ na kiṃ gurujanaiḥ kā vā sakhī preṣyate । rokṣyāmi sthiratā kadā hṛdi bhaved yātavya eva priyaḥ ।। atrautsukyādīnāṃ śabalatā ।
atha rasasaṃkarasyodāharaṇam । rdhigū dhik sāhasamāvayorvighaṭanaṃ ko vā vidhiḥ kāṅkṣati । buddhvā mūrcchati kākatīyanṛpate ! tvadvairinārījanaḥ ।। matto mastiṣkalagnairdalitanṛpavapuḥ kīkasaiḥ spaṣṭadaṃṣṭraḥ ।
saṃgrāmorvyāḥ kaliṅgairbalividhimakarod vīrarudrasya khaḍgaḥ ।। evamanyadapi yathāsaṃbhavamudāhāryam । atra raso nāyakāśraya eva । yadiparaṃ nipuṇanaṭaceṣṭayā tathāvidhakāvyaśravaṇabalena ca sāmājikaiḥ sākṣād bhāvyate, tadā paragatasyāpi rasasya samyagbhāvanayā paratra niratiśayānandajananamaviruddham । athavā mālatyādiśabdebhyo yoṣinmātrapratītau smṛtyārūḍhena tattadyoṣidviśeṣeṇa anukāryeṇa sāmājikāśrayatvamapi na viruddham । naṭasyānukaraṇamātraparatayā naiva rasāśrayayogyatā । tasya bhāvukatvābhyupagame api sāmājikatvameva । anubhāvādīnāṃ prakāśanaṃ tu śikṣābhyāsapāṭavenaiva ghaṭate । rasādīnāṃ parasparavirodhe api kaviprauḍhoktisamāśrayaṇenaikatra samāveśo na viruddhaḥ । virodhakramaḥ aśṛṅgāratilake'; kathitaḥ "śṛṅgārabībhatsarasau tathā vīrabhayānakau ।
raudrādbhutau tathā hāsyakaruṇau vairiṇau mithaḥ" ।। iti। rasād rasotpattirapi matā । tathā coktaṃ aśṛṅgāratilake' "hāsyo bhavati śṛṅgārāt karuṇo raudrakarmaṇaḥ ।
adbhutaśca tathā vīrād bībhatsācca bhayānakaḥ" ।। vyabhicāribhāvānāṃ tattadrasānuguṇyamevaṃ pratipāditaṃ aśṛṅgāratilake'; । tathā hi "śaṅkāsūyā bhayaṃ glānirvyādhiścintā smṛtirdhṛtiḥ । autsukyavismayāvegā vrīḍonmādau madastathā ।।
viṣādo jaḍatā nidrāvahitthaṃ cāpalaṃ mṛtiḥ । iti bhāvāḥ prayoktavyāḥ śṛṅgāre vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।। śramaścapalatā nidrā spapno glānistathaiva ca । śaṅkāsūyāvahitthaṃ ca hāsye bhāvā bhavantyamī ।।
saṃtrāso maraṇaṃ dainyaṃ glāniścaiva bhayānake । apasmāro viṣādaśca bhayaṃ vego mṛtirmadaḥ ।। unmādaśceti vijñeyā bhāvā bībhatsasaṃbhavāḥ । āvego jaḍatā moho harṣaṇaṃ vismayaḥ smṛtiḥ ।।
iti bhāvā nibaddhavyā rasajñairadbhute rase । dainyaṃ cintā tathā glānirnirvedo jaḍatā smṛtiḥ ।। vyādhiśca karuṇe vācyā bhāvā bhāvaviśāradaiḥ । harṣo asūyā tathā garva utsāho mada eva ca ।।
cāpalyamugratā caiva raudre bhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । amarṣaḥ pratibodhaśca vitarko atha matirdhṛtiḥ ।। krodho asūyātha saṃmoha āvegaścopaharṣaṇam । garvo madastathogratvaṃ bhāvā vīre bhavantyamī" ।।
iti। "rasaḥ sarvo api saṃpūrṇastirodhatte rasāntaram ।।ḥ iti bhāratīyoktaprakrīyayā yadyapyeka eva rasaḥ, tathāpi mahākaviprasiddhyā rasasaṅakaraḥ svīkriyate । tatra rasāderaprādhānye rasavadādyalaṃkārā bhavanti । anyāṅgatvena rasanibandhane rasavadalaṃkāraḥ । bhāvanibandhane preyo alaṃkāraḥ । rasābhāsabhāvābhāsanibandhane ūrjasvidalaṃkāraḥ । bhāvaśāntinibandhane samāhitālaṃkāraḥ । tathā bhāvodayādayo api ।
"rasabhāvatadābhāsatatpraśamananibandhane rasavatpreyaūrjasvisamāhitāni । bhāvodayabhāvasandhibhāvaśabalatāśca pṛthagalaṃkārāḥ aiti । eteṣāmudāharaṇamalaṃkaraṇe bhaviṣyati । sphuratprādurbhāvaḥ kramagalitavedyāntaramatiḥ । tvamandānandātmā pariṇamati pūrṇo rasabharaḥ ।। vibhāvādyā yasmin kila dadhati viśrāntimucitām ।
rasībhāvaṃ bibhratyatha ca paṭatāṃ tantava iva ।। kallolā iva saṃbhavanti vilayaṃ cāyānti bhāvā muhuḥ । loke syādanukārya eva kathito nāṭye tu sāmājike ।। iti śrīvidyānāthakṛtau pratāparudrayaśobhūṣaṇe alaṃkāraśāstre rasaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।
।। atha doṣaprakaraṇam ।। atha kāvyajīvitabhūtarasanirūpaṇānantaraṃ tadupaskārahetūnāṃ guṇānāṃ samyagvivekāya doṣā nirūpyante । doṣaḥ kāvyāpakarṣasya hetuḥ śabdārthagocaraḥ । śabdārthamayatvāt kāvyasya tadapakarṣahetūnāmapi doṣāṇāṃ śabdagatatvenārthagatatvena ca dvaividhyam ।
śabdagatānāmapi padavākyagatatvena ca dvaividhyam । tatra padagatadoṣāḥ kathyante । aprayuktamapuṣṭārthamasamarthaṃ nirarthakam । neyārthaṃ cyutasaṃskāraṃ saṃdigdhaṃ cāprayojakam ।।
kliṣṭaṃ gūḍhārthakaṃ grāmyamanyārthaṃ cāpratītikam । avimṛṣṭavidheyāṃśaṃ viruddhamatikṛt tathā । aślīlaṃ paruṣaṃ ceti doṣāḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ ।। eṣāṃ svarūpaṃ nirūpyate ।
yadaprayuktaṃ kavibhiraprayuktaṃ taducyate । prakṛtānupayuktārthamapuṣṭārthaṃ taducyate ।। yogamātraprasiddhaṃ yadasamarthaṃ taducyate । pādapūraṇamātraṃ yat tannirarthakamucyate ।।
svasaṃketaprasiddhārthaṃ neyārthaṃ parikīrtyate । śabdaśāstraviruddhaṃ yat cyutasaṃskāramucyate ।। saṃdigdhaṃ tanmataṃ yat syāt saṃdigdhārthapratītikṛt । tadaprayojakaṃ yat syādaviśeṣavidhāyakam ।।
kliṣṭaṃ tadarthāvagatirdūradūrā yato bhavet । prayuktamaprasiddhārthe gūḍhārthaṃ parikīrtyate ।। pāmaravyavahāraikaprasidhdaṃ grāmyamucyate । yadrūḍhipracyutaṃ nāma tadanyārthamudāhṛtam ।।
śāstramātraprasiddhaṃ yadapratītikamucyate । avimṛṣṭavidheyāṃśaṃ guṇībhūtavidheyakam ।। viparītārthadhīryasmād viruddhamatikṛnmatam । aślīlaṃ yadamāṅgalyajugupsāvrīḍadhīkaram ।।
paruṣaṃ nāma tad yat syādvihitaṃ paruṣākṣaraiḥ ।। atra vanavṛttīnāṃ śatrustrīṇāṃ vacaneṣu doṣā udāhriyante । vimukhā daivatāḥ sarve te no duścyavanādayaḥ । araṇyagṛhamedhinyo yairvayaṃ hanta kalpitāḥ ।।
atra daivatā iti puṃliṅgaprayogaḥ doṣaḥ; duścayavana iti ca indraparatvena kavibhirna prayuktaḥ । vyarthāṣṭārdhārdhabāhūnāmamīṣāmīdṛśāṃ daśām । kathaṃ sahāmahe dhigdhik kaṭhinaṃ hanta jīvitam ।। atra vyarthabāhudvayānāmiti vivakṣite aṣṭārdhārdhabāhūnāmityanupayuktam ।
etadevāvimṛṣṭavidheyāṃśasyodāharaṇam । bāhudvayasya vaiyarthye vidheye tasyopasarjanatvaṃ pratīyate । vihāya vasudhāmenāṃ caturambudharāvṛtām । ka nu gantavyamasmākamaraṇye apyasukhā sthitiḥ ।।
atra jaladhiparatvenāmbudharapadamasamartham । vihāya ca gṛhāṃstān vai vyatyastanavavṛttayaḥ । kadā bhaviṣyate vāsaḥ kaṭakeṣu mahībhṛtān ।। atra vai iti nirarthakam ।
vyatyastanavaśabdena vanapratītiḥ svasaṃketamātrāyateti neyārthakam । bhaviṣyate iti bhavaterātmanepaditvaṃ śabdaśāstraviruddhamiti cyutasaṃskāram । mahībhṛtāṃ kaṭakeṣu vāsa ityanena rājñāṃ nagareṣu vāsaḥ ? uta parvatānāṃ nitambeṣu ? iti saṃdehāt saṃdigdham । hanta vartāmahe vajraghaṭṭanāt prāk calātmasu ।
nabhasvadaśanārātidhvajāgrajavirodhiṣu ।। atra nabhasvadaśanāḥ sarpāḥ, teṣāmarātirgaruḍaḥ, sa eva dhvajo yasyeti viṣṇuḥ, tasyāgraja indrastasya virodhiṣu parvateṣu ityarthapratīteratidūratvāt kliṣṭam । parvateṣu vartanaṃ duḥ khāvahamiti prakṛte vajraghaṭṭanāt prāk calātmasviti parvataviśeṣaṇasyānupayuktatvādaprayojakam । śoṇitābjadṛśaḥ kāmaṃ śyāmagallakaṭisthalāḥ ।
vidagdhahṛdayāḥ śokavahninā rājakanyakāḥ ।। atra śoṇitaśabdasya rudhire prasiddhasya pāṭalavarṇaparatvena prayogād gūḍhārtham । gallakaṭiśabdau kapolajaghanaparatvena grāmyaprayuktau । vidagdhahṛdayā iti viśeṣaṇaṃ dagdhahṛdayasyāvācakatvādanyārtham ।
manūpadeśāḥ kva gatāḥ kulācāryairudīritāḥ ।। atra manuśabado mantraparatvena mantraśāstramātraprasiddha ityapratītikam । ambikāramaṇasyāṅghrisevā vyarthā kathaṃ bhavet । rājñāmakāryamitrāṇāṃ vināśaṃ samupeyuṣām ।।
atrāmbikāramaṇaśabdānmātṛsaṃbhogakāriṇaḥ pratītiḥ । akāryamitraśabdādakāryeṣu mitrāṇīti pratītiḥ । viyogaduḥ khaparatayā prayuktādvināśaśabdānnaśapratītiriti viruddhamatikṛt । abhipretapadāvāsaḥ kadā naḥ saṃbhaviṣyati ।
nīcaṃ sādhanameteṣāṃ parotsargaikajīvinām ।। atrābhipretapadāvāsaśabdāt pretalokapadāvāsapratīteramaṅgalatvam । nīcaṃ sādhanamityanena tucchamohanapratītervrīḍākaratvam । parotsargaukajīvināmityatrotsargaśabdādadhovāyupratīterjugupsākaratvam ।
kutaḥ kāntāravṛttīnāṃ kārtārthyārthitvamasti naḥ । atra kārtārthyārthitvamiti paruṣavarṇārabdhatvam । ।। śabdahīnaṃ kramabhraṣṭaṃ visaṃdhi punaruktimat ।
vyākīrṇaṃ vākyasaṃkīrṇamapūrṇaṃ vākyagarbhitam ।। dve bhinnaliṅgavacane dve ca nyūnādhikopame । bhagnacchando yatibhraṣṭamaśarīramarītikam ।। visargaluptamasthānasamāsaṃ vācyavarjitam ।
samāptapunarāttaṃ ca tathā saṃbandhavarjitam ।। patatprakarṣamadhikapadaṃ prakramabhaṅgavat । caturviṃśatirucyante doṣā vākyasamāśritāḥ ।। eṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca ।
śabdaśāstrahataṃ vākyaṃ śabdahīnaṃ prakīrtyate । na saṃśṛṇumahe hanta hitamāptairnimantritam । yena kākatibhūbhartuḥ sevāṃ hitvā hatā vayam ।। atra hitaṃ na saṃśṛṇumahe iti padadvayaprayoge doṣāviṣkārādvākyameva duṣṭamiti na padadoṣaśaṅkā ।
saṃpūrvasya śṛṇoterātmanepaditve karmaṇo anupādānaniyamāt । atha kramabhraṣṭam । kramabhraṣṭaṃ bhavedārthaḥ śābdo vā yatra na kramaḥ ।। prabhave kākatīndrāya turagān kariṇo athavā ।
upāyanamakurvāṇā vayaṃ daivena vañcitāḥ ।। atra kariṇo yadvā turagāniti vaktavye vyutkrameṇoktam, turagāpekṣayā kariṇāmutkṛṣṭatvāt । athavā kariṇa ityarthakramabhaṅgaḥ । kā nāma gaṇanāsmāsu kākatīyasya bhūpateḥ ।
yaśaḥ pratāpayormagnau sūryācandramasāvapi ।। atra yaśaḥ pratāpayoścandrasūryau magnāviti śabdakrame ucite tathā noktam । yaśaḥ pratāpayoḥ sūryācandramasau magnāviti samudāyadvayānvaye yathāyogyamarthānvaye siddhe nārthakramavirodhaḥ । api tu śabdaprayoga eva kramabhaṅgaḥ ।
atha visandhi । visaṃhito virūpo vā yasya saṃdhirvisaṃdhi tat । śauryāṇi īdṛśānyāsan pṛthvaiśvaryaṃ kva vā gatam । atra śauryāṇi īdṛśānīti visandhi ।
pṛthvaiśvaryamiti saṃdhivairūpyam । atha punaruktimat । śabdārthapaunaruktye tu tadvākyaṃ punaruktimat ।। jīrṇakānanasaṃkīrṇe vindhye kānanavṛttayaḥ ।।
atra kānanasaṃkīrṇe kānanavṛttaya iti punaruktimat । atha vyākīrṇam । vyākīrṇaṃ tadvibhaktīnāṃ vyākīrṇe ca mitho anvaye । sukhārthino mahīpālā vartadhvaṃ kākatīśituḥ ।
ājñāmurasi bibhrāṇāḥ śirasi kroḍamudrikām ।। atra kroḍamudrikāmurasi śirasyājñāṃ bibhrāṇā iti saṃbandhaḥ । atha vākyasaṃkīrṇam । vākyāntarapadaiḥ kīrṇaṃ vākyasaṃkīrṇamucyate ।।
mānena mahatāsmābhirvane vaktre na tiṣṭhatām । vindhayasya jīvitaṃ tanno jātamadya tṛṇaṃ kṛtam ।। atra mahatā mānena asmābhiryattṛṇaṃ vaktre na kṛtaṃ tadadya vindhyasya vane tiṣṭhatāṃ no jīvitaṃ jātamiti vākyadvayapadānāmanyonyasaṃkīrṇatā । apūrṇaṃ tadbhaved yatra na saṃpūrṇaḥ kriyānvayaḥ ।
śaileṣvasmākamāvāso vanyaiḥ socchvasitā vayam । mṛgairbandhumataścāsmān paśyan dhātā pramodatām ।। atra śailavāsān vanyavṛttīn mṛgabāndhavān paśyanniti vivakṣitasaṃbandhau na saṃpūrṇaḥ । atha vākyagarbhitam ।
tad vākyagarbhi taṃ yasya madhye vākyāntaraṃ bhavet ।। jñātvāpyandhrapurīndrasya krodhāgnimatiduḥ saham । yadvā na laṅghyate daivaṃ tasminnipatitā vayam ।। atrātiduḥ sahaṃ krodhāgniṃ jñātvāpi tasminnipatitā vayamiti vākyamadhye yadvā na laṅghyate daivamiti vākyāntaramanupraviṣṭamiti vākyagarbhitatvam ।
atha bhinnaliṅgavacane । yatropamā bhaved bhinnavacanā bhinnaliṅgakā । tadbhinnavacanaṃ bhinnaliṅgaṃ cāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।। samudrā iva gambhīraṃ mano yādavabhūbhujaḥ ।
giriṇevāndhranṛpatidhvajinyā kaluṣīkṛtam ।। atra samudrā iva gambhīramiti bhinnavacanam । giriṇeva dhvajinyeti bhinnaliṅgam । athādhikanyūnopame ।
yatropamānamadhikaṃ nyūnaṃ vā syādviśeṣaṇaiḥ । tatrādhikopamaṃ pūrvaṃ nyūnopamamataḥ param ।। dvayoḥ yathākramamudāharaṇam । kṣāmakṣāmamukhāḥ kāntāḥ kānane mālaveśituḥ ।
grīṣme nadya iva glānapadmotpalabisāvilāḥ ।। atra kṣāmakṣāmamukhānāṃ kāntānāmupamānabhūtāsu nadīṣu mlānapadmatvamātraṃ vaktavyam । mlānotpalabisāvilā ityadhikam । hārāṅgarāgasubhagā nagareṣu yathā vayam ।
tathaiva nirjharākīrṇā vibhānti dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।। atra hārasthāne nirjharā uktāḥ । aṅgarāgasthāne kimapi noktamiti nyūnopamatvam । atha bhagnacchandoyatibhraṣṭe ।
chandobhagnaṃ vaco yatra tadbhagnacchanda ucyate । yatra sthāne yatibhraṃśastad yatibhraṣṭamucyate ।। vindhyāraṇyakṛtakuṭumbarakṣaṇasya kiṃ bhadraṃ bhavati janasya mādṛśasya ।। atra vindhyāraṇyeti tṛtīyavarṇe yatibhaṅgaḥ ।
pādāntavarṇasya gurutvābhāvācchandobhaṅgaḥ । athāśarīram । kriyāpadena rahitamaśarīraṃ prakīrtyate । hanta niṣkaruṇo dhātā krīḍato maṇikuṭṭime ।
kānane kaṇṭakākīrṇe sthitān pāṇḍyaśiśūnimān ।। atra kriyāpadaṃ na vihitam । etadevānanvayākhyaṃ dūṣaṇam । athārītikam ।
rasānanuguṇā rītiryatrārīti taducyate ।। akharvagarvadurvāradorargalanirargalāḥ । hā bandhuvargāḥ sarve api kṛtāntātithayaḥ kṛtāḥ ।। atra karuṇe anucito varṇāḍambaraḥ ।
atha visargaluptam । otvaṃ lopo visargasyāsakṛlluptavisargakam । yatra visargo bahudhautvaṃ lopaṃ vā prāpnoti tadvisargaluptam । vyartho manoratho yāto jāto vāso dhruvo marau ।
mlānā dīnā hatā jīrṇā vanānteṣvīdṛśā vayam ।। athāsthānasamāsam । apadasthasamāsaṃ tat samāso yatra nocitaḥ ।। kuto vaimukhyamasmāsu brahmaṇaḥ paruṣātmanaḥ ।
ityudagratarabhrāmyadbhṛkuṭīkuṭilānanāḥ ।। atra vedhase krudhyatāṃ nṛpāṇāmuktau na samāsaḥ । kiṃ tu kavivacane samāsa ityapadasthasamāsaḥ । atha vācyavarjitam ।
noktaṃ syādyatra vaktavyaṃ tadāhurvācyavarjitam । durdaśāṃ pratipannānāmasmākaṃ jīvitaṃ matam ।। atra durdaśāṃ pratipannānāmapītyapiśabdo vaktavyo noktaḥ । atha samāptapunarāttakaṃ patatprakarṣaṃ ca ।
samāpya punarādāne samāptapunarāttakam । patatprakarṣaṃ tatprāhuḥ prakarṣo yatra viślathaḥ ।। dhāvanmṛgeṣu saṃbhrāmyatkariṣūdyattarakṣuṣu । vindhyāraṇyeṣu tiṣṭhāmaḥ kṣubhyadbhallūkapaṅktiṣu ।।
atra vindhyāraṇyeṣu tiṣṭhāmaḥ iti samāpya kṣubhyadbhallūkapaṅktiṣviti punarādānāt samāptapunarāttakam । atha bhrāmyatkariṣūdyattarakṣuṣu dhāvanmṛgeṣviti vaktavye na tathoktamiti patatprakarṣatā । atha saṃbandhavarjitam । saṃbandhavarjitaṃ tat syād yatreṣṭenānvayo hataḥ ।
bhadrāsanāni dṛṣadaḥ chatrāṇi ca mahīruhaḥ । durdaśārājyamūrdhābhiṣiktāḥ punaraho vayam ।। atra rājye bhadrāsanāni dṛṣada ityādisaṃbandho noktaḥ । athādhikapadam ।
yatrādhikapadoktiḥ syāt tatrādhikapadaṃ matam ।। vimuktā vallabhairetā vanānte ghūrjarastriyaḥ । sudhāṃśumaṇḍalākārarūpakramavipāṇḍurāḥ ।। atra sughāṃśumaṇḍalākāra ityetāvatā paripūrṇe maṇḍalākāravipāṇḍuratve rūpakrama ityadhikam ।
atha bhagnaprakramam । prakrāntaniyamatyāge bhagnakramamihocyate ।। guhā gṛhāṇi śabarā bāndhavā vindhyabhūḥ purī । sarito dīrghikāḥ kaṣṭamākrīḍāḥ kānanāni naḥ ।।
atra bahuvacanatayā prathamaṃ prakamya vindhyamūḥ purītyekavacanokteḥ prakramabhraṣṭam । ।। athārthadoṣāḥ ।। apārthaṃ vyarthamekārthaṃ sasaṃśayamapakramam ।
bhinnaṃ caivātimātraṃ ca paruṣaṃ virasaṃ tathā ।। hīnādhikopame syātāmasadṛkṣopamaṃ tathā । aprasiddhopamaṃ hetuśūnyaṃ ca niralaṃkṛti ।। aślīlaṃ ca viruddhaṃ ca tathā sahacaracyutam ।
evamaṣṭādaśa proktā doṣā arthasamāśrayāḥ ।। eṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । samudāyārthaśūnyaṃ yadapārthaṃ tat prakīrtyate । kutaḥ śuṣyadapā nadyaḥ kā vārtā colamaṇḍale ।
phaṇāḥ sahasraṃ śeṣasya bhāraḥ kati kulācalāḥ ।। atra na kaścidvākyārthaḥ pratīyate । atha vyartham । yat prayojanaśūnyaṃ syāt tad vyarthaṃ parikīrtyate ।।
nirmalaṃ kulamudvelaṃ śauryaṃ vaḥ prathitaṃ yaśaḥ । kimityandhrapateḥ pādapīṭhaṃ pāṇḍyairna sevyate ।। atra nirmalaṃ kulamityādipraśaṃsā sevā kartavyetyupadeśe nopayujyate । athaikārtham ।
uktābhinnārthakaṃ yat syādekārthaṃ tannigadyate । viśīrṇaṃ śatadhā ceto mūrcchitān vīkṣya bālakān । śiśūn niścetanān dṛṣṭvā khaṇḍitaṃ śataśo manaḥ ।। atra pūrvottarārdhayorabhinnārthatvam ।
atha sasaṃśayam । vākyārthasaṃśayo yatra tat sasaṃśayamiṣyate ।। karikumbhau stanāvadya jayatāṃ kṣāmatāṃ gatau । latā vapuḥ śriyaḥ strīṇāṃ hasantu mlānatāṃ gatāḥ ।।
atra karikumbhayoḥ stanayośca latānāṃ vapuḥ śriyāṃ ca kartṛkarmatvasaṃśayaḥ । athāpakramam । yatra pūrvāparībhāvavihatistadapakramam । hanta vyādāya vaktrāṇi nidrāntyantarvaṇaṃ striyaḥ ।
tṛṇaistatpatitairasmān śikṣayantyastathākramam ।। atra nidrottarakālīnamukhyādānasya pūrvakālatvamuktamityapakramatvam । atha bhinnam । saṃbandhavarjitaṃ yat syāt tadbhinnaṃ parikīrtyate ।।
nūnaṃ phāleṣu lāṭānāṃ na dhātrā likhitā lipiḥ । yadasmākaṃ kuṭumbāni viṣīdanti marusthale ।। atra marusthalanivāsaviṣādasya phālasthalagatalipyabhāvasya ca na saṃbandhaḥ । athātimātram ।
yat sarvalokātītaṃ tadatimātraṃ prakīrtyate । mā bhūdekārṇavaṃ viśvamiti saṃkocitāśrubhiḥ । araṇye lāṭanārībhirasaṃkhyā nimnagāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। atrāśrubhirjagadekārṇavamityayuktiḥ ।
atha paruṣam । atikrūrārthasahitaṃ paruṣaṃ parikīrtyate ।। dāvānalendhanaṃ sadyaḥ kriyantāmarbhakā ime ।। atra palāni yācamānān śiśūnuddiśyātiparuṣoktiḥ ।
atha virasam । aprastutarasaṃ yat tadvirasaṃ parikīrtyate । candrānanāḥ kaṭākṣairnaḥ paśyatāmṛtavarṣibhiḥ । śocitvālamiti kliṣṭāḥ kirātaiścolasubhruvaḥ ।।
atra puruṣaviyogakhinnānāṃ strīṇāṃ vanacaraiḥ saṃbhogaprārthanaṃ virasam । atha hīnopamam । hīnaṃ yatropamānaṃ syāt taddhi hīnopamaṃ matam ।। śunakairiva sāraṅgā bhavadbhirnihatā dviṣaḥ ।
kva gataṃ pauruṣaṃ tadvaḥ kānanaikanivāsinām ।। atra śunakairiva bhavadbhiriti hīnopamam । athādhikopamam । yatropamānamadhikaṃ tad bhavedadhikopamam ।
amī pāresarastīraṃ bakā niścalamūrtayaḥ । maharṣaya ivāsmābhiradya sopadravāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। atra bakā maharṣaya ivetyadhikopamam । athāsadṛśopamam ।
yadatulyopamānaṃ tad bhavedasadṛśopamam ।। eṣa vindhyācalaḥ sāndrakuñjoccalitanirjharaḥ । phālekṣaṇasphuradvahniśikhāṭopa iveśvaraḥ ।। atra kuñjoccalitanirjharasya vindhyācalasya phālekṣaṇaspuradvahnerīśvarasya ca mitho na sādṛśyam ।
athāprasiddhopamam । aprasiddhopamānaṃ yadaprasiddhopamaṃ matam । bāṣpāmbuklinnanetrāṇi mukhānyaṅgamṛgīdṛśām । himadūṣitapatrāṇi kumudānīva nirmudām ।।
atra mukhānāṃ kumudānyupamānatayā kaviloke na prasiddhāni । atha hetuśūnyam । hetorvinārthakathanaṃ hetuśūnyaṃ pracakṣate ।। mudhānudhāvanaṃ jātaṃ mārge asmin mauktikāṅkite ।
anveṣṭumanyato yāmi padavīyaṃ na subhruvaḥ ।। atra subhruvaḥ padavīyaṃ na bhavatīti heturnoktaḥ । atha niralaṃkṛti । alaṃkāreṇa rahitaṃ niralaṃkāramucyate ।
āghrāya surabheryonimunmukhaidīrghamehanaiḥ । mahokṣerlambamānāṇḍairviṣvag vyākulitaṃ vanam ।। atra na kaścidalaṃkāraḥ । ślādhyaviśeṣaṇābhāvāt na svābhāvoktiḥ ।
athāślīlam । aślīlārthasya kathanamaślīlaṃ parikīrtyate ।। asyāpi pūrvamevodāharaṇam । atha viruddham ।
viruddhaṃ deśakālādiviruddhaṃ bahudhocyate । diśyuttarasyāṃ nedīyānudvelo lavaṇārṇavaḥ । marudeśe api gaṅgā naḥ pipāsāṃ śāmayiṣyati ।। atra diśyuttarasyāṃ lavaṇārṇava iti digvirodhaḥ ।
marau gaṅgeti deśavirodhaḥ । araṇyamahiṣodagraviṣāṇodarajanmanām । mahatyarghe api muktānāṃ striyo muktāvibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। atra mahiṣaviṣāṇebhyo muktānāṃ janmeti lokavirodhaḥ ।
evaṃ viruddhāntaramapyudāhāryam । atha sahacarabhraṣṭam । mataṃ sahacarabhraṣṭamatulyānāṃ nibandhane ।। śāntyā śrutaṃ hriyā nārī manmathena ratotsavaḥ ।
śrutena dhiṣaṇā vanyavṛttyā jīvanti śātravāḥ ।। atra śrutadhiṣaṇābhyāṃ nārīratotsavayorapakṛṣṭatvāt sahacarabhraṣṭam । evaṃ doṣāntarāṇi yathāsaṃbhavamūhyāni । rasabhāvādīnāṃ svaśabdavācyatā duṣṭaiva ।।
doṣaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam । ।। atha guṇaprakaraṇam ।। atha guṇā nirūpyante । śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatā mādhuryaṃ sukumāratā ।
arthavyaktirudāratvaṃ tathā kāntirudāttatā ।। ojaḥ suśabdatā preyānaurjityamatha vistaraḥ । samādhiḥ saukṣmyagāmbhīrye saṃkṣepo bhāvikaṃ tathā ।। saṃmitatvaṃ tathā prauḍhī rītiruktirgatistathā ।
caturviṃśatirete syurguṇāḥ kāvyaprakāśakāḥ ।। eṣāṃ madhye keṣāṃcid doṣaparihārakatvena guṇatvam । keṣāṃcit svata evotkarṣahetutvād guṇatvam । tatra ye svata eva cārutvātiśayahetavaste paramutkṛṣṭāḥ । duṣṭatvaparihārahetūnāṃ guṇatvaṃ na sarvasaṃmatam । ye tu doṣābhāvatayā guṇatvamicchanti teṣāmeva saukumāryādayo guṇatvena saṃmatāḥ । śrutikaṭurūpadoṣanirākaraṇāya saukumāryaṃ saṃmatam । grāmyadoṣanirākaraṇāya kāntiḥ svīkṛtā । apuṣṭārthanirākaraṇāyārthavyaktirmatā । nyūnādhikapadanirākaraṇāya saṃmitatvaṃ matam । anucitārthanirākaraṇārthamudāttatā svīkṛtā । visaṃdhinirākaraṇāya aurjityaṃ matam । patatprakarṣanirākaraṇāya rītiriṣṭā । kliṣṭaparihārāya prasādo mataḥ । aślīlaparihārārthamuktiḥ svīkṛtā । cyutasaṃskāraparihārārthaṃ sauśabdyamiṣṭam । prakramabhaṅganirākaraṇāya samatā matā । paruṣadoṣanivṛttyarthaṃ preyān mataḥ । evaṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ keṣāṃciddoṣaparihārakatvena guṇatvam । eṣāṃ guṇānāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca । mithaḥ saṃśliṣṭapadatā śleṣa ityabhidhīyate । bahūnāṃ padānāmekapadavadavabhāsamānatvaṃ śliṣṭatvam ।
nmāṇikyadyutirañjitāṅghrimakhilaprakhyātaśauryodayam । vyomāgāramanalpavaibhavamamuṃ stotuṃ vayaṃ neśmahe ।। atra pāṭhasamaye padānāmekavadavabhāsamānatvāt śleṣaḥ । atha prasādaḥ ।
prasiddhārthapadatvaṃ yat sa prasādo nigadyate ।। pratāparudradevo ayaṃ bhāti lakṣmīpatiḥ svayam । yenāmya locane phullapuṇḍarīkamanohare ।। atra jhaṭityarthasamarpakapadatvāt prasādaḥ ।
atha samatā । avaiṣamyeṇa bhaṇanaṃ samatā sā nigadyate । guṇā vidadhate satāṃ jagati vīrarudraprabhoḥ । viyaccarataraṅgiṇīviharadūrmimarmaspṛśaḥ ।।
atra pādacatuṣṭye api tulyavadbhaṇanāt samatvam । atha mādhuryam । yā pṛthakpadatā vākye tanmādhuryaṃ prakīrtyate ।। yaśaḥ śriyaḥ kākatibhūpaterdiśāṃ nitambabimbeṣu dukūlarītayaḥ ।
urojayormauktikahāravibhramāḥ śirassu jātīkusumasragujjvalāḥ ।। atra vākye pāṭhasamaye api pṛthakpadatvapratītermādhuryam । atha sukumāratvam । sukumārākṣaraprāyaṃ saukumāryaṃ taducyate ।
sukumāratvaṃ nāma sānusvārakomalavarṇatvam । amandānandaniṣyandasundarīvadanendubhiḥ । nagare kākatīndrasya divāpyābhāti candrikā ।। athārthavyaktiḥ ।
yattu saṃpūrṇavākyatvamarthavyaktiṃ vadanti tām ।। jātaḥ khelati vīrarudranṛpatirniḥ sīmaśauryodayaḥ । yat sākṣādavatīrya kākatikule svairaṃ samujjṛmbhate ।। atrārthapratipādane vākyasya nirākāṅkṣatayā paripūrṇatvādarthavyaktiḥ ।
atyujjvalatvaṃ bandhasya kāvye kāntiritīṣyate । kṣoṇīreṇubhare nabhasyatibhṛśaṃ bhūvibhramaṃ bibhrati । gāḍhaṃ gūḍhatamā ca gautamanadī pātālagaṅgāyate ।। athaudāryam ।
vikaṭākṣarabandhatvamāryairaudāryamiṣyate ।। masrasyoccaistarāsthyutkaṣaṇabhavakaṭatkāraraudrāgradaṃṣṭrān । kurvantyāyodhanorvyo bhayamavanibhṛtāmandhrasainyena sṛṣṭāḥ ।। athodāttatā ।
ślāghyairviśeṣaṇairyogo yastu sā syādudāttatā । bṛṃhamāṇagajākīrṇā hreṣamāṇahayākulā । saṃkrīḍatsyandanā kṣveḍabhaṭā rudravibhoścamūḥ ।। athaujaḥ ।
ojaḥ samāsabhūyastvam ।। bhṛṅgaśreṇinibaddhajhaṃkṛtikalāvācālitaprāṅgaṇāḥ । modante bhuvi vīrarudranṛpatervidvadgṛhaśreṇayaḥ ।। atha suśabdatā ।
supāṃ tiṅāṃ ca vyutpattiḥ sauśabdyaṃ parikīrtyate । rakṣan suprajasaḥ prajāstribhuvanakṣemaṅkaraprakriyaḥ । bhūmnā saṃcarate adya kākatikule rudrāvatāro hariḥ ।। atha preyaḥ ।
preyaḥ priyatarākhyānaṃ cāṭūktau yadvidhīyate ।। prāgalbhyaṃ tvayi, pauruṣaṃ tvayi, kalāsaṃpattvayi, śrīstvayi । śrīmatkākatinātha ! pālaya bhuvaṃ vairiñcakalpān śatam ।। athairjityam ।
aurjitvaṃ gāḍhabandhatvam । kṣudrakṣatriyapakṣaśikṣaṇavidhau protkṣiptakaukṣeyakāḥ । garjaddurjanagarvaparvatabhidādambholayaḥ kelayaḥ ।। atha samādhiḥ ।
samādhiranyadharmāṇāṃ yadanyatrādhiropaṇam ।। cāṭūktyā mānayantī muhuramaranadīṃ candramagre hasantī । lokeṣu triṣvamīṣu prabhavati mahatī vīrarudrasya kīrttiḥ ।। atha vistaraḥ ।
samarthanaprapañcoktiruktasyārthasya vistaraḥ । śrotuṃ bahvabhinandituṃ ca phaṇināmekaḥ kṣamo nāyakaḥ । stā eva śrutayaḥ phaṇā daśaśatānyatyadbhutāndolane ।। atha saṃmitatvam ।
yāvadarthapadatvaṃ tu saṃmitatvamudāhṛtam ।। kākatīyanarendrasya kīrtticandanacarcanam । digaṅganā vitanvanti vataṃsīkṛtatadguṇāḥ ।। atha gāmbhīryam ।
dhvanimattā tu gāmbhīryam । viṣaṃ kaukṣeyake gaṅgā kīrttau digvasanaṃ ripau । indurmukhe ca rudrasya kākatīyasya dṛśyate ।। atra śaṅkarasya kaṇṭhe viṣaṃ, maulau gaṅgā, kaṭisthale digvastraṃ, śirasi candra iti dhvanyate ।
atha saṃkṣepaḥ । saṃkṣiptārthābhidhānaṃ yat tat saṃkṣepaḥ prakīrtyate ।। vaṃśo asti kākatīyānāṃ tatrāsan bahavo nṛpāḥ । teṣāṃ bhāgyavivarto ayaṃ vīrarudro nareśvaraḥ ।।
atrātivistarakathanayogyārthasya saṃkṣepokteḥ saṃkṣepaḥ । atha saukṣmyam । antaḥ saṃjalparūpatvaṃ śabdānāṃ saukṣmyamucyate । adhyadhaḥ parisaṃśliṣṭāḥ ṣṭhākṛñbhūdhātavaḥ sadā ।
vartante kākatīyendre kartaryanyatra karmaṇi ।। atrādhitiṣṭhatyadhaḥ karoti paribhavatītyantaḥ saṃjalparūpatvāt saukṣmyaṃ bhavati । atha prauḍhiḥ । prauḍhirukteḥ parīpāka iti kāvyavido viduḥ ।।
daityāreḥ pratibimbanaṃ suragirerindoḥ samuttejanam । svardhenoriti tarkayanti kavayaḥ śrīvīrarudraprabhum ।। athoktiḥ । syāduktiṃ tāṃ kavayo viduḥ ।
diṭṭhā kamalāsattī raṇṇo tuha suhaa cittacariatsa । bhāsanto vi tumaṃ taṃ kuvalaalacchiṃ pasāhesi ।। (।dṛṣṭā kamalāsaktī rājñastava subhaga citracaritasya । bhāsvānapi tvaṃ tāṃ kuvalayalakṣmīṃ prasādhayasi ।।)
atha rītiḥ । yathopakramanirvāho rītirityabhidhīyate ।। ṣaḍ guṇān sevate rājā ṣaḍ ripūnavamanyate । ṣaḍ darśanānyupādatte ṣaḍ balāni ca vīkṣate ।।
atha bhāvikam । bhavato vākyavṛttiryā bhāvikaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।। svāmiṃstāta kulottaṃsa vīrarudra jagatprabho । putriṇāṃ dhurameṣo ahaṃ putreṇāropitastvayā ।।
atra premarūpabhāvavaśāt svamiṃstāteti vākyavṛttiḥ । atha gatiḥ । gatirnāma suramyatvaṃ svarārohāvarohayoḥ ।। mahobhirniḥ sīmairdinakarakarāṭopapaṭubhiḥ ।
dadhatsvapyudvelatyarinṛpamanassveva satatam ।। atra pūrvārdhe dīrghākṣaraprāyatvāt svarasyārohaḥ । uttarārdhe avarohaḥ । eteṣāṃ guṇānāmarthagatatvamapi kecidicchanti । prācāmācāryāṇāṃ matena saṃghaṭanāśrayatvameva guṇānām । taduktamalaṃkārasarvasve"saṃghaṭanādharmatvena śabdārthadharmatvena ca guṇālaṃkārāṇāṃ vyavasthānam'; iti । anayaiva bhaṅgyā guṇālaṃkārāṇāṃ nirūpitaḥ svarūpabhedaḥ । anyathā svarūpabhedasya durnirūpatvāt । kāvyaśobhākaratvameva guṇālaṃkārasvarūpatvam । taduktaṃ rud'rabhaṭṭena' "yo hetuḥ kāvyaśobhāyāḥ so alaṃkāraḥ prakīrtyate । guṇo api tādṛśo jñeyo doṣaḥ syāt tadviparyayaḥ ।। a; iti ।
ato guṇānāṃ saṃghaṭanāśrayatvameva yuktam । guṇaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam । ।। atha śabdālaṃkāraprakaraṇam ।। alaṅkārasvarūpanirūpaṇam ।
atha guṇanirūpaṇānantaramalaṅkārā nirūpyante । alaṃkriyate aneneti cārutvaheturalaṃkāraḥ । "upaskurvanti taṃ santaṃ ye aṅgadvāreṇa saṃśritāḥ । hārādivadalaṃkārāste anuprāsopamādayaḥ ।।
a; iti । yathā karacaraṇādyavayavagatairvalayanū parādibhistattadalaṃkāratayā prasiddhairavayavyevālaṃkriyate tathā śabdārthāvayavagatairanuprāsopamādibhistattadalaṃkāratayā prasiddhairavayavībhūtaṃ kāvyamupaskriyate । āśrayāśrayibhāvenālaṃkāryālaṃkārabhāvo lokavat kāvye api saṃmataḥ । cārutvahetutve api guṇānāmalaṃkārāṇāṃ cāśrayabhedādbhedavyapadeśaḥ ।
saṃghaṭanāśrayā guṇāḥ, śabdārthāśrayāstvalaṃkārāḥ । tatra prathamaṃ śabdārthobhayagatatvena traividhyamalaṃkāravargasya । arthālaṃkārāṇāṃ cāturvidhyam; kecit pratīyamānavastavaḥ; kecit pratīyamānaupamyāḥ kecit pratīyamānarasabhāvādayaḥ; kecidasphuṭapratīyamānā iti । samāsoktiparyāyoktyā'kṣepavyājastutyupameyopamānanvayātiśayoktiparikarāprastutapraśaṃsānuktanimittaviśeṣoktiṣupratīyamānaṃ vastu kāvyopaskāratāmupayāti ।
rūpakapariṇāmasaṃdehabhrāntimadullekhāpahnavotprekṣāsmaraṇatulyayogitādīpakaprativastūpamādṛṣṭāntasahoktivyatirekanidarśanāśleṣeṣvaupamyaṃ gamyate । rasavatpreyaūrjasvisamāhitabhāvodayabhāvasaṃdhibhāvaśabalatāsu rasabhāvādirvyajyate । paviśeṣanimīlanasāmānyāsaṅgatitadguṇātadguṇavyājoktivakroktisvabhāvoktibhāvikodātteṣu sahṛdayahṛdayāhlādi sphuṭaṃ pratīyamānaṃ nāsti । ।। atretthamalaṃkārakakṣyāvibhāgaḥ ।।
sādharmyaṃ trividhambhedapradhānamabhedapradhānaṃ bhedābhedapradhānaṃ ceti । upamānopameyayoḥ svato bhinnatvācchābdametanna vāstavam । rūpakapariṇāmasaṃdehabhrāntimadullekhāpahnavānāmabhedapravānasādharmyanibandhanatvam । dīpakatulyayogitānidarśanādṛṣṭāntaprativastūpamāsahoktipratīpavyatirekāḥ bhedapradhānasādhargyanibandhanāḥ ।
upamānanvayopameyopamāsmaraṇānāṃ bhedābhedasādhāraṇasādharmyamūlatā । utprekṣātiśayoktī adhyavasāyamūle । vibhāvanāviśeṣoktiviṣamacitrāsaṅgatyanyonyavyāghātātadguṇabhāvikaviśeṣāṇāṃ virodhamūlatā । yathāsaṃkhyaparisaṃkhyārthāpattivikalpasamuccayānāṃ vākyanyāyamūlatā ।
parivṛttipratyanīkatadguṇasamādhisamasvabhāvoktyudāttavinoktayo lokavyavahāramūlāḥ । kāvyaliṅgānumānārthāntaranyāsānāṃ tarkanyāyamūlatā । kāraṇamālaikāvalīmālādīpakasārāḥ śṛṅglāvaicitryamūlāḥ । vyājoktivakroktimīlanānyapahnavamūlāni ।
samāsoktiparikarau viśeṣaṇavaicitryamūlau । ।। athālaṃkārāṇāṃ parasparavailakṣaṇya nirūpyate ।। āropagarbhatve apyāropyamāṇasya prakṛtopayogānupayogābhyāṃ pariṇāmarūpakayorbhedaḥ । āropaviṣayasyāropyamāṇarūpasaṃbhavāsaṃbhavābhyāmullekharūpakayorbhedaḥ ।
āropaviṣayasya saṃdehabhrānt yapahnavaiḥ sandehabhrāntimadapahnavānāṃ parasparaṃ bhedaḥ । sādharmyamūlatve api tulyayogitādīpakanidarśanāvyatirekadṛṣṭāntebhyaḥ sādharmyasya vācyatvādupamānanvayopameyopamā bhidyante । sādharmyasya vācyatvagamyatvābhyāmupameyopamāprativastūpamayorbhedaḥ । vastuprativastubimbapratibimbabhāvābhyāṃ prativastūpamādṛṣṭāntayorbhedaḥ ।
prastutāprastutānāṃ vyastasamastatvābhyāṃ tulyayogitādīpakayorbhedaḥ ।। upamānasya prasiddhatvāprasiddhatvābhyāmupamotprekṣayorbhedaḥ । arthasāmyaśabdasāmyābhyāmupamāśleṣayorbhedaḥ । upamānopameyayorbhedābhedābhyāmupamānanvayayorbhedaḥ ।
upamānopameyabhāvasya paryāyayaugapadyābhyāmupameyopamānanvayayorbhedaḥ । aprastutasya vācyatvagamyatvābhyāmaprastutapraśaṃsāsamāsoktyorbhedaḥ । vācyavyaṅgyayoḥ prastutatve paryāyoktiḥ vācyasyāprastutatve aprastutapraśaṃsā । vyāptipakṣadharmatādyabhāvāt kāvyaliṅgasyānumānādbhedaḥ ।
sādhāraṇaguṇayogād bhedānupalabdhau sāmānyam । utkṛṣṭaguṇayogānnyūnaguṇatirodhāne mīlanam । anyavyavacchede tātparyābhāvāduttarālaṃkārasya parisaṃkhyāto bhedaḥ । kākatālīyatayā kāryasādhane kāraṇāntaropanipāte samādhiḥ ।
ahamahamikayā kāryasādhane bahūnāṃ kāraṇānāmudyame dvitīyaḥ samuccayaḥ । nihnavasya vācyatvagamyatvābhyāmapahnavavyājastutyorbhedaḥ । anyeṣāṃ bhedaḥ spaṣṭa eva । yadyapi vyājoktimīlasāmānyeṣu kathaṃcit sādṛśyamasti; tathāpyavivakṣitatvānna sādṛśyamūleṣu gaṇanā ।
śabdālaṃkārā nirūpyante । athālaṃkārasvarūpavibhāgānantaraṃ śabdārthayormadhye śabdasyārthaṃ pratītyantaraṅgatvāt prathamaṃ śabdālaṃkārā nirūpyante । bhavedavyavadhānena dvayorvyañjanayugmayoḥ । āvṛttiryatra sa budhaiśchekānuprāsa iṣyate ।।
yatrāvyavahitayorvyañjanayugmayordvayoḥ paunaruktyaṃ tatra chekānuprāsaḥ । mahīmahīnavibhave dhatte kṣemaṃkare kare । rājanyajanyavijayī rājā rājadguṇodayaḥ ।। vṛttyanuprāsaḥ ।
ekadviprabhṛtīnāṃ tu vyañjanānāṃ yathā bhavet । punaruktirasau nāma vṛttyanuprāsa iṣyate ।। re re kṣudramahīkṣitaḥ ! kṣaṇamitaḥ śrīkākatikṣmāpater- vīkṣadhvaṃ dhvajinīṃ durīkṣasubhaṭāṃ protkṣiptakaukṣeyakaiḥ । yotsyadhve yadi labhyamakṣayapadaṃ kāntārapakṣo vṛthā kṣmābhṛtkukṣicarattarakṣunikarāt tatrātmarakṣā kutaḥ ।।
yamakam । yamakaṃ paunaruktye tu svaravyañjanayugmayoḥ ।। chekānuprāse vṛttyanuprāse ca svarapaunaruktyamānuṣaṅgikam । yamake tu sasvarayoḥ vyañjanayugmayoḥ āvṛttiḥ ।
tasyādimadhyāntagatatvena bahavo bhedāḥ । atra diṅmātramudāhriyate । pratāpaḥ kākatīndrasya mahāmahimatejasaḥ । śriyaṃ dadhāti padmeṣṭamahāmahimatejasaḥ ।।
yatrārthaḥ pramukhe kiṃcit bhāsate punaruktavat । punaruktavadābhāso alaṃkāraḥ sa satāṃ mataḥ ।। yatrārthaḥ punaruktavadābhāsate, anvayavelāyāmanyathā bhavati, sa punaruktavadābhāso alaṃkāraḥ । arthālaṅkāratve apyasya śabdapaunaruktyāśritatvācchabdālaṃkāraprastāve lakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ।
jiṣṇurindraḥ kṣitibhujāṃ śrīpatiḥ puruṣottamaḥ । bhāsvān sūryasphurattejāḥ kākatīndro virājate ।। athobhayapaunaruktyālaṃkāraḥ kathyate । lāṭānuprāsaḥ ।
śabdārthayoḥ paunaruktyaṃ yatra tātparyabhedavat । sa kāvyatātparyavidāṃ lāṭānuprāsa iṣyate ।। yatra śabdārthayostātparyabhedamātraṃ na svarūpabhedastatra lāṭānuprāsaḥ । guṇā guṇāste gaṇyante ye rudranṛpamāśritāḥ ।
nītirnītirasau tasya lakṣmīrlaṃkṣmīśca kathyate ।। citrālaṃkāraḥ padmabandhādiḥ । padmādyākārahetutve varṇānāṃ citramucyate । ādigrahaṇāccakrabandhādayaḥ ।
yānāsaktāsanasthā sukhayatu kamalābhyāsasujñānamāyā । yāge saktā ratijñā sukṛtiṣu phalitagrāmasasyāyatāyā ।। dikṣvārabdhanijapratāpajanitāṃ bhākṛddhurāṃ yacchataḥ । rājatpālanamoditātmani bhuje yogyāśritatvād dharā ।।
atra cakrabandhe vaijanāthakṛtivīrarudrayaśa iti pratīyate । vidyāvarye abhinetaryuruharicaritaṃ viśvavistārabhāji । vanyairadhvanyavāri kṣatimati vividhe jantubhiḥ sthānabhājaḥ ।। śabdālaṃkāraprakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।
।। atha arthālaṃkārāḥ ।। tatra prathamamanekālaṃkārabījabhūtatvādupamā nirūpyate । svataḥ siddhena bhinnena saṃmatena ca dharmataḥ । sāmyamanyena varṇyasya vācyaṃ cedekadopamā ।।
yatra svataḥ siddhena svato bhinnena sahṛdayasaṃmatenāprakṛtena saha prakṛtasya dharmataḥ sādṛśyamekadā vācyaṃ ced bhavati tatropamā । svataḥ siddhenetyanenotprekṣāvyāvṛttiḥ । utprekṣāyāmaprasiddhasyāpyupamānatvasaṃbhavāt । prācāṃ bhumībhujāṃ yaśaḥ pidadhatī koṭīndutulyadyutiḥ । railokyāṭṭahāsaprabhave kakubhāṃ prānteṣu vidyotate ।। atra prabhāśabdo jātivacanaḥ । trailokyāṭṭahāsaprabhāyāḥ kaviprauḍhoktisiddhatvānnopamāśaṅkāvakāśaḥ । svato bhinnenetyanenānanvayanyāvṛttiḥ । ananvaye ekasyaivopamānopameyatvasaṃbhavāt । tathā hi
santu loke suvarṇādriratnākarasudhākarāḥ । tathāpi vīrarudro ayaṃ vīrarudra iva svayam ।। saṃmatenetyanena nyūnopamādivyāvṛttiḥ । yathā udanvāniva gambhīraḥ suvarṇādririvonnataḥ ।
diṅmahebha iva kṣoṇīdhaureyaḥ kākatīśvaraḥ ।। atra samudrasuvarṇādridiggajānāmupamānatvaṃ yogyamityupamaiveyam । dharmata ityanena śleṣālaṃkāravailakṣaṇyam । śleṣe śabdasāmyamātramabhyupagataṃ na guṇakriyāsāmyam । tathā hi nīrājayantyadhrapurīramaṇyaḥ pradīpajālairvaravīrarudram । candrānanā gotrapatiṃ rajanyastārāgaṇairmerumiva sphuradbhiḥ ।।
atra pratāparudraṃ purastriyo nīrājayanti meruṃ rajanya iveti nopamā । gotrapatimiti viśeṣaṇārthasya sāmyābhāvāt । gotraśabdena rājapakṣe kulapratītiḥ, merupakṣe parvapratītiḥ । tathā candrānanā iti strīpakṣe candra iva ānanaṃ yāsāmiti samāsaḥ । rātripakṣe candra evānanaṃ yāsāmiti śabdamātrasāmyena nopamāprāptiḥ । anyena varṇyasya sāmyamityanena pratīpālaṃkāro vyāvartyate । tathā hi loko ayamaviśeṣajñaḥ kiṃ kurmaḥ kasya kathyate । yat kākatinarendreṇa sumerurupamīyate ।।
atrāprakṛtasya meroḥ prakṛtena rājñā sādṛśyamiti pratīpālaṃkāro nopamā । ekadā sāmyamityanena upameyopamāvyāvṛttiḥ । upameyopamāyāmupamānopameyayoranekadā sāmyapratipādanam । dharmo artha iva pūrṇaśrīrartho dharma iva sthitaḥ । kāmastāviva tau kāma iva rudranareśvare ।।
atra dharmo artha iva artho dharma ivetyanekadā ivaśabdadvayena dharmārthakāmānāṃ sādṛśyaṃ pratipādyata ityupameyopamā । vācyamityanena pratīyamānaupamyānāṃ rūpakasaṃdehabhrāntimadullekhāpahnavatulyayogitādīpakaprativastūpamādṛṣṭāntasahoktivyatirekanidarśanānāṃ vailakṣaṇyam । tathā hi pratāparudranṛpatermaṇḍalāgravidhuṃtudaḥ । akhaṇḍavikramoddāmo grasate rājamaṇḍalam ।। atra maṇḍalāgravidhuṃtudayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyānyathānupapattyā sādṛśyaṃ lakṣyata iti nopamā; kiṃ tu rūpakālaṅkāraḥ ।
kimeṣa daśamaḥ prajāpatirapūrvasargakramaḥ । cirāditi vitarkyate jagati kākatīndro janaiḥ ।। atra kākatīśvarasya haritpatiprabhṛtīnāṃ ca parasparābhedapratīteḥ saṃdehanibandhanānyathānupapattyā sādṛśyamākṣipyate; tataḥ saṃdehālaṃkāraḥ । kākatīyavibhoḥ kīrttivibhave vyāptarodasi ।
divāpi candrikābuddhyā cakorā yānti nirvṛtim ।। atra kīrttivibhave candrikābuddhiḥ candrikāsādṛśyaṃ vinā na saṃbhavatīti sādṛśyākṣepāt bhrāntimadalaṅkāraḥ । śauryātibhūmikhanirityarivīravargāḥ । śrīkākatīndranagarīmaniśaṃ stuvanti ।।
atra nagaryāṃ tattatpadārthatāropaḥ sādṛśyādṛte na saṃbhavatīti sādṛśyakalpanādullekhālaṃkāraḥ । vīrarudrasya bhūpālajayahomaṃ vitanvataḥ । dhūmarajiriyaṃ bhāti na camūreṇurutthitā ।। atrotthitāṃ camūreṇumavalokya dhūmapaṅktirityapahnavenāropaḥ sādṛśyamūla eveti sādṛśyākṣepādapahnavaḥ । evaṃ tulyayogitādiṣvapi sādṛśyasya gamyatvānnopamāśaṅkā । ataḥ sarvebhyaḥ sādṛśyamūlebhyo vilakṣaṇeyamupamā ।
sā prathamaṃ dvidhā - pūrṇā luptā ceti । upamānopameyasādhāraṇadharmasādṛśyapratipādakānāṃ caturṇāṃ prayoge pūrṇā । ekasya dvayostrayāṇāṃ vā lope luptā । pūrṇā dvividhāśrautī ārthī ceti । sākṣātsādṛśyapratipādakayathevādiśabdānāṃ prayoge śrautī । dharmivyavadhānena sādṛśyapratipādakānāṃ sadṛśasaṃkāśanīkāśapratīkāśādiśabdānāṃ prayoge ārthī । dve api vākyasamāsataddhitagatatvena trivedhe । evaṃ pūrṇopamā ṣaṭprakārā । luptopamā ekonaviṃśatibhedā । "tena tulyaṃ kriyā ced vatiḥ'; iti sadṛśārthe vihitasya vaterupādāne ārthī । "tatra tasyeva'; iti ivārthe vihitasya vaterupādāne śrautī । ata eva sādṛśyārthe vihitasya vateḥ prayoge dharmopādāna evānvayasaukaryādanuktadharmā taddhitagā śrautī luptā nāsti । kalpabādiprayoge tvārthyeva । athodāharaṇāni । vākyagā pūrṇā śrautī yathā tretāyāṃ raghunāyakasya mahitakhyātau bhujāyāṃ yathā ।
visrabdhādya kalau tathaiva ramate kṣoṇyandhrabharturbhuje ।। bhāsvānivodyannudayādrilambī bhadrāsanastho varavīrarudraḥ । utpaśyatāmandhrapurījanānāṃ netrābjajāḍyaṃ śamayatyaśeṣam ।। atra bhāsvāniveti ivena saha nityasamāsaḥ । taddhitagā pūrṇā śrautī yathā
kūrmavaccheṣavad gotragirivaddiṅmahebhavat । bhuje pratāparudrasya dhurīṇe bhāti medinī ।। taistairmahīpālanasaṃvidhānaistaistaiḥ prajārañjanavaibhavaiśca । virājate saṃprati kākatīyalakṣmīpatirdāśaratheḥ samānaḥ ।।
tādṛkpālanasāmarthyasaṃpadā kākatīśvaraḥ । haridīśvarasaṃkāśaḥ śāsti madhyamaviṣṭapam ।। hemācalavadaunnatye gāmbhīrye kṣīrasindhuvat । pratāpe bhānuvad bhāti vīrarudranareśvaraḥ ।।
eṣūdāharaṇeṣūpameyopamānasādhāraṇadharmasādṛśyapratipādakāni catvāri nibaddhānīti pūrṇatvam । atha luptopamāyā udāharaṇāni । yathā rucāṃ svāmini cakravākyo yathā ca nīhārarucau cakoryaḥ । yathā prasūnastabake bhramaryastathā prajāḥ kākativīrarudre ।।
pratāparudradevasya pādapīṭhīmanāratam । ārādhayanti bhūpālāḥ praṇatā devatāmiva ।। kākatikṣmāpaterjaitraprasthānapaṭahadhvanim । tulyaṃ dambholinirghoṣaiḥ śṛṇvantyarimahībhṛtaḥ ।।
śaśvatpurīmekaśilābhidhānāṃ vasvokasārāsadṛśīmavekṣya । namanti bhūpā bhuvi kākatīyarājyapratiṣṭhāṃ bahumanyamānāḥ ।। pratāparudranṛpaterjaganmahitatejasaḥ । kandarpakalpamākāraṃ paśyantyandhrapurandhrayaḥ ।।
eṣūdāharaṇeṣu dharmasyānupādānam । dugdhārṇavīyatvambhodhīn kailāsīyati bhūdharān । pratāparudradevasya yaśovaiśadyavaibhavam ।। dvīpeṣvabdhiṣu dīrghikīyati haritsvekāntagehīyati ।
prāsādīyati vīrarudranṛpateḥ sphāraḥ pratāpodayaḥ ।। darśaṃ kṣīrapayonidhiṃ priyasuhṛddarśaṃ giriṃ rājatam । darśaṃ khelati vīrarudranṛpateḥ kīrttirjagadvyāpinī ।। nṛpeṣu śikṣāvidhidaṇḍacāraṃ kāntāsu puṣpāyudhadhanvacāram ।
prajāsu cālambanayaṣṭicāraṃ caratyayaṃ rudranarendrakhaḍgaḥ ।। sudhāpravāhati satāmasatāṃ kālakūṭati । vīrarudranarendrasya guṇajyotsnāvijṛmbhitam ।। eṣūdāharaṇeṣu dvayoranupādānam । ambhodhīn dugdhārṇavīyatītyatra karmakyaci dugdhārṇavāniva karotīti, gotraśikhareṣu krīḍādrīyatītyādhārakyaci krīḍādrīṣviva vartata iti, candramātmajadarśaṃ paśyantīti karmaṇamuli ātmajamiva paśyantīti, śikṣāvidhidaṇḍacāraṃ caratīti kartṛṇamuli śikṣāvidhidaṇḍa iva caratīti ivaśabdo antargata iti tasya luptatvam । anuktadharmīvadiḥ kartṛkyacā luptā yathā
jyotsnīyanti sudhīyanti candanīyanti sarvataḥ । pratāparudranṛpateḥ śubhrāḥ kīrttermahormayaḥ ।। atra kīrttīnāṃ svarūpamupameyam । śeṣāyate mahīṃ voḍhuṃ kalpaśākhāyate arthinām ।
pratāparudradordaṇḍaḥ kāladaṇḍāyate dviṣām ।। guṇaśreṇīślāghāpihitaharidīśānayaśasaḥ । kriyante yadvidvajjanamaṇigṛhaprāṅgaṇabhuvaḥ ।। vīrarudrasamo rājā nāsti nāstyeva bhūtale ।
yasya dharmānubandhena kaliḥ kṛtayugīkṛtaḥ ।। kīrttyā kārttikakaumudīdhavalayā tulyaṃ na kiṃcit kvacit । kaṇṭhāliṅganamīśiturvitanute nīrandhramadreḥ sutā ।। na bhāvi trailokye kimapi jayinaḥ kākativibhoḥ ।
prakāśante naktaṃdivamuditarociḥ paricayāḥ ।। pūrvodāharaṇadvaye vadānyo nānyo astīti rājeti śabdābhyāṃ vitaraṇaśīlatvaṃ prajārañjakatvaṃ ca sādharmyamuktam । anantarodāharaṇadvaye dharmasyāpyanupādānamiti bhedaḥ । eṣu caturṣūdāharaṇeṣu na pratīpālaṃkāraśaṅkā । upamānasyākṣepābhāvāt; upameyasyādhikyāvivakṣaṇācca । yatropameyasyādhikyavivakṣayopamānatvamucyate tatraiva pratīpālaṃkāraḥ । anuktevādiḥ samāsagā luptā yathā asatāmuṣṇabhānūṣṇaṃ satāṃ śītāṃśuśītalam । pratāparudradevasya caritaṃ viśvamaṅgaḷam ।।
kākatīndro raṇe bhāti bhīmasenaparākramaḥ । kiṃtvaduḥ śāsanāḥ sarve yasya pratyarthipārthivāḥ ।। atra bhīmasenasya parākrama iva parākramo yasya saḥ bhīmasenaparākrama iti dharmevādyupamāluptā । iti luptopamā darśitāḥ । atha sādhāraṇadharmopādāne dvaividhyam । dharmasya sakṛdupamānopameyagatatvena nirdeśaḥ, ubhayagatatvena pṛthagupādānaṃ ca । pṛthagupādānaṃ ca vastuprativastubhāvena bimbapratibimbabhāvena ca dvividham । ekasyārthasya śabdadvayenābhidhānaṃ vastuprativastubhāvaḥ । dvayorarthayordvirupādānaṃ bimbapratibimbabhāvaḥ । sakṛnnirdeśo yathā
nṛpāḥ praṇatamūrdhānaḥ sevante kākatīśvaram । asādhūnāṃ vinetāraṃ guruṃ śiṣyā ivābhitaḥ ।। atra nareśvarāṇāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca praṇatamūrdhāna iti sakṛdeva sādharmyamuktam । yathā asādhūnāṃ vinetāramiti rājño gurośca tulyadharmatvaṃ sakṛdevoktam । vastuprativastubhāvena dvidhā nirdeśo yathā vaṃśo ayaṃ kākatīyānāṃ vīrarudreṇa bhūṣitaḥ ।
anvavāyaḥ kakutsthānāṃ rāmeṇeva pariṣkṛtaḥ ।। atra bhūṣitapariṣkṛtaśabdābhyāmekārthapratītervastuprativastubhāvaḥ । sphuracchravetātapatraśrīḥ kākatīyanareśvaraḥ । hāṭakādririvābhāti śṛṅgasaṅgīndumaṇḍalaḥ ।।
atra śvetātapatracandramaṇḍalayoḥ sādṛśyena kākatīndrasuvarṇācalayoḥ sādṛśyamiti bimbapratibimbabhāvaḥ । aparamapi dvaividhyamasyālaṃkārasyasamastavastuviṣayā ekadeśavartinī ceti । yathākramaṃ dvayorudāharaṇam vibhāti bhūrdyairiva kākatīndrapurī virājatyamarāvatīva । paurāḥ prathante tridaśā ivarddhi dhatte marutvāniva vīrarudraḥ ।।
eṣā samastavastuviṣayā । ekadeśavartinī yathā dvipaiścaradbhirdharaṇīdharairvā turaṅgamaśreṇibhirūrmibharvā । nānāyudhairvyālajalagrahairvā balaṃ triliṅgādhipaterdurāpam ।। atra triliṅgādhipaterbalaṃ samudra ivetyarthāt pratīterekadeśavartitvam । mālārūpeṇāpyayamalaṃkāro dṛśyate । yathā
kundati kumudati haṃsati hārati harati kṣapākarati । kailāsati ca yaśaḥ śrīvaiśadyaṃ vīrarudrasya ।। atraikasyopameyasyānekopamānadarśanāt mālātvam । upamāyāṃ bhedābhedasādhāraṇasya sādharmyasya prayojakatvam । evaṃ bhedāntaraṃ yathāsaṃbhavamudāhāryam ।। ananvayālaṃkāraḥ ।
ekasyaivopamānopameyatve ananvayo mataḥ ।। yatra dvitīyasabrahmacārinivṛttyarthamekasyaivopamānopameyabhāvo nibadhyate asāvananvayālaṃkāraḥ । yathā santu loke suvarṇādriratnākarasudhākarāḥ । tathāpi vīrarudro ayaṃ vīrarudra iva svayam ।।
upameyopamālaṅkāraḥ । paryāyeṇa dvayostasminnupameyopamā matā ।। tasminnityupamānopameyatvaparāmarśaḥ । yathā dharmo artha iva pūrṇaśrīrartho dharma iva sthitaḥ ।
kāmastāviva tau kāma iva rudranareśvare ।। smaraṇālaṃkāraḥ । sadṛśānubhavādanyasmṛtiḥ smaraṇamucyate ।। yatra sadṛśasya padārthasyānubhavena sadṛśavastvantaraparāmarśo jāyate tatra smaraṇālaṃkāraḥ । yathā
rājñā pratāparudreṇa pāliteyaṃ vasuṃdharā । hariścandranalādīnāṃ prācāṃ smarati bhūbhujām ।। prāptavatyāḥ medinyāḥ pūrvarājasmaraṇam । bhedābhedasādhāraṇasādharmyanibandhanālaṃkārāḥ pradarśitāḥ । saṃpratyāropagarbhālaṃkāraprastāvaḥ । tatrāpi prādhānyāt prathamaṃ rūpakaṃ nirūpyate ।
rūpakālaṅkāraḥ । āropaviṣayasya syādatirohitarūpiṇaḥ । uparañjakamāropyamāṇaṃ tadrūpakaṃ matam ।। atrāropaviṣayasyetyanena adhyavasāyagarbhasya utprekṣādeḥ anāropamūlānāṃ copamādīnāṃ vyāvṛttiḥ । atirohitarūpiṇa ityanena saṃdehabhrāntimadapahnutipramukhānāṃ vyāvṛttiḥ । saṃdehālaṃkāre viṣayasya saṃdihyamānatayā tirodhānam । bhrāntimadalaṃkāre bhrāntyā viṣayatirodhānam । apahnutyalaṃkāre apahnavenāropaviṣayatirodhānam । uparañjakamityanena pariṇāmālaṃkāravyāvṛttiḥ । pariṇāme āropyamāṇasya prakṛtopayogitvenānvayo na prakṛtoparañjakatvena । ataḥ sādṛśyamūlebhyaḥ sarvebhyo vilakṣaṇaṃ rūpakam ।
tasya prathamaṃ traividhyamsāvayavaṃ, niravayavaṃ paramparitaṃ ceti । sāvayavaṃ dvividhamsamastavastuviṣayam, ekadeśavivarti ceti । niravayavaṃ dvividhamkevalaṃ mālārūpaṃ ceti । paramparitasyāpi śliṣṭanibandhanatvenāśliṣṭanibandhanatvena ca dvaividhyam । tayorapi pratyekaṃ kevalamālārūpatayā caturvidhyam । evamaṣṭavidho rūpakālaṃkāraḥ । athodāharaṇāni । yatrāvayavānāmavayavinaśca sāmastyena nirūpaṇaṃ nibadhyate, tat samastavastuviṣayaṃ rūpakam । vairikṣmāpatigarvaparvatabhidābhīmaṃ muhurgarjati । vardhante haridantareṣu jagadānandā yaśaḥ kandalāḥ ।।
yatrāvayavanirūpaṇādavayavino rūpaṇaṃ gamyate, tadekadeśavivarti rūpakam । prasādhitāśāvalayāntarālaḥ śauryākaraḥ kākativīrarudraḥ । vikasvarairvāsanayā trilokīṃ guṇaprasūnaiḥ surabhīkaroti ।। atrāvayavānāṃ guṇānāṃ prasūnasvarūpaṇena nṛpateḥ kalpaśākhitvaṃ nirūpyate । tasmādekadeśavivartitvam । yathā vā
mathitād vairivāraśerbhujāmandarabhūbhṛtā । jātā pratāparudrasya kīrttirlokān dhinotyamūn ।। atra vairijanasya vārāśitvarūpaṇena bhujasya mandarādritvarūpaṇena ca jātāyāḥ kīrttiḥ sudhātvamarthādāpatati, lokānāmamaratvaṃ cetyekadeśavivartti rūpakam । yatrāvayavirūpaṇamātre kavisaṃrambhaviśrāntistanniravayavaṃ rūpakam । avayavarūpaṇamātre api tadeva ।
nissāṇadhvanibhiḥ sphuṭaṃ pratidaladrodaḥ kaṭāhāntaraiḥ । bhītāḥ kākativīrarudranṛpateḥ pratyarthinaḥ pārthivāḥ ।। atra rodasaḥ kaṭāhatvaṃ rūpyate । mālāniravayavaṃ yathā sphāraṃ cāmarabhūṣaṇaṃ dharaṇibhṛcchṛṅgeṣu gaṅgāsarit ।
sphāraḥ kākativīrarudrayaśasāṃ jāgarti visphūrjitam ।। rūpakaheturūpakaṃ paramparitarūpakam । rūpakadvayamātravyavasthitatvādasya na samastavastuviṣaye antarbhāvaḥ । śliṣṭakevalaparamparitaṃ yathā pratāparudradevasya maṇḍalāgravidhuntudaḥ ।
