akhaṇḍavikramoddāmo grasate rājamaṇḍalam ।। kṣmābhṛtpakṣabhidāśaniḥ kuvalayālaṃkārarākāśaśī । kṣoṇībhṛdbhuvanāśrayāmbudhirayaṃ śrīvīrarudro nṛpaḥ ।। kākatīyasya dugdhābdheryaśolīlāmahormayaḥ ।
dikkūlamudrujāṭopāḥ khelantyabbhraṃkaṣocchrayāḥ ।। śauryogrānaladhūmyayā jayaramāyoṣāvilāsabhruvā । prasādārgalayā kṛpāṇalatayā rudro nṛpaḥ krīḍati ।। aśliṣṭamālāparamparitaṃ vaidharmyeṇāpi saṃbhavati । yathā
trāsāndhakāramadhyāhnāḥ kaitavātaparātrayaḥ । jayanti vīrarudrasya raṇaprāṅgaṇakelayaḥ ।। evamaṣṭavidhasyāpi rūpakasya vākyasamāsagatatvena ṣoḍaśa rūpakabhedāḥ saṃbhavanti ।। pariṇāmālaṅkāraḥ ।
āropyamāṇamāropaviṣayātmatayā sthitam । prakṛtasyopayogitve pariṇāma udāhṛtaḥ ।। āropyamāṇaṃ prakṛtopayogītyanena sarvālaṅkāravyāvṛttiḥ । tasya sāmānādhikaraṇyavaiyadhikaraṇyābhyāṃ dvaividhyam । sāmānādhikaraṇyena pariṇāmo yathā
namrairbhajanti makuṭairavanīpavargāḥ । rājñāmayīṃ srajamamandavilāsalakṣmīm ।। kirīṭamāṇikyamayūkhajālairvidhāya puṣpāñjalimarcayante । phalārthino rudranarendrapādapīṭhāntasīmānamarikṣitīndrāḥ ।।
samāsoktāvāropyamāṇasya prakṛtopayogitve apyavācyatvānna pariṇāme antarbhāvaḥ । saṃdehālaṅkāraḥ । viṣayo viṣayī yatra sādṛśyāt kavisaṃmatāt । saṃdehagocarau syātāṃ saṃdehālaṅkṛtiśca sā ।।
sā trividhā । śuddhā, niścayagarbhā, niścayāntā ceti । kimeṣa daśamaḥ prajāpatirapūrvasargakramaḥ । ścirāditi vilokyate jagati vīrarudro janaiḥ ।। kālabhrūkuṭireṣa kiṃ nu mukha evojjṛmbhate sā punaḥ ।
vāteneti vikalpyate pratibhaṭai rudrasya kaukṣeyakaḥ ।। svardhenorathavā kimujjvalatarāścintāmaṇeḥ sphūrtayaḥ । santaḥ kākativīrarudranṛpateḥ smerāḥ kaṭākṣā iti ।। bhrāntimadalaṅkāraḥ ।
kavisaṃmatāsādṛśyādviṣaye pihitātmani । āropyamāṇānubhavo yatra sa bhrāntimān mataḥ ।। kīrttivibhave vyāptarodasi । divāpi candrikābuddhyā cakorā yānti nirvṛtim ।।
apahnavālaṅkāraḥ । niṣidhya viṣayaṃ sāmyādanyārope hyapahnutiḥ ।। tasyāstraividhyamapahnutyāropaḥ, āropyāpahnavaḥ, chalādiśabdairasatyatvapratipādanaṃ ca । ādyadvayasyodāharaṇam nedaṃ dundubhigarjitaṃ tripurajitkalpāntaḍhakkāravaḥ ।
ccheṣāśeṣaśirassu vismitamatha bhraṣṭaṃ digīśairapi ।। pātuṃ madhyamalokapālapadavīṃ prāptaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śivaḥ । jātaṃ vairipuraiḥ kathaṃ kathamavāgbhūtaṃ ca bhūbhṛdgaṇaiḥ ।। arthayogaruciśleṣairullekhanamanekadhā ।
grahītṛbhedādekasya sa ullekhaḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।। śauryātibhūmikhanirityarivīravargāḥ । śrīkākatīndranagarīmaniśaṃ stuvanti ।। ugraḥ sapatneṣu, guṇeṣu bhāsvān, rāmaḥ pratīkeṣu, raṇeṣu bhīmaḥ ।
līlāsu lakṣmyāḥ puruṣottamaścetyācakṣate rudranṛpaṃ kavīndrāḥ ।। utprekṣālaṅkāraḥ । athādhyavasāyagarbhālaṃkāradvayaṃ nirūpyate । viṣayaviṣayiṇoranyataranigaraṇenābhedapratipattiradhyavasāyaḥ । sa dvividhaḥviṣayinigaraṇena viṣayanigaraṇena ca । yatrānyadharmasaṃbandhādanyatvenopatarkitam ।
prakṛtaṃ hi bhavet prājñāstāmutprekṣāṃ pracakṣate ।। yatrāprakṛtaguṇakriyāsaṃbandhādaprakṛtatvena prakṛtasya saṃbhāvanam utprekṣā । sā dvividhāvācyā, pratīyamānā ca । saṃbhāvanāpratipādakānāṃ "nūnaṃ prāya'; ityevamādīnāṃ prayoge vācyā । aprayoge tu pratīyamānā । jātikriyāguṇadravyāṇāṃ caturṇāmadhyavasāyaviṣayatvena sā dvividhā; pratyekaṃ caturvidhā । teṣāṃ bhāvābhāvarūpatayā dvaividhye aṣṭavidhā । adhyavasāyasya guṇanimittatvena kriyānimittatvena ca dvaividhye pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśaprakārā । nimittasya vācyatvagamyatvābhyāṃ dvaividhyaṃ vācyotprekṣāyāmeva । pratīyamānotprekṣāyāmivādyanupādāne nimittasya cāprayoge utprekṣāyā niravalambanatvāt । tathā jātyādīnāṃ svarūpeṇa heturūpeṇa phalarūpeṇa cādhyavasāyaviṣayatve bahuvidhatvam । vācyotprekṣāyāmapi hetuphalayorutprekṣāviṣayatve nimittasyopādānameva । tathā hiyathā sādhye anupātte sādhanatvena nirdeśo nānvayaṃ puṣṇāti, tathā sādhane anupātte sādhyatvena nirdeśo api । tayoranyonyāpekṣitvāt । hetūtprekṣāyāṃ phalaṃ nimittam । tasyānupādāne kaṃ prati phalatvena saṃghaṭate । tathāhi
pratāparudranṛpaterapāre kīrttisāgare । magnā durīśaduṣkīrttisaṅgādiva jagantrayī ।। atrotprekṣānimittasya majjanasyānupādāne saṅgāditi hetūtprekṣā na śobhāmāvahati । yathā vā jayaśrīvāsapadmasya vikāsāyeva bhānumān ।
pratibimbamiṣāt khaḍgaṃ praviśatyandhrabhūbhujaḥ ।। atrotprekṣānimittasya bhānumatpraveśasyānupādāne jayaśrīvāsakamalavikāsāyeveti phalotprekṣaṇamasamīcīnam । ataḥ svarūpotprekṣāyāmeva nimittasyopādānānupādānābhyāṃ dvaividhyam । ataścetthaṃ vācyotprekṣāyā bhedagaṇanā । upāttaguṇanimittajātibhāvasvarūpotprekṣā । upāttaguṇanimittajātyabhāvasvarūpotprekṣā ।
upāttakriyānimittijātibhāvasvarūpotprekṣā । upāttakriyānimittajātyabhāvasvarūpotprekṣā । anupāttanimittijātibhāvasvarūpotprekṣā । anupāttanimittijātyabhāvasvarūpotprekṣā ।
upāttaguṇanimittajātibhāvahetūtprekṣā । upāttaguṇanimittajātyabhāvahetūtprekṣā । upāttakriyānimittajātibhāvahetūtprekṣā । upāttakriyānimittajātyabhāvahetūtprekṣā ।
upāttaguṇanimittajātibhāvaphalotprekṣā । upāttaguṇanimittajātyabhāvaphalotprekṣā । upāttakriyānimittajātyabhāvaphalotprekṣā । evaṃ caturdaśabhedā jātyutprekṣā ।
anenaiva krameṇa guṇakriyādravyotprekṣāpi parigaṇanīyā । evaṃ ca vācyotprekṣāyāḥ ṣaṭpañcāśad bhedāḥ । pratīyamānotprekṣāyastvaṣṭācatvāriṃśad bhedāḥ । atra svarūpotprekṣāyāmapi nimittopādānaniyamāt nimittasya gamyatve guṇarūpatvena kriyārūpatvena ca cārutvaviśeṣābhāvādeka eva bhedo gaṇyate ।
cābhyupagatam । prācāmalaṅkāraprabandheṣu ṣaṇṇavatibhedotprekṣeti gaṇanāmātram । cārutvātiśayastu ṣaṭpañcāśat eva bhedānām । tatra yathāsaṃbhavamudāharaṇāni ।
prācāṃ bhūmibhujāṃ yaśaḥ pidadhatī koṭīndutulyadyutiḥ । trailokyāṭṭahasaprabheva kakubhāṃ prānteṣu vidyotate ।। atra prabhāśabdo jātivacanaḥ । trailokyāṭṭahasaprabhāyāḥ kaviprauḍhoktisiddhatvānnopamāśaṅkāvakāśaḥ । rājyābhiṣekasalilaiḥ sarasīkṛtāyāḥ ।
kṣoṇyāḥ pramodapulakāṅkuramañjarīva ।। atra pulakāṅkuramañjarīvetyutprekṣāyāṃ sarasīkaraṇaṃ kriyārūpaṃ nimittam । pratāparudrasya nakhendukāntiḥ praṇāmabhājāṃ padayornṛpāṇām । lalāṭalagnā vidhinirmitāyā varṇāvalervācanadīpikeva ।।
atra dīpikeveti jātivacanājjātirutprekṣyate । pratāparudrasya guṇāmṛtormidhautā virājantyamalīkṛtāṅgāḥ । prakṣālitātyuddhatabhūmipālāḥ khaḍgāmbubhiḥ svacchatarā bhavanti ।। jayaprasthānodyatkarituragasaṃmardajanitam ।
pratāpākhyān anyān diśi diśi vidhatte dinakarān ।। atrāsūryāmiti jātyabhāvaḥ । jātihetūtprekṣā yathā udārarītyā bhujayā pratāparudrasya viśvaikadurandharasya । viśvaṃbharā komalaśayyayeva vismāritā gotramahīdhravāsam ।।
atra śayyeveti jātihetutvam । jātyabhāvahetūtprekṣā yathā bhūmerakalpavṛkṣatvāditi dhātā vicintayan । sṛṣṭavān kākatīśānaṃ nirvyājatyāgavaibhavam ।। atrākalpavṛkṣatvāditi jātyabhāvasya hetutvam ।
nūnaṃ viśvaṃbharādhārastambhībhavitumāyatau । vīrarudranarendrasya bhujāvājānulambinau ।। atra stambhībhavitumiti jāteḥ phalatvam । paśūnavadhyānālokya śatravaḥ kākatīśituḥ ।
prāyeṇāmānuṣatvāya tṛṇavṛttiṃ samāśritāḥ ।। atrāmānuṣatvāyeti jātyabhāvasya phalatvam । śvāsormibhiḥ sapadi marmaritāntarālāḥ । pratyuttarāṇi dadatīva marau vanāntāḥ ।।
vimukhe sati kākatikṣitīndre vanasīmāpi kaṭhorakaṇṭakāgrā । cikureṣu vikarṣati pratīśān adadāneva nijāntarapraveśam ।। atrādadāneti kriyāsvarūpābhāvaḥ । kriyāhetūtprekṣā yathā rājñāṃ garvāṅkurodbhedāḥ parimlānā dine dine ।
kākatīndrapratāpārkatīvroṣmābhibhavādiva ।। atrabhibhavādiveti kriyāhetutvam । (kriyāhetvabhāvotprekṣā yathā kapolaphalakāvasyāḥ kathaṃ bhūtvā tathāvidhau । apaśyantāvivānyonyamīdṛśīṃ kṣāmatāṃ gatau ।।
dambholisaṃrambhamahājigopaḥ prasthānabherīninado andhrabhartuḥ । līnānivānveṣṭumarātivargān vigāhate śailaguhāntarāṇi ।। sīmādrikuñjeṣu vihārabhājaḥ siddhāṅganā kalpitacandrikārdhān । śrīvīrarudrasya yaśovilāsān gāyantyasaṃspraṣṭumivāndhakāram ।।
atrāsaṃspraṣṭumiveti kriyābhāvasya phalatvam । cakāsti kākatīndrasya kṛpālokanavibhramaḥ । prakṛtiṣvapi sarvāsu prasāda iva mūrtimān ।। pratāparudrasya mahābhiṣekapayaḥ kaṇaiḥ śītalitākhilāṅgā ।
praśāntabhārārtaphaṇīndragāḍhaśvāsāniloṣmeva vibhāti pṛthvī ।। atra praśāntoṣmeti guṇābhāvaḥ । guṇahetūtprekṣā yathā jayaśriyāmāśrayatāmupetaḥ śrīvīrarudrasya raṇe kṛpāṇaḥ । jayaśriyaṃ vairimahīpatīnāṃ samutsuko hartumasūyayeva ।।
atrāsūyayeveti guṇasya hetutvam । guṇābhāvahetūtprekṣā yathā jātā vayaṃ saṃprati vīrarudranarendragambhīrimagulphadanghāḥ । ityapramodādiva jīvaneṣu mālinyamambhonidhayo bhajanti ।। atrāpramodādiveti guṇābhāvasya hetutvam । guṇaphalotprekṣā yathā
āśiṣāṃ viṣadhūmrāṇāṃ nairmalyārthamivotsukāḥ । bhujaṅgyaḥ kākatīndrasya guṇān gātuṃ sudhāmucaḥ ।। atra nairmalyārthamiti guṇasya phalatvam । guṇābhāvaphalotprekṣā yathā araṇyavāsārjitabāndhavāsu mṛgīṣvavairārthamivāśaraṇyāḥ ।
triliṅgadeśeśvaravairināryaḥ parāṅmukhā locanavibhrameṣu ।। atrāvairārthamiti guṇābhāvasya phalatvam । dravyasvarūpotprekṣā yathā na nityamasmin paripūrṇateti tyaktvā nabhaḥ kṣoṇitalāvatīrṇaḥ । ānandayanninduriva svadhāmnā vibhāti loke navakākatīndraḥ ।।
ananyasādhāraṇadānaśauṇḍe sadyaḥ kṛtārthībhavadarthisārthe । śrīkākatīndre bhuvi rājamāne dyauḥ pārijātena vinākṛteva ।। atra divaḥ pārijātābhāva utprekṣyate । dravyahetūtprekṣā yathā pratāparudradevena kṣmābhṛtpakṣavijṛmbhitam ।
samunmūlitamāmūlādapareṇeva vajriṇā ।। kākatīyapratāpoṣmavilīnāṅgena meruṇā । asuvarṇācaleneva viriñcirvyākulīkṛtaḥ ।। atrāsuvarṇācaleneti hetvabhāvaḥ । dravyaphalotprekṣā yathā
dugghārṇavaśatāyeva kailāsācalakoṭaye । nūnaṃ pratāparudreṇa yaśo dikṣu prasāritam ।। atra dugghārṇavaśatāyeti dravyasya phalatvam । vīrarudranarendrasya jayaprasthānasaṃbhavam ।
rajaḥ pihitadiggolaṃ nirākāśamiva sthitam ।। atra nirākāśamityākāśābhāvāya ityarthaḥ । evaṃ bhedāntaraṃ yathāsaṃbhavamudāhāryam । ityaupamyagarbhālaṃkāravivecanam । atiśayoktyalaṅkāraḥ ।
viṣayasyānupādānādviṣayyupanibadhyate । yatra sātiśayoktiḥ syāt kaviprauḍhoktijīvitā ।। yatra kaviprauḍhoktyā viṣayatirodhānena viṣayī nibadhyate sātiśayoktiḥ । tasyāścāturvidhyambhede abhedaḥ, abhede bhedaḥ, saṃbandhe asaṃbandhaḥ, asaṃbandhe saṃbandhaśceti । kāryakāraṇayoḥ paurvāparyaviparyayarūpā tvanadhyavasāyamūlatvād vyatiriktaiva । kiṃ tu prauḍhoktimūlatvādatiśayoktiriti kathyate । tatra bhede abhedo yathā sthāne kalpatarurjātaḥ kākatīyakulodadheḥ ।
lakṣmīpatirasau citraṃ martyalokamahotsavaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrakalpavṛkṣayorabhedādhyavasāyaḥ । abhede bhedo yathā kāpyanyā saraṇiḥ pratāpayaśasoranyaiva bāhvoḥ prathā । sāmagrī caturānanena kiyatī kīdṛkkramā kalpitā ।।
atraunnatyādervāstavābhede api bhedaḥ kalpitaḥ । tataḥ svataḥ siddhakaviprauḍhoktisiddhayoraunnatyayorbhede api abhedādhyavasāyaḥ । viyaddhenuḥ, sarvaṃ jagadapi tathā doṣavidhuram । spṛśeddevaṃ rudraṃ sakalaguṇasāmrājyanilayam ।। atra vidhātṛsṛṣṭisaṃbandhe apyasaṃbandha uktaḥ । atītabrahmasṛṣṭineśvareṇātrābhedādhyavasāyaḥ । asaṃbandhe saṃbandho yathā
svāmin ! satyamadhikriyādya phalitā yadvīrarudraḥ kṛtaḥ । śaṃbhuḥ kṣmāmavatīrṇavāniti kathā jātā haribrahmaṇoḥ ।। atra haribrahmaṇorevaṃvidhagoṣṭyasaṃbandhe api saṃbandha uktaḥ । śaṃbhunā saha kākatīndrasyābhedādhyavasāyaḥ । kāryakāraṇayoḥ paurvāparyaviparyayarūpātiśayoktiryathā mātaḥ ! kathaṃ kākatināthadṛṣṭeragresarāḥ kāmaśarāḥ patanti ।
tadrūpalāvaṇyajitaḥ smaro api nūnaṃ gataḥ kiṃkaratāmamuṣya ।। atra kāryabhūtasya smaraśarapātasya kāraṇabhūtāt priyadṛṣṭipātāt pūrvakālatvamuktam । sahoktyalaṅkāraḥ । sahoktirnirūpyate ।
sahārthenānvayo yatra bhavedatiśayoktitaḥ । kalpitaupamyaparyantā sā sahoktiritīṣyate ।। saṃbandhe upamānopameyabhāvaḥ kalpyate tatra sahoktiḥ । prākaraṇikāprākaraṇikaviṣayatvādupamānopameyabhāvasya sahārthasaṃbandhena dvayorapi prakṛtatvānna tadātmatā । andhrakṣamābhṛtsubhaṭāsidhārā raṇeṣu nīlotpalapatrabhāsaḥ ।
patanti kaṇṭheṣvaribhūpatīnāṃ sākaṃ surastrījanamuktamālyaiḥ ।। atra kṛpāṇapatanottarakālabhāvino divyamālyapatanasya sahakālatvamuktamiti paurvāparyaviparyayaḥ । bhede abhedarūpātiśayoktiḥ śleṣagarbhābhedādhyavasāyarūpā cārutvātiśayahetuḥ । tanmūlā yathā dine dine rudranarādhipasya pratāpalakṣmīrudayaṃ prayāti । prakāśitāśeṣadigantarālā vivasvatā sārdhamanindyabhāsā ।।
atrodayaṃ prayātīti śleṣeṇodayaparvatābhyudayayorabhedādhyavasāyaḥ । vinoktyalaṅkāraḥ । atha sahoktipratipakṣarūpā vinoktirnirūpyate । vinā saṃbandhi yatkiṃcidyatrānyasya parābhavet ।
aramyatā ramyatā vā sā vinoktiriti smṛtā ।। yatra kasyacidasaṃnidhānādvastu ramyamaramyaṃ vā bhavet sā vinoktiḥ । sā dvividhāaramyatā, ramyatā ceti । aramyatā yathā pratāparudradevasya guṇavarṇanayā vinā । kīdṛśī kāvyaracanā saṃśṛṇudhvaṃ kavīśvarāḥ ।।
atra pratāparudraguṇavarṇanena vinā kāvyaśriyo aśobhanatvamuktam । anena kāvyaśobhāmicchadbhiḥ kavibhiḥ pratāparudraguṇā varṇayitavyā iti vidhireva prakāśyate । ramyatā yathā vapuṣmatyānande vimalavibhave rudranṛpatau । prakāśaḥ syādinduryadi divi bhavet so api subhagaḥ ।। atra pratāparudre candramasaḥ kalaṅkena vinā śobhanatvamuktam । sakalaguṇaśālinaḥ pratipakṣasya purastāt tādṛśaguṇavattayaiva ramyatā, nānyatheti ।
samāsoktyalaṅkāraḥ । taulyena yatra prastutavartinām । aprastutasya gamyatvaṃ sā samāsoktiriṣyate ।। yatra prakṛtaviśeṣaṇasāmyādaprastutaṃ gamyate sā samāsoktiḥ । tat trividhamśliṣṭaviśeṣaṇasāmyaṃ, sādhāraṇam, aupamyagarbhaṃ ceti ।
rāgādandhrapateḥ kṛpāṇalatikā gṛhṇāti kaṇṭheṣvarīn । śūnyāntaḥ karaṇā bhajanti khalu te bhāvasthitiṃ kāmapi ।। atra viślathamekhalā pulakitāmiti śliṣṭaviśeṣaṇamahimnā kṛpāṇalatikāyā nāyikātvapratītiḥ । anuraktabhāvavivaśā ityādiviśeṣaṇadvārā ripūṇāṃ nāyakatvapratītiḥ । sādhāraṇaviśeṣaṇena yathā svedaṃ nirbharagātravepathu milanmūrcchaṃ galadbāṣpakam ।
bhūpāḥ śailaguhāsu yānti vijanaṃ bhītyā samāliṅgitāḥ ।। atra śṛṅgārabhayānakasādhāraṇaviśeṣabalād bhītyā samāliṅgitā iti nṛpāṇāṃ nāyakatvapratītiḥ । aupamyagarbhaviśeṣaṇena yathā bhṛtātmā guṇaratnaughaiḥ pūrṇaḥ saujanyavāriṇā । pratāparudranṛpatirdhatte viśvaṃbharāśriyam ।।
atra samāsoktau sarvatra vyavahārasamāropa eva jīvitam । laukike vastuni laukikavyavahārasamāropaḥ, śāstrīyavastuvyavahārasamāropaśceti dvividhaḥ; tathā śāstrīyavastuni śāstrīyavastuvyavahārasamāropaḥ, laukikavastuvyavahārasamāropaśceti । yathākramamudāharaṇāni । saptāṅgasphuraduddāmadānalakṣmīvirājitaḥ । pratāparudro bhadrātmā tanute sārvabhaumatām ।। atra laukike prakṛtavastuni laukikasya sārvabhaumanāmadheyasya diggajasya vyavahārapratītiḥ । tathā
gurupramāṇena nijena sadyastiraskṛtodyatpratipakṣahetau । pratāparudrasya samityudagre khaḍge mahatkhaṇḍanapaṇḍitatvam ।। atra laukike khaḍge tarkaśāstraprasiddhavastuvyavahārasamāropaḥ । śrutigrāhyaṃ tattvaṃ kimapi kalayantī pratipadam ।
budhaśreṇī yasyāṃ nipuṇamadhikartuṃ prabhavati ।। atrālaṃkāraśāstrīye vastuni tantraśāstraprasiddhavalastuvyavahārasamāropaḥ । lasadvarṇā saguṇā rasanirbharā । bhāvānubandhinī bhāti bhāratī kākatīśvare ।।
atrālaṃkāraśāstrīye vastuni bhāratyākhye laukikanāyikāvyavahārasamāropaḥ । samāsoktau viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayordvayorupādānābhāvācchleṣādviśeṣaḥ । vakroktyalaṅkāraḥ । anyathoktasya vākyasya kākvā śleṣeṇa vā bhavet । anyathā yojanaṃ yatra sā vakroktirnigadyate ।।
yatra kayācidvivakṣayā prayuktasya vākyasya anyathā vivakṣayā yojanā kriyate sā vakroktiḥ । uktivakratve kathaṃcit saṃbhavatyapyevaṃvidhalakṣaṇābhāvāt sarvālaṃkārebhyo bhidyate । kākvā yathā bahuvaḷḷaho khu rāā sahi tassa siriṃmi ṇibhbharāsattī । ṇūṇā sirie vi tumaṃ appāṇaṃ kiṃ ṇu ḷahuvasi ।। (।bahuvallabhaḥ khalu rājā sakhi tasya śriyāṃ nirbharāsaktiḥ ।
nyūnā śriyo api tvamātmānaṃ kiṃ nu laghayasi ।।) atra tvamapi śriyo nyūnaguṇā na bhavati । atastvayyapi nṛpatirāsakta eva, kimityātmānaṃ laghūkaroṣīti kākvā pratīyate । śleṣeṇa yathā kṣoṇībhṛttilakaḥ; sumerurayi kiṃ ? no rudradevo vibhuḥ ।
tyālyāṃ khalvapahāsavāci virahaṃ kiṃcidvadhūrvyasmarat ।। atha svabhāvoktiḥ । svabhāvoktirasau cāru yathāvadvastuvarṇanam ।। yatra cārutayā vastuno yathāvadvarṇanaṃ nibadhyate sā svabhāvoktiḥ ।
madaścyutā nartitakarṇatālamuddhūtamūrdhnā tripadasthitena । lolāgrahastena gajena jāto nityotsavaḥ kākativīrarudraḥ ।। vyājoktyalaṅkāraḥ । athoktisāmyād vyājoktirucyate ।
vyājoktiḥ sā samudbhūtaṃ vastu yatra nigūhyate ।। yatra prakāśaṃ vastu sāmyagarbhatvena nigūhanārhatvāt kenacit vyājena pracchādyate sā vyājoktiḥ । yathā sarvāṅgīṇe nṛpatitilakaḥ kākatīyānvayenduḥ । kartavyaḥ syāditi mṛdu hasan vīkṣate mantrivṛddhān ।।
atra kṣoṇīpāṇigrahaṇajanitaṃ romaharṣaṇaṃ dhīrodāttatayā pratāparudradevena mahābhiṣekasalilaśaityavyājena pracchādayatā mantriṇo vīkṣyante । mīlanālaṅkāraḥ । vyājoktyuttaraṃ kiṃcitsāmyānmīlanamucyate । mīlanaṃ vastunā yatra vastvantaranigūhanam ।।
yatra vastunā vastvantaraṃ pracchāditaṃ bhavati sa mīlanālaṃkāraḥ । sa dvividhaḥsahajenāgantukatirodhānam, āgantukena sahajatirodhānaṃ ceti । yathākramamudāharaṇe yuddhaprāṅgaṇavarjiteṣu patiṣu kvāpi pralīnātmasu । saṃkrānto api na lakṣyate pathi mahānūṣmā ciraṃ māravaḥ ।। atra sahajena ripukāminīgatena smarānaloṣmaṇā mārgavaśādāgantuko marūṣmā tirodhīyate । tathā
pratāparudrasya bhujaprabhāvādantarbhayād bhūmibhujāmajasram । svedāśrukampādyudaye apyanaṅgagoṣṭhyāṃ striyaḥ premṇi na viśvasanti ।। atra bhayajanitena kampādinā'gantukena sahajasya premajanitasya kampādestirodhānam । sāmānyālaṅkāraḥ ।
sāmānyaṃ guṇasāmyena yatra vastvantaraikatā ।। yatra evasya vastuno guṇasāmyena vatsvantaraikātmyaṃ bhavati, sa sāmānyālaṃkāraḥ । yathā kailāsadugdhārṇavayānahaṃseṣvalakṣiteṣvandhranarendrakīrttau । trayaḥ pumāṃsaḥ prathame smayante svasevakān saṃbhramato vilokya ।।
atra pratāparudrakīrttyāṃ jagatsu vijṛmbhitāyāṃ kailāsaprabhṛtīnāṃ vimalavastūnāṃ tadaikātmyam । tadguṇālaṅkāraḥ । itaraguṇasaṃnidhānātiśayasāmyāt tadguṇa ucyate । tadguṇaḥ svaguṇatyāgādanyotkṛṣṭaguṇāhṛtiḥ ।।
svaguṇaṃ vihāya saṃnihitavastunaḥ sakāśādutkṛṣṭaguṇaḥ svīkriyate sa tadguṇālaṅkāraḥ । yathā pratāparudradevāṅghrinakhajyotsnāvijṛmbhitaiḥ । namannṛpatimāṇikyamaulayaḥ śucayaḥ kṛtāḥ ।। atra praṇamatāṃ bhūpatīnāṃ padmarāgamukuṭāḥ svāṃ śoṇaprabhāṃ muktvā kākativīrarudrapadanakhajyotsnāgataṃ dhavalimānamudvahanti sma ।
atadguṇālaṅkāraḥ । tatprātipakṣyādatadguṇo nirūpyate । sati hetāvanyaguṇāsvīkāraḥ syādatadguṇaḥ ।। yatra saṃnidhānarūpe hetau satyapyanyaguṇasvīkāro nāsti asāvatadguṇālaṃkāraḥ । yathā
daityāriṃ paritastadaṅgavilasannīladyutidyotite । puṣṇan rudranarendrakīrttivibhavaḥ svāmeva śubhrāṃ chavim ।। atra hariharaviriñcīnāṃ samīpavartiṣu jagatsu tattannānāprabhāsamagreṣvapi nirantaraṃ viharamāṇasya pratāparudrayaśaso niraṅkuśaḥ svakīya eva dhavalim vijṛmbhate । virodhālaṅkāraḥ ।
atadguṇe kiṃcitprakrāntatvād virodhasya virodhālaṃkāro nirūpyate । ābhāsatve virodhasya virodhālaṃkṛtirmatā ।। yatra prathamamābhāsatayā pratīto virodhaḥ paryavasāne parihriyate sa virodhālaṃkāraḥ । tatra jāterjātyādinā saha virodhe catvāro bhedāḥ । kriyāyāḥ kriyāguṇadravyaiḥ saha virodhe trayo bhedāḥ । guṇasya guṇadravyābhyāṃ virodhe dvau bhedau । dravyasya dravyeṇa saha virodhe eko bhedaḥ । evaṃ daśa virodhe bhedāḥ । jāterjātyā kriyayā ca virodho yathā padmākaro api vilasati nitarāmajaḍāśayo ayamurvīśaḥ ।
vimalataravāridhārāpyāsīdvairikṣitīśatāpakarī ।। atra pūrvārdhe jātyorvirodhaḥ, kamalākaro apyajaḍāśaya iti virodhāt । uttarārdhe jātikriyayorvirodhaḥ, vimalataravāridhārāyāḥ saṃtāpakaraṇavirodhāt । atra śleṣamūlo virodhaḥ । amadaḥ sārvabhaumo api bhāsvānapi kalānidhiḥ । vīrarudranarendro ayamadbhutānāṃ vihārabhūḥ ।।
atra sārvabhaumo apyamada iti jātiguṇayorvirodhaḥ । bhāsvānapi kalānidhiriti jātidravyayorvirodhaḥ । kalānidherekatvāt dravyatvam । atrāpi śleṣamūlatā । kriyāyāḥ kriyayā virodho yathā dharmadviṣāmarthamuṣāṃ ca bhaṅgamutpādayan kākativīrarudraḥ । trivargasādhāraṇagocaro api karoti kāmadviṣi bhāvamārdram ।। atra trivargasādhāraṇavṛtterdharmārthavirodhiṣu bhaṅgakaraṇaṃ kāmārau snehakaraṇaṃ ca viruddham । kriyāyā guṇadravyābhyāṃ virodho yathā
eṣa jiṣṇuvihāro api gotravātsalyalālasaḥ । karoti kamalollāsaṃ rājāpyandhranareśvaraḥ ।। atra jiṣṇuvihārasya gotravātsalyamiti kriyāguṇayorvirodhaḥ । kamalollāsaṃ kurvannapi rājeti kriyādravyayorvirodhaḥ । atrāpi śleṣamūlataiva । guṇasya guṇena virodho yathā rajjaṃto bhuvaṇamiaṃ rāetti jae salāhaṇijjo si ।
ruddaṇariṃda ! kahaṃ sā rattā vi a paṃḍurā jāā ।। (rañjayan bhuvanamidaṃ rājeti yathā ślāghanīyo asi । rudranarendra ! kathaṃ sā raktāpi ca puṇḍurā jātā ।।) atra raktatvapāṇḍuratvayorvihodhaḥ । guṇasya dravyeṇa virodho yathā
jvalatpratāparaudro api kākatīyanareśvaraḥ । bhūtvā jaivātṛko bhāti śaśvadviśvapriyaṃkaraḥ ।। atra pratāparaudro api jaivātṛka iti guṇadravyayorvirodhaḥ । vibhāti kākatīndro ayaṃ rudro api caturānanaḥ ।
tathā ca jiṣṇurityeṣa kathyate puruṣottamaḥ ।। evaṃ daśa bhedā darśitāḥ । ayamaśleṣeṇāpi bhavati । yathā svabhāvaśiśirā dṛṣṭirapi kākatibhūbhujaḥ । sarvāṅgatāpinī jātā pratipakṣamahībhṛtām ।।
atra svabhāvaśiśirāpi tāpinīti virodhaḥ । viśeṣālaṅkāraḥ । atha virodhagarbhālaṃkārā nirūpyante । ādhārarahitādheyamekaṃ cānekagocaram ।
aśakyavastukaraṇaṃ viśeṣālaṃkṛtistridhā ।। yatrādhāramantareṇādheyo nibadhyate sa eko viśeṣaḥ । ekasyānekagocaratve dvitīyo viśeṣaḥ । prakṛtādaśakyavastvantarakaraṇe tṛtīyaḥ । yathākramamudāharaṇāni nalanahuṣadilīpadharmaputraprabhṛtinareśvarasaṃśritā yaśaḥ śrīḥ । anudinamadhunābhyupetya maitrīṃ vilasati kākativīrarudrakīrttyā ।।
atra prācāṃ bhūpatīnāmādhārabhūtānāṃ tirodhāne apyāśritāyāḥ kīrtteravasthānam । yathā ca rapyantarbahirandhrapārthivapatiṃ protkṣiptakaukṣeyakam । śailācchelamaṭanti kampavilasadgāmbhīryaśauryaśriyaḥ ।। atra bhayabhrāntānāṃ śatrunṛpatīnāṃ pratāparudranṛpatireko apyanekatra pratīyate । tathā ca
prasādamadhurakramā lagati yatra dṛṣṭirjane । na kiṃ mimadhitiṣṭhati tribhuvane sa sarvādhikaḥ ।। apra sādhāraṇo janaḥ pratāparudradṛṣṭiprasādapātrīkṛtaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na labhata ityaśakyavastvantarakaraṇam । adhikālaṅkāraḥ ।
ādhārādheyavaicitryādadhikālaṃkāro nirūpyate । ādhārādheyayorānurūpyābhāvo adhiko mataḥ ।। yatrāśrayāśrayiṇorānurūpyaṃ nāsti so adhikālaṃkāraḥ । sa dvividhaḥ, āśrayasyālpatvamahattvābhyām । saṃkocādekarāśībhavadatanurucau kākatīndrasya kīrttau ।
kṣīrambhorāśimukhyaiḥ prakaṭitamadhunā taddhanībhāvarūpam ।। atrāśrayasya rodaḥ kuharasyālpatvamāśritasya pratāparudrayaśaso vaipulyam । dvitīyo yathā bhūpāstādṛśasainyavaibhavasamākrāntākhilāśāntarāḥ । niḥ sīme balavāridhau vidadhate pūrtiṃ na koṇe apyaho ।।
atrāśrayasya pratāparudrasainyāmbudhervaipulyam । āśritānāmaṅgavaṅgakaliṅgaprabhṛtirājakānīkinīnāmalpatvam । atha vibhāvanā viśeṣoktiśca । kāraṇena vinā kāryasyotpattiḥ syādvibhāvanā । tatsāmagrayāmanutpattirviśeṣoktirnigadyate ।।
yatra prasiddhakāraṇaparityāgena kāryasyotpattirnigadyate sā vibhāvanā । yatra sākalye satyapi kāryasyānutpattiḥ sā viśeṣoktiḥ । pratāparudreṇa parājitānāṃ pratyarthināṃ vindhyaguhāgatānām । tamāṃsyarātrīṇi samudbhavanti tejāṃsi dhasreṣvapi nodbhavanti ।। prādurbhāvasya prasiddhakāraṇaṃ rātriḥ । tayā vināpi tasyotpattirnibaddhā । aprasiddhaṃ kāraṇaṃ śokādyastyeva । tathā ahassu ravikiraṇeṣu satsvapi tejaso anutpattiriti atra niṣpratāpatvādi nimittamastyeva ।
asaṃgatyalaṅkāraḥ । kāryakāraṇavirodhaprastāvād asaṃgatirucyate । kāryakāraṇayorbhinnadeśatve satyasaṃgatiḥ ।। yatraikadeśavartinorapi kāryakāraṇayorbhinnadeśasthitirnibadhyate asāvasaṃgatyalaṃkāraḥ । yathā
bibhratyurvīdhurāṃ gurvī vīrarudranareśvare । bhavantyatitarāṃ śaśvannamrāḥ sāmantamaulayaḥ ।। atra rājñi bhūbhāraḥ śatruṣu namanamiti । vicitrālaṅkāraḥ ।
virodhaprastāvādvicitraṃ nirūpyate । vicitraṃ svaviruddhasya phalaprāptyarthamudyamaḥ ।। yatra svaviruddhaphalaprāptyarthamudyogaḥ kriyate sa vicitrālaṃkāraḥ । pratāparudranṛpateragre dūrānnareśvarāḥ ।
avarohanti hastibhyastānāroḍhumanargalam ।। atrāroḍhumavarohantīti viparītaphalaprāptyarthaṃ prayatnaḥ । anyonyālaṃkāraḥ । athānyonyaṃ nirūpyate ।
asyāpi virodhamūlatā । tadanyonyaṃ mitho yatrotpādyotpādakatā bhavet ।। yatra parasparaṃ kriyādvārakamutpādyotpādakatvaṃ tadanyonyālaṃkāraḥ । ārohatā rudranareśvareṇa virājate kākatirājapīṭham ।
āruhya tenojjvalaratnabhājā rājāpi lakṣmīmadhikāṃ bibharti ।। atra pratāparudrabhadrāsanayoranyonyālaṃkāryatvam । viṣamālaṃkāraḥ । atha virodhamūlo viṣamālaṃkāraḥ kathyate ।
viruddhakāryasyotpattiryatrānarthasya vā bhavet । virūpaghaṭanā cāsau viṣamālaṃkṛtistridhā ।। yatra kāraṇādviruddhakāryasyotpattistadekaṃ viṣamam । akāryabhūtasyānarthasyotpattirdvitīyam । virūpayorvastunoḥ saṃghaṭane tṛtīyam । tatra prathamaṃ yathā udbhūtāṃ śaradindukāntidhavalāṃ kīrttiśriyaṃ paśyatām ।
śrutvā saṃprati vismayādviramati prāptānubhāvaṃ manaḥ ।। atra nīlavarṇāt khaḍgādindughavalasya yaśasaḥ samutpattiḥ । āstāṃ jayāśā ripubhūpatīnāṃ saṃgrāmasīmāmamupāgatānām । pratāparudrasya vilokanena bhraśyanti jīvaiḥ samamāyudhāni ।।
atra samarodyogaphalasya na kevalaṃ jayasyānutpattiryāvajjīvitabhraṃśarūpānarthotpattirapi । tṛtīyaṃ yathā kva ceyaṃ kāntārasthitiraśivavṛttyekanilayā । pratāpaṃ ślāghante śabarapuravīrāḥ pratidiśam ।। atra mahānagaranivāsayogyānāṃ rājñāmaśivānāṃ vanapradeśānāṃ virūpāṇāṃ saṃghaṭanam ।
evaṃ virodhagarbhālaṅkārā nirṇītāḥ । samālaṅkāraḥ । adhunā viṣamavaidharmyāt samālaṃkāro nirūpyate । sā samālaṃkṛtiryoge vastunoranurūpayoḥ ।।
yatrānyonyānurūpapadārthasaṃghaṭanā kriyate sa samālaṅkāraḥ । yathā vijjāo sakalāo lacchīe samaṃ paāvaruddaṃmi । saṃghaṭiūṇa susarisaṃ hoi kaaccho saaṃ bahmā ।। (vidyāḥ sakalā lakṣmyā samaṃ pratāparudre ।
saṃghaṭayya susadṛśaṃ bhavati kṛtārthaḥ svayaṃ brahmā ।।) atra pratāparudre sakalavidyānāṃ lakṣmyāśca yogaḥ । tulyayogitālaṅkāraḥ । atha gamyamānopamyālaṃkāravargaprastāvaḥ ।
prastutānāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ kevalaṃ tulyadharmataḥ । aupamyaṃ gamyate yatra sā matā tulyayogitā ।। yatra kevalaprastutānāṃ kevalāprastutānāṃ vā samānadharmasaṃbandhādaupamyaṃ gamyate sā tulyayogitā । prastutānāṃ yathā bhadrāsanādhyāsini rudradeve tatkīrttayastaddviṣadaṅganāśca ।
anārataṃ bhrāntiviśeṣabhājaḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pāṇḍuratāṃ bhajante ।। atra kīrttīnāṃ dviṣadaṅganānāṃ ca prākaraṇikatvam । pāṇḍuratāṃ bhajanta iti samānadharmaḥ । aprākaraṇikānāṃ yathā kūrmendrapannagādhīśaharitkarikulādrayaḥ । mitho niḥ sāratāṃ prāptāḥ kākatīndre mahībhṛti ।।
atra kūrmendraprabhṛtīnāmaprākaraṇikatvam । niḥ sāratāṃ prāptā iti samānadharmaḥ । atra gamyamānaupamyaṃ na vāstavam; kiṃ tu vaivakṣikam । dīpakālaṅkāraḥ । prasutāprastutānāṃ tu sāmastye tulyadharmataḥ । aupamyaṃ gamyate yatra dīpakaṃ tannigadyate ।।
yatra prastutāprastutānāṃ samastānāmeva samānadharmasaṃbandhenaupamyaṃ gamyate taddīpakam । tasya dharmasyādimadhyāntagatatvena traividhyam । ādidīpakaṃ yathā bhāi ṇaleṇa kiajuaṃ rahuuladīveṇa soriṇā tetā । dāvāro tavajaṇiṇā kalījuaṃ vīruddeṇa ।। (bhāti nalena kṛtayugaṃ raghukuladīpena śauriṇā tretā ।
dvāparastapojaninā kaliyugaṃ vīrarudreṇa ।।) atra yathā nalarāmadharmaputraiḥ kṛtatretādvāparāḥ śobhante, tathā vīrarudreṇa kaliyugaṃ śobhata ityaupamyaṃ gamyate । madhyadīpakaṃ yathā bhāīrahie jalaṇihī rāaī joṇhāe puṇṇimācaṃdo । suttīe kamalahavo kittīe paāvaruddo vi ।।
(bhāgīrathyā jalanidhī rājate jyotsnayā pūrṇimācandraḥ ।। śrutyā kamalabhavaḥ kīrttyā pratāparudro api ।।) atra bhāgīrathyādibhiḥ samudrādayo yathā rājante tathā kīrttyā pratāparudro rājata ityaupamyaṃ gamyate । antadīpakaṃ yathā asuraloaṃ suraṇāho ṇaraloaṃ vīraruddaṇaraṇāho ।
phaṇiloaṃ phaṇiṇāho rakkhai ṇirupaddavojjeaṃ ।। (asuralokaṃ suranātho naralokaṃ vīrarudranaranāthaḥ ।। phaṇilokaṃ phaṇinātho rakṣati nirupadravodvegam ।।) atra yathā suralokaphaṇilokau suranāthaphaṇināthābhyāṃ rakṣitau, tathā vīrarudreṇa naraloko rakṣita ityaupamyaṃ gamyate ।
atha padārthagatālaṃkāradvayānantaraṃ vākyārthagatamalaṃkāradvayaṃ nirūpyate । pratīvastūpamālaṅkāraḥ । yatra sāmānyanirdeśaḥ pṛthagvākyadvaye yadi । gamyaupamyāśritā sā syāt prativastūpamā matā ।।
yatra vastuprativastubhāvena sāmānyaṃ vākyadvaye nirdiśyate tena gamyaupamyā prativastūpamā । sā sādharmyavaidharmyābhyāṃ dvividhā । manthānācala evaikaḥ kṣamaḥ sindhuviloḍane । pratāparudra evaikaḥ śaktaḥ śatruviloḍane ।। atra yathā samudraviloḍane manthānācalaḥ kṣamastathā śatruviloḍane pratāparudraḥ śakta ityaupamyaṃ gamyate । dvitīyā yathā
pratāparudra evaikaḥ paṭīyān janarañjane । candrādṛte kṣamo nānyaścakoraparitoṣaṇe ।। atra candreṇa yathā cakoraparitoṣaṇaṃ kriyate, tathā vīrarudreṇa janarañjanaṃ kriyata iti vaidharmyeṇaupamyaṃ gamyate । atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ ।
dṛṣṭāntālaṅkāraḥ । yatra vākyadvaye bimbapratibimbatayocyate । sāmānyadharmo vākyajñaiḥ sa dṛṣṭānto nigadyate ।। yatra bimbapratibimbabhāvena sāmānyaṃ vākyadvaye nirdiśyate, sa dṛṣṭāntālaṃkāraḥ । so api sādharmyavaidharmyābhyāṃ dvividhaḥ । ādyo yathā
svarṇādrerdigadhīśavāsanagarīsaṃdigdhakuñjaśriyaḥ । ko apyanyo mahimā jagattrayadhurādhaureyadoḥ śālinaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrasya merośca bimbapratibimbabhāvādaupamyaṃ gamyate । vaidharmyeṇa yathā kākatīndrakṛpādṛṣṭimātrājjāgrati saṃpadaḥ ।
tāvadabjāni nidrānti yāvannodeti bhānumān ।। atra yathā bhāsvadudayamātreṇa padmāni samunmīlanti tathā pratāparudradayāvilokanamātreṇa saṃpadaḥ saṃbhavantīti vaidharmyeṇa bimbapratibimbanam । nidarśanālaṅkāraḥ । atha gamyamānaupamyaprastāvānnidarśanālaṃkāro nirūpyate ।
asaṃbhavaddharmayogādupamānopameyayoḥ । pratibimbakriyā gamyā yatra sā syānnidarśanā ।। yatropamānadharmasyopameyagatatvena nibaddhasyānvayāsaṃbhavāt tatsambandhārthaṃ bimbapratibimbakaraṇamākṣipyate, saikā nidarśanā । tadviparyaye dvitīyā nidarśanā । prathamā yathā stribhuvanamahanīyaḥ kākatīyakṣitīśaḥ ।
mudayaśikharicūḍācumbinastīvrabhānoḥ ।। atra tīvrabhānorabhikhyāyāḥ prakṛte asaṃbhavādabhikhyāsadṛśīmabhikhyāṃ vahatīti bimbapratibimbakaraṇākṣepaḥ । upameyadharmasyopamāne asaṃbhavād yathā vīrarudranarendrasya yaśovaiśadyasaṃpadaḥ । lakṣyante kṣīravārāśilīlādarpaṇamaṇḍale ।।
atra yaśovaiśadyasya dugghārṇavādau asaṃbhavāt sādṛśyopagamena bimbapratibimbanaṃ gamyate । kvacinniṣedhavaśādākṣiptayā prāptyā bimbapratibimbakaraṇākṣepo yathā kākatīndradviṣatkāntā dhāvantyaḥ pratikānanam । padbhyāṃ muñcantyalākṣābhyāṃ sthale raktotpalaśriyam ।। atra muñcantīti niṣedhāt pūrvaṃ raktotpalaśrīprāptirākṣiptā ।
atha vyatirekaḥ । bhedapradhānasādharmyamupamānopameyayoḥ । ādhikyālpatvakathanād vyatirekaḥ sa ucyate ।। yatropamānādupameyasyādhikyena nyūnatvena vā pratipādanena bhedapradhānaṃ sādharmyamupagamyate sa vyatirekālaṃkāraḥ । yathā
dinakṛti kumudairdhṛto na rāgaḥ śaśini parāñci paraṃ saroruhāṇi । kuvalayakamalādṛtaprakāśaḥ prabhavati viśvasuhṛt pratāparudraḥ ।। atra raviśaśinorasaṃbhavena sarvapriyaṃkaratvenopameyabhūtasya pratāparudrasyādhikyaṃ kuvalayakamalādṛtaprakāśa ityuktamiti śleṣasamutthāpito vyatirekaḥ । atha śleṣālaṅkāro nirūpyate ।
prakṛtāprakṛtobhayagatamuktaṃ cecchabdamātrasādharmyam । śleṣo ayaṃ śliṣṭatvaṃ sarvatrādyadvaye nāntye ।। yatra kevalaprakṛtayoḥ kevalāprakṛtayośca śleṣaḥ kathyate; tatra prakāradvaye viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyaśliṣṭatā । prakṛtāprakṛtaviṣaye antyabhede viśeṣaṇamātraśliṣṭatā । viśeṣyayorapi śliṣṭatve śabdaśaktimūladhvaniprasaṅgāt । kevalaprakṛtayoḥ kevalāprakṛtayoścaikaśabdagocaratve tu na dhvaniśaṅkā । atrārthadvayapratipādane aprastutatvena prastutatvena vā vaimagyābhāvādabhidhaiva samarthā । prastutāprastutaviṣaye tu abhidhāyāḥ prastutaikaparatantratvādaprastutārthapratipattirvyañjanavyāpārāyattaiva । tathā coktaṃ kāvyaprakāśe "anekārthasya śabdasya vācakatve niyantrite ।
saṃyogādyairavācyārthadhīkṛd vyāpṛtirañjanam ।।'; iti । tadevaṃ tridhā śleṣaḥ । tatra kevalaprākaraṇikayoryathā rājñaḥ pūjāvidhiṃ dhatte sakalomādhave tithiḥ । nīlakaṇṭhakalāpāṅke sphuradabjamaṇitviṣi ।।
atra pūjāviṣayatayā hariharayoḥ prākaraṇikatvam । aprākaraṇikayoryathā sadṛśaḥ kākatīndro ayaṃ mahākulamahībhṛtām । śirogṛhītasanmārgasphuratkaṭakasaṃpadām ।। atra mahākulānāṃ hariścandraprabhṛtīnāṃ kulaparvatānāṃ copamānatvenāprākaraṇikatvam । prākaraṇikāprākaraṇikayoryathā
mūrtau vilasatsarvamaṅgalaḥ । rājamauliḥ pratāpāṅkarudro rudra iva sthitaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrarudrayoḥ prākaraṇikāprākaraṇikatvam । parikarālaṅkāraḥ ।
viśeṣaṇavaicitryamūlatvāt parikara ucyate । yatrābhiprāyagarbhā syād viśeṣaṇaparamparā । tatrābhiprāyaviduṣāmasau parikaro mataḥ ।। yatra viśeṣaṇāni sābhiprāyāṇi nibadhyante sa parikarālaṃkāraḥ । yathā
tvaṅgattuṅgaturaṅgasainyamahato mānaikavittasya ca । kṣiptasyācaritāni sevaṇapaterjānāti sā gautamī ।। atra rājña ityevamādiviśeṣaṇāni utprāsagarbhāṇi । ākṣepālaṅkāraḥ ।
viśeṣabodhāyoktasya vakṣyamāṇasya vā bhavet । niṣedhābhāsakathanamākṣepaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ।। yatra viśeṣapratipattyarthamuktavakṣyamāṇayoḥ prākaraṇikayorniṣedhābhāsaḥ kathyate, sa ākṣepālaṃkāraḥ । uktaviṣaye vastu vā kathanaṃ vā niṣidhyate । vakṣyamāṇaviṣaye kathanameva niṣidhyate । tatrāpi sāmānyarūpeṇa pratijñāya viśeṣarūpeṇa niṣedhaḥ । aṃśoktāvaṃśāntarasya vā niṣedhaḥ । evaṃ caturvidho ayamākṣepaḥ । krameṇaiṣāmudāharaṇāni । narendramaule ! na vayaṃ tava saṃdeśahāriṇaḥ ।
jagatkuṭumbinaḥ kaścinna śatruriti kathyate ।। atra rājasandhivigrahakāriṇāmuktau na vayaṃ saṃdeśahāriṇa iti vastuniṣedhaḥ । sa cānupapadyamānaḥ saṃdhivigrahakālocitakaitavavacanaparihāreṇa tattvavāditve paryavasitaḥ, sarvajagatpālakasya tava śatrubhāvena nālokanīyā rājānaḥ, kiṃ tu bhṛtyarūpeṇa saṃrakṣaṇīyā ityevamādiviśeṣamākṣipati । kathananiṣedho yathā tritayaśaraṇe trāyasvāsmāniti sphuṭamajñatā । tribhuvananamaskārye siddhaṃ pratāpamahīpate ।।
atra vayamaśaraṇā ityevamādyuktikathananiṣedhā bhāsarūpādavaśyaparipālanīyatvādiviśeṣaḥ pratīyate । vakṣyamāṇaviṣaye sāmānyaṃ pratijñāya kathananiṣedho yathā vijñāpayāmaste kiṃcit kākatīyakulodvaha । vijñāpyate kimathavā sarvajñe rakṣake tvayi ।। iti sāmānyaṃ pratijñāya kathananiṣedhābhāsāt sarvathā vayaṃ rakṣaṇīyā iti viśeṣa ākṣipyate । aṃśoktāvaṃśāntarasya niṣedho yathā
pratāparudraḥ svayamiddhatejā daivaṃ ca tadvikramadattahastam । yūyaṃ ca tūlopamasārabhājastad yuktamevaṃ yadi vā kimuktaiḥ ।। atra pratāparudro mahīyān, yūyamalpā ityaṃśoktyā yadi vā kimuktairityaṃśāntaraniṣedhābhāsena sarvathā praṇāmaiḥ prasādanīyo ayam, na tu prātipakṣyamavalambanīyaṃ yuṣmābhiriti śatrustrīvacanabhaṅgyā viśeṣa ākṣipyate । samānārthatayāniṣṭavidhyābhāso apyākṣepa ityabhyupagamyate ।।
yathā ca iṣṭaniṣedhasyānupapadyamānatayā ābhāsatvaṃ tathā aniṣṭavidherapyanupapadyamānatayā ābhāsatvam । yathā nātha ! pratāparudrasya sevāṃ tyajasi cet tyaja । araṇyagṛhamedhinyā rītirabhyasyate mayā ।। atrāniṣṭabhūtaṃ pratāparudrapādasevātyajanaṃ tadripukāminyā vidhīyate । sa vidhiranupapadyamāna ābhāse paryavasyati । araṇyagṛhamedhinyā rītirabhyasyata ityanena vidhyābhāsa eva upabṛṃhitaḥ ।
vyājastutyalaṅkāraḥ । atha gamyaprastāvāt vyājastutirucyate । nindayā vācyayā yatra stutirevāvagamyate । stutyā vā gamyate nindā vyājastutirasau matā ।।
yatra nindākathanamukhena stutirgamyateekā sā । yatra stutimukhena nindā gamyatesā dvitīyā vyājastutiḥ । krameṇa yathā kākatīyavibhoḥ kīrttyā kiṃ vādya dhavalīkṛtam । yattadīyārivaktreṣu dṛśyate kālimā mahān ।। pratāparudranṛpateraho sāhasikā dviṣaḥ ।
yadviśantyudadhīn śailānārohanti samantataḥ ।। aprastutapraśaṃsālaṅkāraḥ । atha gamyatvaprastāvādaprastutapraśaṃsocyate । aprastutasya kathanāt prastutaṃ yatra gamyate ।
aprastutapraśaṃseyaṃ sārūpyādiniyantritā ।। yatra sārūpyeṇa sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena kāryakāraṇabhāvena cāprastutakathanāt prastutapratītistatrāprastutapraśaṃsā । aprastutāt prastutapratītirityanena samāsoktervyāvṛttiḥ । na ca kāryāt kāraṇapratītāvanumānāvirbhāvaśaṅkā; anumānālaṃkāre pratyāyyapratyāyakayordvayorapi prākaraṇikatvābhyupagamāt । anena paryāyoktasya vyāvṛttirapi । na cāyaṃ dhvaniḥ । pratīyamānasya vācyasiddhyaṅgatvāt । tatra sārūpyeṇa yathā āśāsu praśamitavāsanodayebhyaḥ kiṃ labdhaṃ bhramaragaṇairjarattarubhyaḥ । punnāgo navanavasaurabhaprasūnairāmodaṃ diśati vivāsamārabhadhvam ।।
atra bhramaravṛttāntenāprastutena sarvān asaṃpūrṇavibhavān urvīśvarān vihāya sakalaguṇaparipūrṇaḥ sarvajanānandī pratāparudra eka eva sarveṣāṃ viduṣāṃ sevya iti prastutaṃ pratīyate । sāmānyādviśeṣapratītiryathā yaśasvinī padmabhavasya sṛṣṭirutpādayitrī nṛpaśekharāṇām । tatpālanāllālanabhāgyayogyo jātaścirānmadhyamaloka eṣaḥ ।। atra pratāparudrasya guṇamahattve prastute sāmānyamabhihitam । viśeṣāt sāmānyapratipattiryathā
daṭṭhumaṇā vi ṇa pekkhai ṇa bhaṇai vattuṃ sakoduhalaā vi । parisāsaā vi ṇa ppasai vaṇiāe kīrisī siṭṭī ।। (draṣṭumanā api na paśyati na bhaṇati vaktuṃ sakautūhalāpi । sparśāśayāpi na spṛśati vanitāyāḥ kīdṛśī sṛṣṭiḥ ।।)
atra mugdhānāṃ navasaṃgame mahatī lajjeti sāmānye prastute viśeṣo abhihitaḥ । kāryāt kāraṇapratītiryathā gādhā ivārṇavā jātā nīcā iva mahādrayaḥ । mahīmavataratyasmin kākatīyakuleśvare ।। atrārṇavādīnāṃ gādhatvādibhiḥ kāryabhūtairaprastutaiḥ kāraṇabhūtaṃ pratāparudragāmbhīryādi pratīyate । kāraṇāt kāryapratītiryathā
pratāparudranṛpaterdharitrīkalpaśākhinaḥ । jātā mayi kṛpādṛṣṭiḥ kiṃ vā vismayase sakhe ।। atra kathamīdṛśamahāvibhavabhājanamadhunā bhavasīti kāryaṃ pṛcchate savismayāya suhṛde kāraṇabhūtā pratāparudrakṛpādṛṣṭirabhihitā । vācyasaṃbhāvasaṃbhavobhayarūpatayā yathāsaṃbhavaṃ bhedāḥ svayaṃ draṣṭavyāḥ ।
paryāyoktālaṅkāraḥ । gamyatvaprastāvāt paryāyoktamucyate । kāraṇaṃ gamyate yatra prastutāt kāryavarṇanāt । prastutatvena saṃbaddhaṃ tat paryāyoktamucyate ।।
yatra prastutasyaiva kāryasya varṇanāt prastutameva kāraṇaṃ gamyate, tat paryāyoktam । yathā pratibhūpālaśuddhāntadīrghikāsvājidhūsaraḥ । prakṣālayanti gātrāṇi kākatīyacamūcarāḥ ।। atra ripunagarīdīrghikāvārivihāreṇa pratāparudracamūcarakartṛkeṇa kāryabhūtena samaraprārambha eva svapurāṇi vihāya palāyitā pratinṛpāḥ iti kāraṇaṃ pratīyate ।
। atha pratīpam । ākṣepa upamānasya kaimarthakyena kathyate । yadvopameyabhāvaḥ syāt tatpratīpamudāhṛtam ।।
yatropameyasya lokottaratvādupamānākṣepaḥ kriyate, tadekaṃ pratīpam । yatropamānasyopameyatvaṃ kalpyate, tat dvitīyam । ādyaṃ yathā kīrttau pratāparudrasya vilasantyāṃ digantare । kimarthamudayatyeṣa nirlajjaḥ śaśalāñchanaḥ ।। kākatīyakule lakṣmīpatireṣa na saṃśayaḥ ।
anena kathamalpajñaiḥ sumerurupamīyate ।। anumānālaṅkāraḥ । atha tarkanyāyamūlālaṃkārā nirūpyante । sādhyasādhananirdeśe tvanumānamudīryate ।।
rūpakahetukatvena tarkānumānavailakṣaṇyam । yathā sphuliṅgā dṛśyante bhaṭaghaṭitakaukṣeyakabhuvaḥ । prabhūtaḥ kopāgnirdahati ripubhūpālanagarīḥ ।। kāvyaliṅgālaṃkāraḥ ।
atha kāvyaliṅgam । hetorvākyapadārthatve kāvyaliṅgamudāhṛtam ।। yatra heturvākyagatatvena padagatatvena vā pratipādyate tat kāvyaliṅgam । pratāparudra ityeṣā kāpi pañcākṣarī śubhā ।
hṛdi yāṃ bibhrato bhūpā vaśīkurvanti saṃpadaḥ ।। atra vākyārthagato hetuḥ । padārthagato yathā mlānāpi bhūbhṛtāṃ phālalipirucchvasitā punaḥ । pratāparudradevāṅghrinakhajyotsnāmṛtokṣitā ।।
atra pūrvaṃ parimlānāyā bhūpālaphālalipeḥ punarucchvāse pratāparudranarendracaraṇanakhacandrikāsecanaṃ hetuḥ । tasya viśeṣaṇagatatvāt padārthagatatvoktiḥ । arthāntaranyāsālaṅkāraḥ । athārthāntaranyāsaḥ । kāryakāraṇasāmānyaviśeṣāṇāṃ parasparam ।
samarthanaṃ yatra so arthāntaranyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ।। yatra kāryakāraṇabhāvena, sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena vā prakṛtasamarthanaṃ kriyate, so arthāntaranyāsaḥ । kāryakāraṇabhāvena yathā bhūpāḥ ! pratāparudrasya natā bhavata, nonnatāḥ । unnatān namayatyeṣa natānunnamayatyapi ।।
atra phalarūpeṇaunnatyena namratvakāraṇaṃ samarthitam । udvejitā rudranareśvarasya raṇāpadānaiḥ pratipakṣabhūpāḥ । bibhratyamī citramacetanebhyo bhītasya sarvaṃ bhayakāri nūnam ।। atra bhītasya sarvaṃ bhayakārīti sāmānyamacetanebhyo ripubhūpā bibhyatīti viśeṣaṃ samarthayati । viśeṣāt sāmānyasamarthanaṃ yathā
duṣṭo api mahatāṃ saṃgādbhavatyeva hi sajjanaḥ । pratāparudramabhyetya kaliḥ kṛtayugāyate ।। atra pratāparudrasaṃgatimahimnā kaliḥ kṛtayugasadṛśa iti viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasamarthanam । kāryakāraṇabhāve api kāraṇāt kāryasamarthanaṃ kāvyaliṅge antarbhūtamiti tannoktam । ataḥ prakāratrayamarthāntaranyāsasya । yathāsaṃkhyālaṅkāraḥ ।
tarkanyāyamūlālaṃkārānantaraṃ vākyanyāyamūlālaṃkārā nirūpyante । uddiṣṭānāṃ padārthānāṃ pūrvaṃ paścād yathākramam । anūddeśo bhaved yatra tadyathāsaṃkhyamiṣyate ।। yatra yena krameṇoddiṣṭāḥ padārthāstenaiva krameṇānūddiśyante; tatra yathāsaṃkhyālaṃkāraḥ । yathā
gāmbhīryamaunnaṃtyamanargalatvaṃ pratāparudre samavekṣya dhātā । ambhonidhiṣvadriṣu diggajeṣu sṛṣṭiṃ prayāsaikaphalāmamaṃsta ।। arthāpattyalaṅkāraḥ । ekasya vastuno bhāvādyatra vastvanyad āpatet ।
kaimutyanyāyataḥ sā syādarthāpattiralaṃkriyā ।। yatra kasyacidarthasya niṣpattau tatsamānanyāyāt kaimutyenārthāntaramāpatati so arthāpattiralaṃkāraḥ । na cātrānumānaśaṅkā, kaimutyanyāyasaṃbandharūpatvāt । yathā jagatyāṃ krāmannapyajani vidhuraḥ sevaṇapatiḥ । nṛpāṇāmanyeṣāṃ viphalitaruṣāṃ kaiva gaṇanā ।।
trailokyasāro api suvarṇaśailaḥ pratāparudreṇa nṛpeṇa tulyam । tulāṃ samāroḍhumapūrṇa eva mahībhṛtāṃ kā gaṇanetareṣām ।। atra pratāparudrāpekṣayā merāvapyasāre anyeṣāṃ mahībhṛtāmarthādasāratvaṃ kaimutyādāpatati । parisaṃkhyālaṅkāraḥ ।
atha parisaṃkhyā । ekasya vastunaḥ prāptāvanekatraikadā yadi । ekatra niyamaḥ sā hi parisaṃkhyā nigadyate ।। yatraika vastu yugapadanekatra saṃbhāvyamānamekatraiva niyamyate, sā parisaṃkhyā sā prathamaṃ dvividhā, praśnapūrvikā, tadanyathā ceti । tayordvarjayorvarjanīyasya śābdatvārthatvābhyāṃ dvaividhye cāturvidhyam । tatra śābdavarjanīyā praśnapūrvikā yathā
kiṃ maṇḍanaṃ trilokyāḥ kākatitilako na hāṭakakṣitibhṛt । stotavyaḥ kaḥ sudhiyāṃ rudranarendro na mandaraḥ kṣitibhṛt ।। kiṃ vā kṣaumavitānaṃ lokānāṃ ? kākatīyakulakīrttiḥ । kiṃ saukhyaṃ vasumatyā ? rudranarendrasya bhujavāsaḥ ।।
na strīgoṣṭhyāṃ, vyasanamaniśaṃ nītiśāstre na cākṣe । vidyābhyāse na ca parijane rudradevasya rājñaḥ ।। bhūreva bhuvanaṃ devaḥ svayaṃbhūreva pārthivaḥ । pratāparudra evaikaśilaiva nagarī śubhā ।।
kṣoṇīṃ rudranarādhīśe rakṣati kṣatavidviṣi । balisadmanyahibhayaṃ tridive gotrabhitkathā ।। alaṅkārasya śleṣeṇa cārutvātiśayaḥ । uttarālaṅkāraḥ ।
uttarāt praśna unneyo yatra praśnottare tathā । bahudhā ca nibadhyete taduttaramudīryate ।। yatrottarānnibadhyamānāt praśna unnīyate tadekamuttaram । cārutvārthamasakṛllokottaraṃ praśnapratipādanapūrvamuttaraṃ dvitīyamuttaram । krameṇa yathā yadadya jñātavyaṃ prabhavati yadā rudranṛpatiḥ ।
mahīdevāścodyadvividhavibhavārambhamuditāḥ ।। atra pratāparudro yadā prabhavati tadārabhya pūrṇadharmapratiṣṭhā mahī । mahīdevā api tathāvidhasaṃtoṣabhājaḥ । kimadhunā pṛcchasītyuttarāt kiṃ pratāparudrarājye dharmapratipālanamasti kiṃ sukhino bhūsurā ityunnīyate praśnaḥ । dvitīyaṃ yathā kiṃ ṇu dhaṇaṃ ? kulavijjā; ko loho ? sajjaṇeṇa sahavāso । kā ṇaarī ? easilā; ko rāā ? vīraruddaṇaraṇāho ।।
(ki nu dhanaṃ ? kulavidyā; ko lābhaḥ ? sajjanena sahavāsaḥ । ekaśilā; ko rājā ? vīrarudranaranāthaḥ ।।) vikalpālaṅkāraḥ । vākyanyāyamūlālaṅkāraprastāvādvikalpa ucyate ।
virodhe tulyabalayorvikalpālaṃkṛtirmatā ।। yatra tulyapramāṇānuśiṣṭayorviruddhayoryugapatprāptau ekasyāsaṃbhavastatra vikalpaḥ । aupamyagarbhatvāccārutvam । yathā bhūpālāḥ kriyatāṃ mūrdhnāṃ dhanuṣāṃ vā vinamratā ।
pādacchāyāndhranāthasya vindhyādreryā niṣevyatām ।। atra pratāparudre prabhavati rājñāṃ saṃdhivigrahābhyāṃ tulyabalapramāṇābhyāṃ śironamanadhanurnamane yugapadeva prāpte, tayorviruddhatvādyaugapadyāsaṃbhave vikalpaḥ । samuccayālaṅkāraḥ । vikalpapratipakṣabhūtaḥ samuccayo nirūpyate ।
guṇakriyāyaugapadyaṃ samuccaya udāhṛtaḥ ।। yatra guṇānāṃ vaimalyādīnāṃ kriyāṇāṃ ca darśanādīnāṃ yugapadavasthānaṃ tatra samuccayālaṃkāraḥ । yathā pratāparudranṛpatau bhadrāsanamupeyuṣi । satāṃ prasannaṃ hṛdayamasatāṃ kaluṣaṃ manaḥ ।।
pecchai imaṃ ṇarindo pavisai maaṇo a galai māṇo a । ghuṇṇai maṇo a suṇṇaṃ kiṃ edaṃ uvaha sahiāo ।। (prekṣate imāṃ narendraḥ praviśati madanaśca galati mānaśca । ghūrṇate manaśca śūnyaṃ kimetat paśyata sakhyaḥ ।।)
ete bhinnaviṣayatve udāharaṇe । ekaviṣayatve yathā sevārthaṃ cirayatsu kākatipure bhūpeṣu tadyoṣitaḥ । śuṣyanti pralapanti yānti tanutāṃ muhyanti mūrcchanti ca ।। mādyaddanti calatpadāti vicaladvāji pradhāvadratham ।
kampaṃ bhrāmyati sarvataḥ prativanaṃ pratyarthibhūbhṛdgaṇaḥ ।। dvitīyaḥ samuccayaḥ । khalekapotanyāyena bahūnāṃ kāryasādhane । kāraṇānāṃ samudyogaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ samuccayaḥ ।।
sādhayitumahamahamikayā bahūnāṃ kāraṇānāmudyamaḥ, so api samuccaya eva, yugapadanekeṣāmavasthānāt । śubhraṃ yaśaḥ śauryamahacca vṛttaṃ vidyānavadyā vimalaṃ kulaṃ ca । pratāparudrasya nareśvarasya lokottarāṃ rītimudañcayanti ।। atra yaśaḥ prabhṛtīnāṃ lokottararītisaṃpādane pratyekaṃ hetutve api yugapatkhalekapotanyāyena saṃbandhaḥ ।
samādhyalaṅkāraḥ । atha samādhirucyate । ekasmin kāraṇe kāryasādhane anyat parāpatet । kākatālīyanayataḥ sa samādhirudīryate ।।
yatraikasmin kāraṇe kāryasādhanāya pravṛtte kākatālīyatayānyat kāraṇamāgatya tatkāryaṃ sukaraṃ karoti sa samādhyalaṅkāraḥ ।[amādhyalaṅkāraḥ]yathā raṇāṅgaṇe rudranarendraroṣaśamāya rājñāṃ vihitastutīnām । vaktreṣu yadvāyuvaśāt patanti tṛṇāni devasya sa pakṣapātaḥ ।। atra pratāparudranarendrakrodhaśāntyarthaṃ raṇāgre prakrāntastutīnāṃ rājñāṃ vaktreṣu vāyuvaśāt kākatālīyatayā patitaistṛṇaiḥ kopaśāntilakṣaṇakāryasya sukaratvam ।
bhāvikālaṅkāraḥ । atha lokanyāyamūlālaṃkārā nirūpyante । atītānāgate yatra pratyakṣe iva lakṣite । atyadbhutārthakathanādbhāvikaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।।
yatrādbhutacaritopavarṇanād bhūtabhāvinorvastunoḥ pratyakṣāyamāṇatvaṃ bhavati sa bhāvikālaṅkāraḥ । na ca bhūtabhāvinoḥ pratyakṣavadavabhāso viruddhaḥ । atyadbhutavastuvarṇanayā bhāvukānāṃ hṛdi bhāvanodayāt । tathā ca bhāvanāyāḥ punaścetasi nidarśanāt pratyakṣāyamāṇatvaṃ ghaṭata eva । yathā pānthasya kāminībhāvanayā tasyāḥ pratyakṣāyamāṇatvam । na ceyaṃ svabhāvoktiḥ; tasyāṃ vastusvabhāvasya yathāvadvarṇanayā pratyakṣāyamāṇatā । iha tvatyadbhutatvena । nāpi rasavadādyalaṅkāraḥ; tatra vibhāvādyanusaṃdhānenaiva rasāderbhāvyatvam, na tvatyadbhutatvena । na ceyamutprekṣā, atītānāgatayoḥ pratyakṣatvenādhyavasāyābhāvāt, na cāyaṃ bhrāntimadalaṅkāraḥ, bhāvanāyā abhrāntirūpatvāt । ataḥ sarvottīrṇa evāyamalaṅkāraḥ । yathā dhvajāgre kākatīndrasya bhāti kroḍākṛtirhariḥ । mṛdbinduriva daṃṣṭrāgre yasyālakṣyata medinī ।। atrāṣṭādaśadvīpayuktāyā medinyā daṃṣṭrāgre mṛdbindurūpateti atyadbhutavarṇanayā tathāvidhabhāvanāyāṃ pratyakṣavat pratītisaṃbhavaḥ ।
pratyanīkālaṅkāraḥ । atha pratyanīkālaṅkāraḥ pratipādyate । balinaḥ pratipakṣasya pratīkāre suduṣkare । yastadīyatiraskāraḥ pratyanīkaṃ taducyate ।।
yatra prabalasya pratipakṣasya pratīkārāsāmarthyāt tadīyatiraskāro bhavati tat pratyanīkam । yathā kākatīyapatiśauryamahoṣmanyakkṛtasvamahimā baḍabāgniḥ । tadgabhīrimasanābhimajasraṃ bādhate nidhimapāṃ bahirantaḥ ।। atra sādṛśyahetukaṃ tadīyatvamityalaṃkāratvam ।
vyāghātālaṅkāraḥ । atha vyāghātaḥ । yena yat sādhitaṃ vastu tenaiva kriyate anyathā । anyena tadalaṃkāro vyāghātā iti kathyate ।।
yadvastu yena kenacit kartrā yena sādhanena sādhitaṃ, tadvastu tenaiva sādhanenānyena kartrā yadanyathā kriyate sa vyāghātaḥ । yathā kākatīyābhijāto ayaṃ nābhijātādhikasthitiḥ । dorbhyāṃ labdhodayān bhūpāṃstābhyāmanudayān sṛjan ।। paryāyālaṅkāraḥ ।
atha lokanyāyamūlālaṅkāranirūpaṇaprastāvāt paryāyālaṃkāro nirūpyate । krameṇaikamanekasminnādhāre vartate yadi । ekasminnathavānekaṃ paryāyālaṅkṛtirmatā ।। yatra kramādekamādheyamanekasminnādhāre vartate sa ekaḥ paryāyaḥ । na cātra viśeṣālaṃkāraḥ, tatraikasyānekatra yugapadvartanam, atra krameṇa । tathaikasminnādhāre anekamādheyaṃ vartate sa dvitīyaḥ paryāyaḥ । na cātra samuccayālaṃkāraḥ, tatrāpyekatrānekeṣāṃ yugapadvartanam, atra krameṇa । yathā
paścānmastakamaṇḍale phaṇabhṛtaḥ pātālalokeśituḥ । bāhau sarvadhurīṇasāramahite baddhotsavā medīnī ।। atraikasyā medinyāḥ kramādanekatra vartanam । dvitīyaḥ śauryoktayaḥ samabhavannabhimānagarbhāḥ ।
tatraiva dīnavacanāni samudbhavanti ।। sūkṣmālaṅkāraḥ । atha sūkṣmālaṅkāro nirūpyate । asaṃlakṣitasūkṣmārthaprakāśaḥ sūkṣma ucyate ।।
vidagdhamātrajñeyasyārthasya yatrākāreṅgitābhyāṃ prakāśanaṃ sa sūkṣmālaṅkāraḥ । guruaṇasavihammi vahū daṭhṭhūṇa ṇareṃdapesiāṃ dūiṃ । savvaṃgeśu sahāsaṃ katthūrivilevaṇaṃ kuṇai ।। (gurujanasavidhe vadhūrdṛṣṭvā narendrapreṣitāṃ dūtīm ।
sarvāṅgeṣu sahāsaṃ kastūrīvilepanaṃ karoti ।।) udāttālaṃkāraḥ । athodāttālaṃkāraḥ kathyate । tasyāpi lokanyāyamūlataivānantaryakāraṇam । tadudāttaṃ bhaved yatra samṛddhaṃ vastu varṇyate ।।
yatra mahāsamṛddhiśālino vastuno varṇanaṃ kriyate, tatra udāttālaṅkāraḥ । sauvarṇeṣu gṛheṣu ratnaracitadvāstoraṇeṣu sthitāḥ । modante yadavekṣya rudranṛpatestattyāgalīlāyitam ।। atha samānanyāyāt parivṛttirnirūpyate ।
samanyūnādhikānāṃ ca yadā vinimayo bhavet । sākaṃ samādhikanyūnaiḥ parivṛttirasau matā ।। samanyūnādhikānāṃ samādhikanyūnairvinimayaḥ parivṛttiḥ । samena samaparivṛttiḥ, nyūnenādhikaparivṛttiḥ, adhikena nyūnaparivṛttiśceti । samena samaparivṛttiryathā sādhārasamuco vāco dattvā kākatibhūbhuje ।
ato labhante kavayaḥ sahasraṃ gandhasindhurān ।। atra vacasāṃ gandhasindhurāṇāṃ ca samatvam । upāyanaṃ gajāśvādi kṛtvā sarve api bhūbhujaḥ । pratāparudradevasya labhante susthirāṃ kṛpām ।।
atra tyajyamānādupāyanāderādīyamānasya pratāparudrakṛpāvilasitasyaivādhikyam । adhikena nyūnaparivṛttiryathā pratāparudreṇa raṇe jitāḥ pratyarthibhūbhujaḥ । dattvā bhūṣāṃ kirātebhyo labhante valkalādikam ।। tyajyamānādābharaṇajātādādīyamānasya valkalādernyūnatvam ।
kāraṇamālālaṅkāraḥ । atha śṛṅkhalānyāyamūlālaṅkārā nirūpyante । pūrvapūrvaṃ prati yadā hetuḥ syāduttarottaram । tadā kāraṇamālākhyamalaṅkaraṇamucyate ।।
yadā pūrvapūrvaṃ krameṇottarottaraṃ prati hetutāṃ bhajate, sa kāraṇamālākhyo alaṅkāraḥ । yathā vidyayā vinayotkarṣo vinayena guṇārjanam । guṇaiḥ prajānurāgaśca kramo ayaṃ kākatīśvare ।। ekāvalyalaṅkāraḥ ।
yatrottarottareṣāṃ syāt pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ prati kramāt । viśeṣaṇatvakathanamasāvekāvalī matā ।। yatra pūrvapūrvaṃ prati krameṇottarottaraṃ viśeṣaṇatvaṃ bhajate, sa ekāvalyalaṅkāraḥ । pratāparudranagarī sujanairupaśobhitā ।
sujanāḥ sphītavibhavairvibhavāḥ sthairyaśālinaḥ ।। etat sthāpanenodāharaṇam । apohanenāpi bhavati; yathā na tadrājyaṃ prajā yatra na bhavantyūrjitaśriyaḥ । na tāḥ prajāḥ prabhuryāsāṃ na svayaṃ kākatīśvaraḥ ।।
mālādīpakālaṅkāraḥ । yadā tu pūrvapūrvasya saṃbhaveduttarottaram । pratyutkarṣāvahatvaṃ tanmālādīpakamucyate ।। yatra pūrvapūrvasyottarottaraguṇāvahatvaṃ sa mālādīpakālaṅkāraḥ ।
bhāgyabhūmā mahīṃ prāptaḥ kākatīndrabhujaṃ mahī । bhujaḥ pratāpamatulaṃ pratāpaśca jagattrayam ।। sārālaṅkāraḥ । uttarottaramutkarṣaḥ sārālaṅkāra ucyate ।।
jagatsu vasudhā bhāti tasyāmekaśilāpurī । kākatīyānvayastatra tasmin rudranareśvaraḥ ।। sakalabhuvanasārabhūtaṃ pratāparudraṃ viṣayīkurvataścirādasyālaṅkārasya sāra ityanvarthābhidhānam ।। śāstre arthālaṅkāraprakaraṇaṃ samāptam ।
।। atha miśrālaṅkāraprakaraṇam ।। atha saṃsṛṣṭisaṃkarau nirūpyete । yathā laukikānāmalaṅkārāṇāṃ hiraṇmayānāṃ maṇimayānāṃ ca pṛthak saundaryahetūnāmanyonyasaṃbandhena cārutvātiśayo dṛśyate; tathaiva kāvyālaṅkārāṇāṃ rūpakādīnāṃ mithaḥ saṃbandhena saundaryātiśayaḥ pratīyate । sa ca saṃbandho dvividhaḥsaṃyogarūpaḥ, samavāyarūpaśceti । saṃyoge tilataṇḍulanyāyaḥ । samavāye kṣīranīranyāyaḥ । tilataṇḍulanyāyena saṃbandhe saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । kṣīranīranyāyena saṃbandhe saṃkaraḥ । anayoḥ pṛthak cārutvātiśayahetutvādalaṅkāradhurandharatvam; na tu pūrvoktālaṅkāraśeṣatā । saṃsṛṣṭiḥ ।
tatra prathamaṃ saṃsṛṣṭirnigadyate । tilataṇḍulasaṃśleṣanyāyād yatra parasparam । saṃśliṣyeyuralaṅkārāḥ sā saṃsṛṣṭirnigadyate ।। yatra tilataṇḍulanyāyena parasparasaṃbaddhā rūpakādayo bhavanti sā saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । sā trividhāśabdālaṅkāragatatvena, arthālaṅkāragatatvena, ubhayālaṅkāragatatvena ca ।
stvaṅgattuṅgaturaṅgamapratibhayā drāksyandanasyandanāḥ । niḥ sīmāḥ prasaranti rudranṛpaterjaitraprayāṇodyamāḥ ।। atra cchekānuprāsavṛttyanuprāsayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । kākatīndracamūrdhatte mahimānamudanvataḥ ।
grasate yā dviṣadbhūpadhvajinīstaṭinīriva ।। atra nidarśanopamāyoḥ saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । pratāparudradordaṇḍo maṇḍalāgreṇa maṇḍitaḥ । dṛśyate samare vīrairutphaṇaḥ phaṇavāniva ।।
atra vṛttyanuprāsopamāyoḥ saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । aṅkaraḥ । atha saṅkaro nirūpyate । kṣīranīranayād yatra saṃbandhaḥ syāt parasparam ।
alaṅkṛtīnāmetāsāṃ saṅkaraḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ ।। yatra kṣīranīranyāyenālaṅkārāṇāṃ mithaḥ saṃbandho bhavati sa saṅkaraḥ । tasyāṅgāṅgibhāvena ekavācakānupraveśena saṃdehena ca traividhyam । tatrāṅgāṅgibhāvasaṅkaro yathā kṣoṇībhṛtkaṭakoparodhapaṭubhiḥ prāvṛḍvihārā iva । yātrāḥ kākativallabhasya jagatāmānandamātanvate ।।
atra yātrāḥ prāvṛḍvihārā ivetyupamālaṅkāreṇa dvipaghaṭākādambinītyatropamā prasādhyata iti sajātīyayoraṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ; kādambinīva dvipaghaṭeti samāsāśrayaṇāt । kṣoṇībhṛtkaṭakoparodhetyatra śleṣamūlātiśayoktiḥ । vijātīyasaṅkaro yathā pratāparudrasya kṛpāṇadhārā pratyarthiphāleṣu patatyamandam । prakṣālanāyeva kṛtasya dhātrā tadvartino durlipikalmaṣasya ।।
atra prakṣālanāyevetyutprekṣayā durlipikalmaṣasyetyatra rūpakaṃ prasādhyata iti vijātīyayoraṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ । vijitāripuro mūrtau vilasatsarvamaṅgalaḥ । bhuvi śaṃbhurivābhāti kākatīyanareśvaraḥ ।। atra vijitāripura ityarthasāmyādupamā, vilasatsarvamaṅgala iti śabdasāmyāt śleṣaśca śambhurivetyekasminnivaśabde anupraviṣṭau ।
jātaḥ pratāparudrenduḥ kākatīyānvayāmbudhau । dhatte janacakorāṇāṃ prasādajyotsnayāmṛtam ।। atra kākatīyakulāmbudhau ityādau rūpakopamāyoḥ saṃdehasaṅkaraḥ । kākatīyānvaya evāmbudhiḥ, kākatīyānvayo ambudhiriveti samāsadvayasaṃbhavāt । na cātra sādhakaṃ bādhakaṃ vā pramāṇamanyatarasyāstīti saṃdeha eva paryavasyati । sādhakabādhakapramāṇasaṃbhave tu saṃdehanivṛttiḥ । atra sādhakaṃ yathā pratāparudranṛpateḥ pārijātāt samudbhavāḥ ।
vataṃsayanti diṅnāryo madhurāḥ kīrttimañjarīḥ ।। atra kīrttaya eva mañjarya iti rūpakālaṅkāre vataṃsayantīti sādhakaṃ pramāṇam। vataṃsīkaraṇenābhedapratītiḥ । bādhakaṃ yathā kākatīndrasya niḥ sāṇadhvanau dikṣu vijṛmbhite । vyākulakṛtasattvo abhūt pratipakṣabalārṇavaḥ ।।
atra pratipakṣabalārṇava ityupamāyā vyākulīkṛtasattva iti bādhakaṃ pramāṇam; "upamitaṃ vyāghrādibhiḥ sāmānyāprayoge'; ityanuśāsanena sāmānyaprayogasyopamābādhakatvāt । ataḥ pāriśeṣyādrūpakālaṅkāraḥ । evaṃ yathāsaṃbhavamanyeṣāmalaṅkārāṇāṃ saṃsṛṣṭisaṅkarau boddhavyau tatra tatra prabandheṣu ।। śāstre miśrālaṅkāraprakaraṇaṃ samāptam । pritāparudrīyaṃ nāmālaṅkāraśāstraṃ samāptam ।।
